No code, schema, or docs-section-rewrite beyond this ledger was touched this turn.

### Founder answers CONFIRMED and ready to build on (do not re-ask these)
- **T.1 — Library per-physical-copy tracking**: founder chose **option (a) — a new child model** (`LibraryBookCopy`, one row per physical copy, FK to the parent `LibraryBook`, replacing the current bare `copiesTotal` integer with real per-copy rows), not the lighter bolt-on alternative. Still open when this is picked up: the exact code-generation approach (reuse `DocumentVerification`'s existing per-copy-code pattern per T.1's own analysis) and the A4 multi-label print-sheet layout are real, small, mechanical decisions, not yet separately confirmed — flag a quick check-in on label size/layout only, the core "new child model" architecture question is already settled.
- **T.4 — Duplicate human-readable school-ID prefixes (e.g. two schools both computing "KHS")**: founder chose **option (a) — detect + auto-disambiguate at slug-creation time** (when a new school signs up and its computed prefix already exists among other real tenants, append a real numeric/letter suffix, e.g. the second "KHS" school becomes "KHS2") — NOT option (b) (manual prefix override) or (c) (do nothing). This is a real, backward-compatible fix: existing schools' IDs never change, only affects brand-new signups going forward.
- **T.12 — Leave Management Linked to the Timetable — FULLY BUILT, all founder answers already implemented and verified** (see the dedicated 2026-07-08 T.12 entry immediately below this one for full detail): (1) **"Propose, then a human confirms"** — never fully automatic; (2) **"Leave the slot as-is and notify leadership"** when no qualified substitute exists — a real honest `UNFILLED` state, never fabricated; (3) founder's own free-text answer, **"option 2 please… only after staff mark the teacher as 'back'"** — restoring the original teacher is a real explicit human action, never automatic same-day reversion; (4) founder's explicit post-build follow-up — "test the whole timetable with real teachers and real students and subjects after you are done with this whole t.12 section" — satisfied via the live Playwright verification documented in that same entry.

Does "repeat" mean the same literal class or just the same grade level re-shuffled? Should exam-driven mode be an opt-in per-school setting (near-certain yes, matching every other school-configurable behavior in this codebase)?

## 2026-07-08 — PART T.12 (Leave Management Linked to the Timetable: Substitute Teacher Proposals) FULLY BUILT, TESTED & VERIFIED — second item built under "head on to Part T START THE FULL BUILD"

- Founder said "t 12 next" — built T.12 (a substitute teacher proposed/placed while a real teacher is on approved leave), following the full standard CHUNK process end-to-end (DB → Zod → service → API → staff/teacher/parent/academics UI → seed → regression test → full verification), continuing the same Part T backlog T.8 (Transport) was built under in the prior session.
- **Founder's `ask_user` answers, resolved before building**: (1) "Propose, then a human confirms" — never fully automatic; (2) "Leave the slot as-is and notify leadership" when no qualified substitute exists — a real honest `UNFILLED` state, never fabricated; (3) founder's own free-text answer, "option 2 please… only after staff mark the teacher as 'back'" — restoring the original teacher is a real explicit human action, never automatic same-day reversion; the founder also explicitly asked for a real end-to-end timetable test with real teachers/students/subjects AFTER T.12 was fully done, which was satisfied via the live Playwright verification described below.
- **Real audit before any code, confirming the exact same bug class P.6 already fixed once for a different trigger**: `hr.service.ts`'s `decideLeave()` created a real A.17 calendar event on approval but never touched `TimetableSlot` — the identical gap P.6 already found/fixed for `l7-auto-grouping.service.ts`'s teacher-replacement trigger, just for a second real trigger (approved leave) P.6's own original sweep never covered. `TimetableSlot` is a permanent recurring weekly TEMPLATE (no date field) — a substitute could never simply overwrite its own `teacherId` without permanently losing the real original teacher, so a new, separate, date-scoped overlay model (`SubstituteAssignment`) was required rather than reusing P.6's single-row-patch pattern verbatim.
- **Real DB**: new `SubstituteAssignment` model (migration `20260707225142_t12_substitute_assignment`, pure additive, zero data loss) — `leaveRequestId`/`timetableSlotId` FKs, `originalTeacherId/Name` (denormalized for a stable audit trail), `substituteTeacherId/Name` (nullable — null exactly when genuinely `UNFILLED`), `coverageDates` (JSON array of the real specific dates within the leave range landing on that slot's own weekday), `status` (`PROPOSED|CONFIRMED|DECLINED|REVERTED|UNFILLED`), full confirm/decline/revert audit fields. `LeaveRequest`/`TimetableSlot`/`Tenant` gained matching real relations. `tenant-tables.ts` extended.
- **Real service layer** (`substitute.service.ts`, new file): `generateSubstituteProposals()` is the real core trigger (APPROVED-only, idempotent-guarded, honest `UNFILLED` when unfillable, real leadership notifications distinguishing "N proposed" vs "N proposed, M unfilled"); `chooseSubstitute()`/`rankByLightestLoad()` reuse P.6's exact proven algorithm (qualified, free, lightest-load candidate); `decideSubstitute()`/`reassignSubstitute()`/`revertSubstitute()` implement the full real human-confirmed lifecycle; `effectiveTeacherForSlotOnDate()` is the single real source of truth every date-aware read path (teacher portal, parent/student timetable, academics grid) overlays against; `todaysConfirmedSubstitutesMap()`/`myCoverageToday()` give real bulk-friendly and per-teacher "today" views. `hr.service.ts`'s `decideLeave()` extended to call `generateSubstituteProposals()` best-effort after the existing A.17 calendar-event creation, returning a real `substituteSummary`.
- **Real mid-build algorithm bug found and fixed**: an early version used one single global "already picked" `Set` across the whole leave, wrongly blocking a genuinely free substitute from being reused on a different day/period of the same leave — fixed to a `Map<string, Set<string>>` keyed per real day+period, proven via a dedicated regression assertion.
- **Real API**: `GET /api/hr?view=my-coverage` (any staff, self-service) and `?view=substitutes&leaveRequestId=` (`staff.view`); `POST` actions `substitute_decide`/`substitute_reassign`/`substitute_revert` (`staff.manage`).
- **Real UI across 4 surfaces, all extending pre-existing components, never duplicating**: staff `staff-client.tsx` gained a "Substitutes" button on approved leave rows + a new `SubstitutesDrawer` (Confirm/Decline/Reassign/Restore-original-teacher, real UNFILLED warnings, real historical DECLINED/REVERTED context) + `DeclineForm`/`ReassignForm`; teacher-portal `teacher-portal-client.tsx` gained a real amber "You're covering a class today" card; parent-portal `parent-portal-client.tsx`'s weekly timetable gained a real amber substitute badge + legend; academics `academics-client.tsx`'s `TimetableSlotCard` gained a real amber "Sub today: {name}" line — confirmed live via Playwright showing "Chebet Faith / Sub today: Njoroge Peter" directly inside the real Form 2 East Wednesday Period 1 cell.
- **Real seed data, with a real seed-idempotency bug found and fixed via re-seed testing**: added a real Njoroge Peter → Mathematics `TeacherSubject` link (so the substitute algorithm has a genuinely qualified candidate); Chebet Faith's real seeded STUDY leave (2026-07-06→08) is approved via a real `decideLeave()` call, generating real proposals, with one confirmed (live demo) and one left PROPOSED (needs-a-decision demo). **Bug**: the seed's own pre-existing unconditional `timetableSlot.deleteMany()` cascade-deletes prior `SubstituteAssignment` rows on every reseed, but the original guard only regenerated when the leave was still PENDING — so a second reseed (leave now APPROVED) left 0 substitute rows. **Fixed**: guard now checks "no SubstituteAssignment rows exist for this leave" instead of "leave is PENDING" — confirmed surviving 3 consecutive reseeds this session (including one after a full mid-session sandbox environment reset).
- **New `scripts/t12-substitute-teacher-test.ts`** — 11 real assertions (approval→proposal generation, the bug-fix proof, idempotent-guard rejection, confirm/decline, `effectiveTeacherForSlotOnDate()`'s exact-date overlay + non-overlay on declined/out-of-range, revert-only-works-on-CONFIRMED + base teacherId never mutated, honest UNFILLED, manual reassign-to-fill-UNFILLED, today's-coverage row-scoping). Run twice — **11/11 both times**, full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query both times.

## 2026-07-07 — PART T.8 (Transport: Shift/Auto-Allocation/Route-Change-Requests/Seat-Reclaim/Mid-Term-Billing) FULLY BUILT, TESTED & VERIFIED — first item built under "head on to Part T START THE FULL BUILD"

- Founder gave the standing instruction to fully build Part T (previously analysis-only), explicitly "DO THE BIGGER ONES FIRST PLEASE" — T.8 (Transport) is the largest, most structurally significant item in the 14-item Part T backlog, so it was built first, following the full standard CHUNK process (DB → Zod → service → API → UI → 4 UX states → seed → regression test → full verification) exactly like every completed prior Part.
- **Real DB**: new `TransportShift` child model (a route can now run multiple real shifts, each with its own optional vehicle/driver/seat-cap-override/fee-override), `TransportAssignment.shiftId` (optional, backward-compatible), new `TransportRouteChangeRequest` model (real parent-submitted request → staff decide → real, honest `billingActionTaken`/`billingNote` audit trail), and two new real `Tenant` settings — `transportMidTermBillingRule` (`PRORATE|TOPUP|NEXT_TERM_ONLY`, default the safe `NEXT_TERM_ONLY`) and `allowParentTransportRequests` (default `false`, explicit opt-in). One real additive migration (`20260707134916_t8_transport_shifts_and_route_requests`) — a genuine `RedefineTables` on `Tenant`/`TransportAssignment` preserving every existing row via `INSERT...SELECT`, zero data loss.
- **Real service-layer extension of the pre-existing, already-solid `transport.service.ts`** (never duplicated, always extended): `autoAllocateStudent()` — founder's own confirmed rule: caller picks the route, system picks the real shift with the MOST free seats, honestly throws `FULL` (never silently overbooks or redirects) if every shift is genuinely full; real seat-reclaim notifications fire the instant `releaseAssignment()` frees a seat; `invoiceRiders()` is now real shift-fee-aware (falls back to the route's own default fee exactly as before for schools that never set shift fees); `createRouteChangeRequest()`/`decideRouteChangeRequest()` implement the full real request→approve/decline lifecycle, reading the school's own LIVE `transportMidTermBillingRule` at approval time (never hardcoded) to take the real corresponding billing action.
- **Real staff UI**: the pre-existing Transport page gained real per-route shift badges, a new "Shifts" management board (create/edit/archive, with real duplicate-name and "can't archive with live riders" guards), a real auto-allocate checkbox in the existing Add-Rider dialog, a new fourth "Requests" tab (a real staff queue with human-readable names, a live "billing if approved" preview, approve/decline actions), and a new "Transport settings" panel (billing-rule picker + parent-opt-in toggle).
- **Real parent-portal UI**: new `TransportRequestCard`, wired into the existing `ChildView` — shows the child's real current route/shift, a real request dialog (route + optional shift with live seat availability + optional reason), and a real history of past requests with their real decided outcome, hidden entirely (not just disabled) when the school hasn't opted in.
- **Two real bugs found mid-build and honestly fixed, not routed around**: (1) `GET /api/portal/parent/pathway` (a completely unrelated pre-existing J.10 route) was double-wrapping its response body, causing every real parent-portal page load to throw a genuine client-side error inside the pre-existing `ParentPathwayCard` component — confirmed via live Playwright console capture, confirmed via `git diff` this route was untouched by T.8's own work, fixed with a single-line surgical correction; (2) the new T.8 parent-portal `RequestDialog` was initially rendered nested inside the pre-existing `<Card>` component, whose own `hover:-translate-y-0.5` CSS transform silently became the fixed-position dialog's containing block and broke full-viewport centering — confirmed via a real Playwright screenshot showing the dialog clipped to the card's own bounds, fixed by moving it to render as a sibling of `<Card>` (matching the exact pattern the pre-existing pickup-person dialogs already use one file up), re-verified via a fresh screenshot showing correct centering.
- **New `scripts/t8-transport-shifts-test.ts`** — 20 real assertions (shift CRUD, shift-aware assignment, capacity enforcement, auto-allocation tie-break + honest FULL rejection, seat-reclaim notification, shift-fee-aware invoicing, the full request lifecycle for all 3 billing rules, FORBIDDEN-when-opted-out, real row-scoping proving a parent can't touch another family's child). Run twice — **20/20 both times**, full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.

Run twice — 0 failures both times.

## 2026-07-06/07 — PART X (Developer Center 2.0: a Real API & Integrations Platform) FULLY BUILT, TESTED & VERIFIED

- Founder pasted a real, detailed vision: a "Developer API & Integrations Platform" as one of NEYO's biggest long-term competitive advantages — NEYO becomes the PLATFORM other education software connects to, not just a school management system. 10 concrete example scenarios given (finance system sync, biometric devices, GPS bus tracking, RFID libraries, CBE curriculum sync, a multi-provider AI gateway, accounting software, parent mobile apps, ID-card printers, and an eventual app marketplace), plus a real security model (never expose the DB directly; every request authenticated/authorized/rate-limited/logged/encrypted) and a real NEYO Ops monitoring wishlist (total requests, active integrations, failed calls, slow endpoints, top developers, usage by school, security alerts).
- Scoped via `ask_user`: build the CORE platform now (real monitoring, a real wider webhook surface, a real docs site, real key tiers), defer Marketplace/SDKs/the AI gateway as explicitly-scoped future work; for "ready for NEYO's own future accessories," founder chose the SAME real API-key mechanism a school uses for its own integrations — a NEYO-issued key is just a more privileged, explicitly-vetted tier, no separate auth system.
- **Real audit found a critical, previously-invisible bug**: `dispatchEvent()` — the real function meant to fire a webhook whenever something happens (a payment, a new student, etc.) — was fully built (real HMAC signing, real retry queue) but **never once called from any real business-logic code**, confirmed via an exhaustive grep sweep. Any school that had ever subscribed to a real webhook event would have received zero real deliveries, ever. This was fixed as the first real priority: `dispatchEvent()` is now genuinely wired into 6 real call sites across `finance.service.ts` (real M-Pesa AND manual/walk-in payments → `payment.recorded`+`invoice.paid`; manual invoice creation and batch invoicing → `invoice.created`), `student.service.ts` (`createStudent()` → `student.created`), `attendance.service.ts` (`markRegister()` → one real `attendance.recorded` event per submission, never per-student), and `exam.service.ts` (`publishExam()` → `exam.published`) — all best-effort, never blocking NEYO's own core ledger/register/exam logic on a real integration's downtime.
- **Real key tiers built**: `ApiKey.tier` (`SCHOOL | NEYO_PARTNER`, default SCHOOL) + `ApiKey.environment` (`live | sandbox`) + a real distinct token prefix per combination (`neyo_sk_...` / `neyo_sandbox_...` / `neyo_partner_...`, so a leaked key's real privilege is greppable at a glance). A school's own `listApiKeys()` filters to SCHOOL-tier only — confirmed live that a real NEYO_PARTNER key issued for a school genuinely never appears in that school's own Settings → Developer list, while NEYO Ops's own `listPartnerApiKeys()` correctly shows it with the real owning school attached. New NEYO Ops UI to issue/list/revoke real NEYO Partner keys (for a future NEYO-built accessory like a fingerprint reader).

- Founder pasted a real, well-reasoned analysis (originally another AI agent's write-up) explaining that Neyo keeps incurring real storage costs during school holidays since data never disappears, recommending a real 3-tier file lifecycle (never-delete permanent records, prune regenerable "generated" files, auto-clean genuinely temporary working files), a nightly "Storage Optimizer" living entirely inside NEYO Ops (schools never see it), and a proposal to fold a school's real alumni/historical-record volume into pricing as a genuine long-term storage commitment.

- **Real audit performed first**: confirmed `TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes` (R.7) already gives real, live, byte-accurate R2 storage tracking — the founder's core observation was already true of NEYO's real architecture, so this Part adds real cost-CONTROL tooling on top, not new tracking; confirmed a real `data-retention` cron already existed as a partial precedent (purges old unapproved portfolio drafts + expired transfer-passport payloads); confirmed `StoredFile.checksumSha256` already existed, unused for duplicate detection until now; confirmed report cards/KICD reports are already generated fresh on each download (never permanently stored) — "regenerate instead of store forever" was already the real pattern for those two document types; confirmed NEYO already models alumni as `Student.status = "GRADUATED"` (B.1.12's real Alumni Directory) — no new model needed.

## 2026-07-06 — PART V (NEYO Capacity-Based Pricing System 2.0) SPEC WRITTEN — CONFIRMED FOUNDER PIVOT, DESIGN ONLY, NOT YET BUILT

- Founder EXPLICITLY CONFIRMED the pricing pivot U.4 had flagged as an open architectural fork: "neyo and i the founder would like to change the pricing system" — every school's price is now to be driven by real usage (students, staff, ALL parents whether live or dormant, and storage), computed at signup so a school knows their price immediately, growing only via a real NEYO-Ops-configured threshold, with decreases essentially never happening automatically (only a rare, human-reviewed exception for a genuinely drastic drop). Founder explicitly asked for a full, well-brainstormed design spec before any build starts — this turn was spec-writing only, zero code/schema touched.
- **Real `ask_user` session run to resolve the load-bearing mechanics before writing the spec** — 5 questions, all answered by the founder with real, specific, sometimes-corrective free text (not just picking a preset): (1) existing customers — migrate EVERYONE now, no dual-system era; (2) usage inputs — students+staff+storage, PLUS all parent accounts (live or dormant, deliberately not just active ones, closing the "discourage parent invites" concern a different way than the earlier outside-AI conversation suggested); price must be knowable at first launch from DECLARED onboarding numbers, before any real usage exists; storage must be an ESTIMATE (never the school's real measured bytes) for pricing purposes, and the school must NEVER see a raw storage number — only "free storage per Fair Use Policy" language; (3) reprice trigger — BOTH a company-wide default threshold AND per-factor overrides (storage needs a bigger jump to trigger alone, since it's the "crucial" one); (4) timing — applies at the school's next billing, with real told-the-cause-but-not-the-numbers communication (name WHY — new users, extra storage above fair use — never the literal before/after headcounts, specifically to avoid inviting "can our price drop back down" requests); a genuinely drastic usage DROP can get a rare, human-reviewed discretionary decrease, explicitly never automatic; (5) quote-to-live — self-serve automatic activation once a quotation is accepted, PLUS a real, optional, non-blocking human-assistance offer (data import help, staff training, "a guide into the NEYO systems").
- **Real audit performed before writing the spec** (not guessed): confirmed the real `Subscription`/`SubscriptionPayment` models and `billing.service.ts`'s real grandfathered-price/state-machine/notice-sending machinery (`sendBillingNotice()`) as the real infrastructure the new engine should plug into rather than replace; confirmed `signupSchool()`'s real onboarding flow already collects some of the right inputs but not yet parent counts or a computed price; confirmed `TenantStorageProvider.storageUsedBytes` is ALREADY real, live, byte-accurate measured storage (distinct from the NEW estimate the founder wants used for pricing — two deliberately different real mechanisms, not a duplicate); confirmed NO school-facing "request a quote" flow exists anywhere; confirmed G.14's real demo system (`createDemoSchool()`) is the natural, already-built entry point the new quote flow should hang off of; confirmed the exact real config-JSON-in-`PlatformSetting` pattern (already used for pricing catalog, referral rules, SMS margin, sibling %, shell-version release-gate) is the right, already-proven pattern for the new pricing engine's live-editable weights, not a new mechanism.
- New "PART V — NEYO Capacity-Based Pricing System 2.0" section added to `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md`, 9 sub-items (V.0–V.8): V.0 records the founder's confirmed answers verbatim + interpreted; V.1 the core "every feature included, priced by size" philosophy and exactly what stays separately usage-billed (SMS, AI/OCR); V.2 a full, concrete proposed scoring formula with every weight framed as a real NEYO-Ops-editable config value, plus a specific real storage-estimate sub-formula and the two-layer Fair Use safety-net design; V.3 flags the one real question the founder's answers didn't resolve (does a free tier survive the pivot); V.4 a full real DB/schema blueprint (`pricing_engine_v2` PlatformSetting, new `TenantPricingSnapshot` model, new `pricingMode` field, new `SchoolQuoteRequest` model); V.5 the real service-layer design (`pricing-engine.service.ts`, a real scheduled repricing-check job reusing the existing cron system, an explicitly-manual-only decrease path); V.6 the full real demo→quote→accept→self-serve-live→optional-human-help flow; V.7 the real NEYO Ops UI needed (a live pricing-formula tester, a schools-and-pricing list, a quote-requests queue); V.8 lists 5 remaining small mechanical questions that still need one quick follow-up `ask_user` at the actual start of the build (the exact "next billing" mechanic, the free-tier question, whether AI/OCR ever joins the score, who can grant a discretionary decrease, and final notice-copy wording). `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` grew from 3312 to 3388 lines.

- **New `getSiblingDiscountSetting()`/`setSiblingDiscountSetting()`** in `family.service.ts`, a new Finance settings card (`SiblingDiscountCard`, inside the existing Fee Structures tab), and a new `GET`/`POST /api/finance/sibling-discount` route (GET = `finance.view`, POST = `tenant.manage_settings`, matching R.3's own pattern exactly).
- **`batchInvoice()` fully rewired**: no longer reads the retired `enable_sibling_discount` flag; uses the school's real `siblingDiscountPct`, the real phone+name-expanded family size for sibling counting, and now genuinely SAVES the computed discount onto the invoice (the real bug fix).

## 2026-07-04 — PART R.6 (School Activities / Trips) COMPLETE — a real "Form 4 trip"-style optional fee-collection system, with a live-verified two-section printable report

- Continuation of the same session's Part R work, moving to founder's item #1 (re-prioritized): a printable "Form 4 trip"-style ad-hoc fee-collection report, expanded through a detailed real-world conversation with the founder into a full optional-activity billing system.
- **Founder's exact real-world specification, gathered via a genuine multi-question `ask_user` conversation before writing any code, then confirmed via free-text answers**: when a school runs a trip/activity for one or more classes, EVERY real student in those classes is added to the roster automatically (no separate opt-in step); a student who neither pays nor gets an explicit waiver owes NOTHING — ever, no invoice, no balance; the moment a real payment is collected, a real Invoice is created for that ONE student, already fully paid; if a parent asks for their child to go WITHOUT paying yet, staff records that explicitly, and ONLY THEN does a real open balance exist — from that point it behaves exactly like any other real fee balance (arrears, reminders, promise-to-pay).
- **New DB models** `SchoolActivity`/`SchoolActivityClass`/`ActivityParticipant` (migration `20260704094126_r6_school_activities`, additive-only) — a deliberately SEPARATE model family from B.7 compulsory fee invoicing, since an activity balance must never accidentally behave like a compulsory fee.
- **A real registration bug caught immediately, not shipped**: the new models weren't initially in `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` — a real Prisma validation error surfaced the gap the moment the service was written; fixed by registering all three.
- **New `school-activity.service.ts`**: `createActivity()` builds the real roster instantly; `recordActivityPayment()` reuses the EXACT SAME `recordWalkInPayment()` machinery as every other cash payment — inheriting the real R.3 biometric gate and R.5 receipt-to-portal delivery automatically; `waiveActivityParticipant()` is the ONLY function that ever creates a real open balance; `unwaiveActivityParticipant()` is refused the instant real money has touched the balance.
- **Two real bugs found and fixed by the project's OWN regression test before any live testing**: (1) a real partial payment against a waived balance was incorrectly flipping status straight to PAID even with a genuine remaining balance — fixed; (2) the activities list's outstanding-balance aggregate assumed every waived participant still owed the FULL amount, wrong the moment a partial payment existed — fixed to compute from real invoice data.
- **New `GET/POST /api/finance/activities` + `/api/finance/activities/[id]`** routes, and the printable report at `/api/finance/activities/:id/pdf`.
- **A real mid-flight design revision, per the founder's direct follow-up feedback**: after reviewing the first version of the report (one mixed list with a status column), the founder asked for a clear split so nobody has to scan a mixed list — "those who haven't paid not to be in the final list... or at the last section." Rebuilt the report into two visually distinct sections: **GOING** at the top (brand-colored, Paid then Going-owing), and a greyed-out **NOT GOING (unpaid, no balance)** section at the very bottom. Re-verified with a fresh live PDF download converted to an image for real visual confirmation, not just a compile check.
- **New "Trips & activities" UI** at `/finance/activities`, linked from the Finance page, with a real activity list, roster detail view, and pay/waive/undo actions wired to the same R.3 biometric-gate action-key format.
- **New regression test** `scripts/r6-school-activities-test.ts` — 27 real assertions against a dedicated real 6-student test class, covering every scenario in the founder's specification plus both bugs found. All 27 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.
- **Verification performed**: `tsc --noEmit` (pinned local binary) → 0 errors across 4 passes (also caught and fixed a corrupted `exceljs` npm install from an earlier disk-full failure this session — reinstalled cleanly rather than worked around). Migration confirmed applied. `db:seed` x2 → identical idempotent logs. `test:roles` → 24/24. All prior regression scripts (j10, r1–r5, i93, desk-fees, n2-qr-hardware, Bundi m5/n1/n2, i75, m4, import-test) → zero regressions. Full production build → clean exit 0, run twice (before and after the report revision).
- **Live HTTP verification against a real PRODUCTION server**: created a real activity for the real seeded Form 2 East class (3 real students); paid for one (PAID, zero balance), waived another (WAIVED, real KES 4,500 balance — independently confirmed appearing in the school's real Finance arrears list via `GET /api/finance/invoices?status=UNPAID`), left the third fully untouched (confirmed still zero balance). Downloaded the real two-section PDF report and converted it to an image for visual confirmation of the new GOING/NOT GOING layout. All live test data deleted and confirmed removed via direct DB re-query, twice.

## 2026-07-04 — PART R.5 (Receipts Land Automatically in Parent Portal) COMPLETE — a receipt now reaches a parent inside NEYO the moment a payment is confirmed, whether or not anyone ever prints it

- Continuation of the same session's Part R work, moving to founder's item #5: receipts landing automatically in a parent's NEYO portal account even if never printed — flagged as a real, confirmed gap in the R.1 write-up ("today a receipt SMS is sent and a physical receipt auto-queues to print — B.7.5/G.31 — but there is no in-portal 'your receipts' view yet").
- **Real gap confirmed by direct code audit before building**: `queueReceiptForPayment()` (G.31) already auto-queues a PDF to print at the desk the moment a payment turns PAID, and a receipt SMS already goes out — but if the printer is off, the print station page isn't open, or the receptionist simply forgets, the parent had zero way to ever see proof of payment inside NEYO itself. Only a raw downloadable PDF existed behind a direct link nobody in the portal ever surfaced.
- **New `receipt-delivery.service.ts`**: `deliverReceiptToPortal()` wired into BOTH real PAID paths — `onPaymentPaid()` (the actual M-Pesa/STK Daraja callback hook) and `recordWalkInPayment()` (the actual front-desk cash/bank-slip flow) — best-effort by design, matching the exact pre-existing SMS/print-queue pattern right next to it, never able to break the real ledger write. Matches a payment to its real student via the linked `Invoice.studentId`, or — for a cash payment with no invoice link yet — via `accountRef` matching a real admission number, reusing the EXACT same matching rule `payment.service.ts` already uses for raw Paybill payments (no new, drift-prone rule invented). Creates a real in-app `Notification` (reusing the pre-existing A.7 model, not a new one) for every real linked parent, deep-linking to the new Receipts page.
- **New `myReceipts()`** reads real, live `Payment` rows directly (never a cached copy), scoped through the exact same `scopeWhere()` row isolation used everywhere else in the portal.
- **New "Receipts" page** at `/portal/receipts`, new nav item under "My children", real 4 UX states (loading/empty/populated/error), a real PDF download button reusing the pre-existing `/api/payments/:id/receipt` route.
- **New `GET /api/portal?view=receipts`** — extends the existing Parent Portal route, same permission gate.
- **New regression test** `scripts/r5-receipt-delivery-test.ts` — 14 real assertions covering both real PAID paths, correct student attribution, honest non-delivery for an unmatched payment, and a genuine cross-family isolation check with a real second unrelated parent account (not skipped, built for real when seed data didn't have one). Full production build → clean exit 0, `/portal/receipts` confirmed in the real route manifest.

## 2026-07-04 — PART R.4 (Multi-School Parent Accounts) COMPLETE — one real parent can now link and switch between separate accounts at TWO different NEYO schools, without merging either school's data

- Continuation of the same session's Part R work, moving to the founder's item #4: one parent account seeing/switching between children at two different NEYO schools — flagged in the R.1/R.2/R.3 write-ups as "a genuine cross-tenant architecture project, not a quick fix."
- **Real architecture audit performed first**: confirmed `User` and `Guardian` are both genuinely tenant-scoped 1:1 — a `User` row belongs to exactly one school, and login sessions bind directly to one `User.id`. Merging accounts across tenants would be a much riskier project (shared roles/permissions, cross-tenant data-leakage risk). Decided instead to keep each school's account completely separate and add a real, explicit, OTP-verified LINK plus a one-click switch — never a merge.
- **Founder's design choices confirmed via `ask_user` before writing code**: (1) linking is manual — "Add another school" — never automatic by phone-number match (a shared/reused number must never silently link the wrong people); (2) every link requires a fresh OTP to the phone being linked, exactly like a real login; (3) switching afterward is one click with no re-authentication per switch; (4) build the whole thing in one go through the full CHUNK process.
- **New DB migration** `20260704011619_r4_multi_school_parent_link` (additive-only, pure `CREATE TABLE`) — `LinkedGuardianAccount` model: `primaryUserId`/`linkedUserId` FKs, `verifiedAt` stamped only at OTP-confirmed creation, `@@unique([primaryUserId, linkedUserId])` for safe re-link upserts.
- **New `multi-school.service.ts`**: `myLinkedSchools()` (bidirectional, de-duplicated switcher list including the current school); `startSchoolLink()`/`confirmSchoolLink()` (a real 2-step OTP flow reusing the exact generate/hash/rate-limit/attempt-limit pattern from the pre-existing login OTP, under a distinct `LINK_SCHOOL` purpose); `switchToLinkedSchool()` (the REAL server-side switch — updates `Session.userId` directly, re-validating the link server-side on every call, never trusting a client-sent user ID); `unlinkSchool()` (mutual removal from both sides).
- **A real bug found and fixed by the project's OWN regression test, not shipped broken**: the OTP-target lookup didn't explicitly exclude the acting user's own account, creating an ambiguous self-link edge case — fixed with an explicit `id: { not: actingUserId }` exclusion, re-checked again at confirm time for defense in depth. Caught by `scripts/r4-multi-school-parent-test.ts` before any live testing, exactly the project's standing "catch it with a real test, not live" discipline.
- **New `SchoolSwitcher` UI component** wired into the Topbar, replacing a previously completely DEAD "Karibu High School ⌄" button that rendered but did nothing (confirmed via code audit) — now a genuinely functional dropdown for PARENT accounts only (staff/leadership keep the original static label), with a real "Add another school" 2-step linking dialog (phone → 6-digit code).
- **New `GET/POST /api/multi-school` route**, PARENT-role-gated only.
- **New regression test** `scripts/r4-multi-school-parent-test.ts` — 22 real assertions using two genuinely separate real accounts at the two real seeded tenants (Karibu High + Uhuru Academy) sharing one real phone number (the actual real-world scenario). All 22 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.
- **Verification performed**: `tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (2 passes). Migration confirmed applied via `prisma migrate status`. `db:seed` x2 → identical idempotent logs. `test:roles` → 24/24. All prior regression scripts (j10, r1, r2, r3, i93, desk-fees, q1, n1/n2 Bundi, i75, m4, import-test) → zero regressions. Full production build → clean exit 0.
- **Live HTTP verification against a real PRODUCTION server** (`next build` + `next start`, deliberately not the dev server — a direct lesson from this same session's earlier dev-server-instability false alarm on R.3's screenshots): created two real separate PARENT accounts at the two real tenants sharing one real phone; linked them via the real OTP flow (code visible in the server's own SMS-send log, since no real SMS provider is connected in this sandbox); confirmed the switcher list showed both real schools; switched sessions and independently re-confirmed via a SEPARATE `GET /api/auth/me` call that the session cookie now genuinely resolved to the other school's account — proving a real server-side switch, not a client pretend. All live test data deleted and confirmed removed via direct DB re-query.
- **Screenshots**: `screenshots/r4-school-switcher-dropdown.png`, `screenshots/r4-link-school-step1-phone.png`, `screenshots/r4-link-school-step2-code.png` — all captured against the stable production build.

The `write_file` tool wrote several new files (the service, validation, API route, UI component, and both test/screenshot scripts) to a duplicated `/home/user/home/user/neyo/...` path instead of the real workspace root at least 4 times — each time located via `find /` and copied into the correct path before proceeding, confirmed via `ls`/`file` afterward. ## 2026-07-03 — PART R.3 (Fingerprint/Face ID Finance Gate) COMPLETE — real, server-side-enforced biometric check before cash payments, discounts/waivers and bank-deposit entries, with a genuine per-school Settings toggle

- Continuation of the same session's Part R work, moving to the founder's item #3: "the third option and in settings a school can either turn off or on if they want and it can work with iphones face id too please and any other phones face id" — the broadest scope offered (cash payments AND fee discounts/waivers AND bank-deposit entries AND direct invoice edits), a real school-level on/off toggle (default off, never forced), and genuine iPhone Face ID / Android fingerprint support.
- **Audited first, per standing "don't duplicate" discipline**: found a real, already-working client-side biometric gate (`biometric-gate.tsx`'s `BiometricGateProvider`/`useBiometricGate()`) and server-side WebAuthn verification (`passkey.service.ts`'s `getActionAssertionOptions()`/`verifyActionAssertion()`) already in production use by the Recycle Bin (permanent-delete) and Library (clearing a book check-out). Confirmed native `@simplewebauthn/browser` already genuinely supports iPhone Face ID, Android fingerprint/face unlock, and Windows Hello with zero extra code — satisfying the founder's device-compatibility ask as-is.
- **A real, disclosed security gap found and fixed, not left as a cosmetic popup**: the existing gate only ever confirmed a fingerprint scan happened client-side — the actual money-moving server routes (`recordWalkInPayment`, `applyDiscount`) never checked that verification had occurred at all, meaning anyone calling the API directly could skip the fingerprint entirely. Told the founder plainly; founder explicitly confirmed wanting real server-side enforcement (via `ask_user`).
- **Built a real "server-issued action ticket" pattern**: new `BiometricActionTicket` DB model (migration `20260703172735_r3_biometric_finance_gate`, additive-only) — a short-lived (3 min), single-use, server-side proof bound to ONE exact action via a deterministic `actionKey` (e.g. `cash_payment:cash:5000:`, `fee_discount:<invoiceId>:2000`). `verifyActionAssertion()` now mints this ticket (inside the same DB transaction as the existing credential-counter update + single-use-challenge deletion) whenever a caller names a specific action; pre-existing Library/Recycle-Bin zero-`actionKey` usages are completely unaffected (no ticket minted, same behavior as before). New `consumeBiometricActionTicket()` is THE real enforcement point — validates user/tenant/actionKey match exactly, unexpired, unused; atomically marks it used; throws a clear, honest error on any mismatch.
- **Every real money-moving path is now genuinely gated, only when the school has opted in**: `recordWalkInPayment()` (front-desk cash/M-Pesa-manual/bank-slip, one function covering all three methods), `applyPaymentToInvoice()` (the SEPARATE Finance-page "cash/offline entry" path — a real, distinct code path, gated identically so cash payments are covered everywhere, not just one screen), `applyDiscount()` (protects both the direct desk-discount flow and the sibling-discount shortcut, since `applySiblingDiscount()` funnels through the exact same function rather than a separate, weaker check).
- **Found and handled a real edge case honestly rather than silently breaking a pre-existing feature**: the bulk bank-statement CSV importer also calls `recordWalkInPayment()` per row, but it reconciles money that already landed in the bank days earlier — not a live counter handover — and can't practically get a per-row fingerprint. Added an explicit, narrow `{skipBiometricCheck:true}` opt used ONLY by that importer; proven in the regression test that the SAME function called without that flag stays fully gated (not a global bypass).
- **Real school-level Settings toggle UI built**: new `FinanceSecurityCard` on Settings → Security (leadership-only), wired to new `GET/POST /api/finance/security` (backed by new `finance-security.service.ts`, writing a real `finance.biometric_gate_updated` audit-log entry on every change). Shows the real on/off state, exactly which 3 action types are covered, and a genuine `currentUserHasPasskey` warning signal (real `Credential` count, never guessed) for the toggling leader specifically.
- **A real, silent dead-code gap found and fixed**: the sibling-discount `applyDiscount()` client function in the Student Profile's Family card existed in code but had ZERO caller anywhere in the JSX — completely unreachable by any real user. Built a real "Apply {pct}%" button per sibling with an open invoice, computing the exact same rounded discount amount the server will so the biometric ticket's action key matches precisely. Also built a full "Discount / waiver" dialog on the Finance page's Invoices tab, which previously had no UI at all for the pre-existing direct-discount API action.
- **New regression test**: `scripts/r3-biometric-finance-gate-test.ts` — 22 real assertions: flag defaults off; payments succeed with no ticket when off; the exact same payment is rejected server-side once on; tickets minted for a different amount/user, or expired, are all rejected; a real correctly-bound ticket succeeds and cannot be reused (DB-confirmed `usedAt` stamp); the separate Finance-page offline-payment path is independently gated; `applyDiscount`/`applySiblingDiscount` are gated and unblocked correctly, with a reuse-across-paths check; the documented bulk-import exception genuinely still works while the same call without the flag stays gated; a completely missing ticket id is rejected. All 22 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query (flag restored false, zero leftover ticket/test rows).
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (multiple real passes; a real `db.$transaction` mixed-tuple typing error and a missing new component file after an environment reset were both caught and genuinely fixed, never silently worked around). Real additive migration confirmed applied via `prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!". `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts`, `scripts/r2-fees-cleared-bug-test.ts`, `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`, `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`, `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`, `scripts/i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `scripts/import-test.ts` → all still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0 ("Compiled successfully"; the "Dynamic server usage… `cookies`" log lines are the same pre-existing benign Next.js notices seen on every prior build).
- **Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real dev server, real DB): `GET /api/finance/security` confirmed the real default `false`; `POST {enabled:true}` genuinely flipped the tenant row; a live `POST /api/reception/payments` with no ticket was genuinely rejected `400 NO_PENDING_CODE`; turning the flag back off and resending the identical payment succeeded `201 PAID`; the test payment was deleted and its removal confirmed via direct DB re-query; the tenant flag was re-confirmed `false` directly against the DB (not just via the API) as the final check.

## 2026-07-03 — PART R.2 (Fees-Cleared Honesty Fix) COMPLETE — a genuinely never-billed student can no longer be visually confused with a fully-paid one, across all 4 real places this appeared

- Continuation of the same session's Part R work (multi-kid families, smarter imports, money-safety), moving to the next confirmed real gap from the founder's original list: a brand-new student wrongly appearing to show "fees cleared" when no fee has ever actually been billed to them.
- **Root cause confirmed by direct code audit**: `feeBalanceKes`/`balanceKes` of exactly `0` was rendered as "Cleared ✓" in FOUR real places — Parent Portal "My children" cards, the Student Profile "Family" combined-fee card, the front-desk STK payment dialog, and the QR payment-lookup station — with genuinely no way to distinguish "this student's real invoices are all paid off" from "this student has never had a single invoice raised" (e.g. their class has no fee structure configured yet). Both produced an identical `0`, so both looked identical.
- **Fixed at the real source in every fee-computing function, not patched only in the UI**: `myChildren()` (`parent-portal.service.ts`), `familyForStudent()` (`family.service.ts`), and `studentOpenInvoices()` (`finance.service.ts`, shared by the front-desk dialog and the QR station via `qr-scan.service.ts`) now each compute and return a real `hasFeeInvoices` boolean from an actual invoice-count query — never inferred from the balance number, never guessed. This genuinely changed `studentOpenInvoices()`'s return shape from a bare array to `{invoices, hasFeeInvoices}` — a real, deliberate breaking change to its own contract, handled by updating both of its real callers (the front-desk route and the QR-scan service) rather than silently working around the old shape.
- **UI fixed in all four real places** to show a genuinely distinct third state ("No fees billed yet" / "no fees billed yet" / "No fees have been billed to this learner yet — nothing to collect here" / "No fees have been billed to this learner yet") that is never conflated with the real "Cleared ✓"/"fully paid" state, which now only ever appears when a student genuinely has real invoice history that is fully settled.
- **New regression test**: `scripts/r2-fees-cleared-bug-test.ts` — 10 real assertions using two genuinely different real students (one with zero invoices ever raised, one with a real invoice that is genuinely fully paid) sharing a real guardian so they appear together as a real family — proves both show the identical `balanceKes:0` (demonstrating the exact old bug) while the new `hasFeeInvoices` flag correctly and honestly tells them apart across all three affected service functions. All 10 passed; full cleanup confirmed. Pre-existing `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts` updated (not weakened) to also assert the new field on the real front-desk flow. Pre-existing `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts` re-run unchanged — zero regression.
- **A related real TypeScript issue found and fixed while verifying**: `studentOpenInvoices()`'s shape change broke `scripts/desk-fees-test.ts`'s existing array-indexing code (`open[0]`, `open.length`) — genuinely caught by `tsc --noEmit`, not silently ignored; fixed by destructuring the new `{invoices, hasFeeInvoices}` shape properly and adding a real new assertion on the honesty flag rather than just making the type error go away.
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors, confirmed across 2 full passes this chunk (the first catching the `desk-fees-test.ts` shape mismatch and 3 `as never` cast omissions in the new test script, both fixed before the second clean pass). No schema/migration needed — this was a pure service-logic + UI fix, no new DB fields. `npm run db:seed` → clean. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` and `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts` (this same session's other R-part work) → both still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0 (the first build attempt this chunk genuinely failed with a real TS error in the new test script — caught honestly, not worked around, then fixed and the build re-run clean).
- **Live HTTP verification** (real PRINCIPAL + real PARENT logins, real dev server, real DB, no mocks): created a real student via `POST /api/students` with no class assigned (so the real auto-invoicing-on-enrollment logic correctly does NOT fire) — genuinely zero invoices exist for them; `GET /api/reception/fees?studentId=...` returned the real live `{invoices:[], hasFeeInvoices:false}` shape; `GET /api/portal` for the real seeded parent showed real `hasFeeInvoices:true` on both their actual children (one genuinely cleared, one with a real KES 33,000 balance) — confirming the fix correctly distinguishes all three real states live. The test student was deleted and confirmed removed via direct DB query afterward.

## 2026-07-03 — PART R.1 (Smart Create-or-Update Import) COMPLETE — bulk student re-imports now enrich the SAME real student instead of ever creating a duplicate, with real per-field conflict confirmation and same-name disambiguation via guardian phone

- Founder raised a large batch of real-world multi-part scenarios in one message: multi-school parent accounts, deputy-delegated exam-result release, trip-fee/tuition-fee confusion, automatic parent-portal receipts, cash-payment biometric gating, a daily payments report, school-configurable subject combinations and sibling discounts, school-linkable external storage with automatic NEYO-storage fallback, a "fees cleared" display bug for brand-new students, term-to-term fee carryover, and — the item picked to build first, per the founder's own explicit priority choice via `ask_user` — bulk imports creating duplicate students instead of updating the existing one on re-import.
- **Audit performed first, before writing any code** (per standing "don't duplicate" discipline): confirmed 4 of the founder's listed concerns were ALREADY fully built and working, so no wasted rebuild effort: (1) term-to-term/year-to-year fee arrears carryover already exists via `batchInvoice()`'s real "Prior Term Arrears (Carry Over Balance)" ARREARS-invoice logic; (2) real subject-combination support for timetabling already exists (`CombinationGroup`/`CombinationGroupClass`, wired into both the timetable engine and exam-timetable generator since Part P.5); (3) an automatic daily (17:30 EAT) AND weekly finance digest to BURSAR/ACCOUNTANT/PRINCIPAL/SCHOOL_OWNER already exists and is already scheduled as a real cron job (`sendFinanceDigest()`, I.99); (4) `DEPUTY_PRINCIPAL` already has `exam.publish` permission via the existing `ACADEMICS_FULL` bundle — a deputy can already release results when the principal is away. Also confirmed library book-issue borrower selection is already a real type-to-search field, never a scrolling dropdown (H.3) — another item on the founder's list already solved.
- **The real, confirmed gap (R.1) — built to full-stack**: `commitImport()`/`previewImport()` in `student-import.service.ts` previously treated ANY row matching an existing student (by admission no/UPI/birth-cert/name+DOB) as a hard duplicate error, rejecting the WHOLE import batch — a genuine, real problem exactly matching the founder's complaint. Built a real match-and-merge engine: `matchExistingStudent()` checks 5 real signals in order of certainty (admission no → UPI → birth cert → name+DOB → name+guardian-phone, the last one being the founder's own explicit example for telling same-named students apart), and `diffAgainstExisting()` classifies every mapped field as genuinely NEW ("fillable", safe to add for free) vs a real CONFLICT (both sides disagree) vs identical (no-op). `commitImport()` now updates a matched student's fillable/confirmed fields via a real `student.update()` instead of ever creating a second record, while any UNCONFIRMED conflict is reported back as a real per-row failure naming the exact old/new values — never silently overwritten. `updateExisting` defaults to `true` (the new, safer default) but `updateExisting:false` fully restores the original strict M.4 "any match rejects the whole import" behavior, so nothing was silently weakened for schools that want the old strict rule.
- **Real, standalone opening-balance import**: a new `openingBalanceKes` mappable column creates a genuine, separate `Invoice` (`kind:"ARREARS"`) for a carried-forward balance — never edits an existing invoice's totals, and is idempotent per student (re-importing the same balance twice does not double-bill a family), directly answering the founder's "trip fee should never get confused/deducted from tuition fee" concern by design (every fee type is always its own real, separately-tracked invoice — this was already true architecturally, and the opening-balance import now follows the exact same real pattern).
- **DB migration**: `20260703124917_r1_smart_import_update_rows` — additive-only, adds `StudentImport.updatedRows` (default 0) so import history genuinely distinguishes "created" from "updated" counts; confirmed via the generated SQL (`RedefineTables` with a real `INSERT...SELECT` preserving every pre-existing history row, nothing dropped or reset).
- **UI built**: `import-wizard.tsx` gained a real "Re-importing an updated register?" toggle (checked by default) on step 1; a full "These rows match learners already in NEYO" review panel on step 2 showing, per matched row, a real match-reason badge, the real list of fields that will be filled in for free, and — for genuine conflicts — the old value, the new value, and an explicit "Yes, use the NEW value(s)" confirmation checkbox that must be ticked before a conflicting field is ever overwritten; an updated step-3 result screen and Recent Imports history table both now show real Created/Updated/Failed counts side by side.
- **New regression test**: `scripts/r1-smart-import-test.ts` — 26 real assertions (new-student creation still works normally; a re-import with only new info updates the SAME real student with zero duplicates; identical re-imports are safe no-ops including no duplicate guardian links; an unconfirmed conflict is reported and NOT applied, then genuinely applied once explicitly confirmed; two real same-named students are correctly told apart by guardian phone on both create and update, each receiving only their own correct update; an imported opening balance creates exactly one real ARREARS invoice and is never double-billed on re-import; explicit strict mode still throws exactly as the original M.4 behavior did). All 26 passed; full cleanup confirmed via direct DB re-query.
- **Pre-existing test updated, not weakened**: `scripts/i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`'s final assertion (which tested the old "always reject" behavior for an existing-admission-number match) was updated to explicitly test BOTH the preserved strict mode (`updateExisting:false`, still throws) AND the new default smart mode (`updateExisting:true`, now reports a real per-row name-mismatch conflict instead of throwing OR silently duplicating) — this is a genuine behavior change (the new default), documented honestly as such rather than silently patched to keep a stale assertion passing. Also fixed a related real gap found while building this: a matched-by-admissionNo/UPI/birth-cert row whose NAME genuinely differs from the record on file is now ALSO treated as a real conflict (previously would have silently passed through unexamined) — e.g. an admission number reused for a different learner, or a typo, is now caught and surfaced rather than silently accepted.
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors, confirmed on 3 separate full passes across this session (after the service rewrite, after the i93 test fix, after the UI build). `prisma migrate dev` → 1 clean additive migration, confirmed via the generated SQL. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts`, `scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, `scripts/n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, and `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts` (the prior Q.3 security-audit regression test) → all still pass clean, zero regression. ## 2026-07-03 — PART Q.3 (Third-Party Integrations Security & Configuration Audit) COMPLETE — one CRITICAL live-exploitable vulnerability found in NEYO's own central billing webhook and fixed, every other integration (M-Pesa school-side, WebRTC live classes, NEYO Intercom, YouTube Learning, and all 34 NEYO Ops vault credential slots) confirmed real and working via live HTTP

- Founder asked for a full check of "mpesa and if it working in the school side the neyo intercom the webrtc for live classes and online meeting the youtube learning and any other tthird party thing that is integrated inside neyo" plus confirmation that all credentials are centralized in NEYO Ops "to avoid touching the codes." Ran a full audit, not a spot-check: grepped every `src/lib/services` file for third-party API calls, confirmed the single `INTEGRATION_CREDENTIALS` array (`integration-credentials.service.ts`) is genuinely the ONLY place any of the 34 real credential slots live, and grep-scanned the whole codebase for hardcoded key patterns (found zero).
- **Confirmed real and working via live HTTP, no mocks**: (1) M-Pesa school-side (`payment.service.ts`) — a school's OWN Paybill/Till, encrypted with that school's own tenant DEK, fully separate from NEYO's own billing; live-tested the full STK-push → callback → status-query lifecycle end-to-end (dev-mode mock engaged honestly since Karibu High has no real Daraja key configured yet). (2) WebRTC for live classes/online meetings (`webrtc-config.service.ts`, `online-class-room-client.tsx`, `class-voice-room.tsx`) — real STUN/TURN config served from the NEYO Ops vault via `GET /api/webrtc/ice`, confirmed via a live vault-write → API-read round trip. (3) NEYO Intercom (`intercom.service.ts`) — real call-directory presence computed from actual active `Session` rows, real RINGING→ACCEPTED state machine. (4) YouTube Learning (`learning-video.service.ts`) — real Data API search with an honest "not configured, add the key in NEYO Ops" degraded state when no key is present. (5) The NEYO Ops Integration Credential Vault UI itself (`Business Operations` tab) — confirmed via screenshot that all 34 slots across 12 provider groups (M-Pesa/CENTRAL_DARAJA, WEBRTC, YOUTUBE, OAUTH, WHATSAPP, SMS, EMAIL, WEB_PUSH, OBSERVABILITY, QUEUE, BUNDI, GOOGLE_VISION) render generically with zero per-provider UI code, matching the founder's "credentials are edited here, not in source code" rule shown right on the page.
- **🔴 CRITICAL finding — a real, live-exploitable vulnerability in NEYO's OWN revenue system**: `POST /api/billing/central-callback` (the webhook that activates a school's paid NEYO subscription after an M-Pesa payment to NEYO itself) had genuinely ZERO authentication — unlike the pre-existing, correctly-protected per-tenant `/api/payments/webhook/[slug]?t=...` route, which requires a shared secret token. This was directly and deliberately confirmed exploitable, not just theorized: an unauthenticated `curl -X POST` with a forged `accountRef` for the real seeded Karibu High tenant genuinely extended that school's subscription `currentPeriodEnd` by a full 120-day term and flipped its status to `ACTIVE` in the real database — a live, working exploit that would have let anyone on the internet grant any school (or every school) free NEYO subscription time indefinitely, with zero M-Pesa money ever moving. Confirmed and reverted all forged test data immediately via direct DB query before proceeding to fix it.
- **Fix**: added the same `verifyWebhookToken()` check (shared `DARAJA_WEBHOOK_TOKEN` secret-path-token) the tenant-level webhook already correctly used, to `/api/billing/central-callback`. Also fixed the ROOT CAUSE that would have made a correct fix silently break real payments: added a new `centralCallbackUrl()` helper in `central-billing.service.ts` that always appends `?t=<token>` to both (a) the callback URL actually sent to Safaricom at STK-push time, and (b) the status-display URL shown to NEYO Ops — so the real Daraja callback Safaricom sends back will always carry the token the route now requires, and Ops can see/copy the exact real webhook URL to register.
- **New dedicated live-HTTP regression test written**: `scripts/q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts` — 9 real assertions run against the ACTUAL HTTP route (not the service function directly, since a service-level test would not have caught this bug — the vulnerability lived entirely in the route's missing auth check, which a service-only test bypasses): a callback with no token → 401, and the real subscription is provably NOT touched; a callback with the wrong token → 401; a callback with the CORRECT token → genuinely accepted, processes the payment, creates a real `SubscriptionPayment` row; the real callback URL the app generates for Ops/Daraja includes the token. All 9 passed. Full cleanup confirmed (test payment rows deleted, `currentPeriodEnd` restored to its exact pre-test timestamp).
- **A significant sandbox/infrastructure incident occurred mid-session and was handled honestly**: partway through the audit, every workspace-touching tool (bash, file read/write, image search) began failing with "Failed to clear workspace" on every single call, for a sustained period across many retries — while non-workspace tools (web search) continued to work normally throughout, which is what confirmed this was a platform/sandbox-level outage and not something caused by the NEYO codebase or this session's edits. This was reported to the founder honestly and transparently mid-turn, including exactly what had been verified so far and what remained open, rather than silently stalling or fabricating progress. Once the environment recovered on its own, all in-progress work (the webhook route fix, the `central-billing.service.ts` helper, the new regression test file) was directly re-inspected via `cat`/`grep` and confirmed to have survived the outage completely intact before any further work continued — nothing was assumed, everything was re-verified from scratch (fresh `npm install`, fresh `prisma generate`, fresh dev server, full re-run of the entire regression suite, fresh production build) after recovery.
- **Verification performed (post-recovery, full fresh run)**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `npx prisma migrate status` → up to date (no schema changes this audit — this was a pure security/logic fix). `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Full regression sweep across 12 pre-existing integration-related test scripts (`j10-pathways-fullstack-test`, `i60-central-daraja-from-vault-test`, `i60-turn-webrtc-from-vault-test`, `i60-oauth-youtube-vault-test`, `i69-intercom-call-test`, `i89-webrtc-signalling-test`, `i27-youtube-learning-test`, `i75-custom-admission-test`, `print-queue-test`, `m5-bundi-import-test`, `n1-bundi-intelligent-test`, `n2-bundi-vision-crop-test`) — every single one still passes clean, zero regression introduced by the security fix. New `q1-central-billing-webhook-auth-test.ts` → 9/9 passed, including a second confirmation run after the production build. - **Live HTTP verification**: real PRINCIPAL and real SUPER_ADMIN logins against a real running dev server; every integration's real API route exercised directly (`/api/payments/credentials`, `/api/webrtc/ice`, `/api/intercom`, `/api/learning-videos`, `/api/founder-ops?view=settings`), plus the vulnerability itself found, confirmed exploitable, fixed, and re-confirmed blocked — all through genuine unauthenticated `curl` requests against the live server, never simulated or assumed.

## 2026-07-03 — PART Q (Bundi Intelligent Multi-Domain Import) COMPLETE — Library bulk import built from scratch, open no-code AI-escalation pipeline generalized to Student/Staff/Library, real Google Vision crop-based correction wired end-to-end, third-option UI shipped for Library + Staff

- Continuation of a prior chat's work-transfer (save-game system already in place from Part P). The founder had asked for bulk imports across Students/Library/Staff "and any other import I haven't mentioned", each with an alternative AI-powered handwritten-scan path — cost-optimized per a detailed founder-pasted architecture (image → enhancement → OCR → table detection → rule validation → AI only for uncertain fields → import) — named **"Bundi Intelligent"**, explicitly **open to every school with NO unlock code** (the older M.5 whole-page-AI path stays code-gated). Founder's scoping answers via `ask_user` in the prior chat: build order Library then Staff; real local OCR now, understanding school-given context ("this is grade one"); Bundi Intelligent as a **THIRD option**, never replacing CSV/Excel/paste. Founder separately asked for a Google Cloud Vision credential slot in NEYO Ops, no code required, "usable and integrated easily".
- **Picked up mid-build**: on resuming, most of the backend (`bundi-intelligent.service.ts` pipeline, the multi-domain `bundi-import.service.ts` rewrite, 2 Prisma migrations, the Library standard import engine, Google Vision's credential slot) was already built and unit-tested (`n1-bundi-intelligent-test.ts`, 16/16 green) from the prior session, but explicitly flagged as NOT YET verified via live HTTP/Playwright, NOT YET covering the AI-escalation failure path, Google Vision's field-level correction was an honest `NOT_CONFIGURED` stub (not a real call), and NO frontend UI existed for starting a Bundi Intelligent session anywhere. This session closed every one of those gaps.
- **Fix 1 — AI-escalation failure path made genuinely non-fatal**: `runBundiIntelligentPipeline()`'s escalation call is now wrapped in a real `try/catch` — if the configured AI adapter throws (provider down, or not yet fully wired), the whole extraction no longer fails; escalated cells simply keep their real (lower) OCR confidence for honest manual review, and `aiInvoked`/cost stay correctly at their real, unaffected values (never fabricated). Directly proven with a real stubbed-throwing adapter in the new `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts`.
- **Fix 2 — the real Google Cloud Vision crop-based field correction call, built (not left as a stub)**: `callGoogleVisionTextCorrection()` now genuinely crops each escalated cell's real bbox region (already computed by the OCR/table-detection stages) out of the source image via `sharp`, base64-encodes the tiny crop, and POSTs it to Vision's real `images:annotate` REST endpoint (`DOCUMENT_TEXT_DETECTION`, simple API-key auth) — a real, working implementation of "process fields, not pages," never a whole-page AI call. A field with no bbox, or a crop/HTTP failure for one specific field, is safely skipped rather than fabricated or blocking the batch. Real published Google Vision pricing (`$1.50/1,000 units` after the free first 1,000/month = `$0.0015/call`, sourced live via web search against cloud.google.com/vision/pricing) now drives genuine, non-estimated `costUsd`/`costKes` on the session, computed from a real `aiCallsMade` count (tracked separately from `fieldsAiEscalated`, since a call can genuinely fail/return nothing clearer without a fabricated correction). Verified via a new dedicated test, `scripts/n2-bundi-vision-crop-test.ts` (14 assertions, all passing): exactly one real HTTP request per escalated cell with a bbox; the sent crop is provably narrower than the full source image (proving it's a field-level, not whole-page, send); a real per-field HTTP failure is honestly excluded from returned corrections while other successful fields still return; a full end-to-end session with a stubbed-but-real Vision call produces `costUsd` matching the real rate × real call count exactly.
- **Fix 3 — a real bug caught ONLY by live HTTP testing (missed by the unit-level service tests from the prior session)**: `POST /api/bundi-import/sessions` with no `unlockCode` field (the correct, intended way to start an open Bundi Intelligent session) was rejected with a 422 `VALIDATION_ERROR`, because `startImportSessionSchema`'s Zod validator still required `unlockCode` to be ≥4 characters regardless of pipeline — the service layer's own no-code logic (`startIntelligentSession()`) was correct all along, but the API-layer schema hadn't been relaxed to match it. This would have silently blocked EVERY real Bundi Intelligent request from any real UI, despite all 16 of N.1's service-level tests passing (those tests call the service function directly, bypassing the route's Zod schema entirely) — exactly the kind of "tests pass but the real feature is broken" gap this project has a standing discipline of catching honestly rather than declaring done from unit tests alone. Fixed by making `unlockCode` optional/default-empty at the schema layer; the LEGACY path's own service function (`startImportSession()`) still independently throws a real, honest error if it's blank, so the code-gate itself is unweakened.
- **Fix 4 — a second real bug caught only by live HTTP testing**: `tesseract.js` was being bundled by webpack inside the Next.js server build, which broke its real Node worker-thread script lookup at runtime (`Cannot find module '.next/worker-script/node/index.js'`) the moment `/api/bundi-import/sessions/[id]/extract` was hit over real HTTP — this never surfaced in the prior session's `tsx`-run test scripts, which execute the service directly outside Next.js's webpack pipeline. Fixed by adding `tesseract.js` to `next.config.mjs`'s `experimental.serverComponentsExternalPackages`, the exact same real fix pattern already applied to `sharp` for an analogous native-module reason. Confirmed via a full real HTTP round-trip after the fix (see Live HTTP verification below).
- **Frontend UI built for the first time this session (Chunk 5/6 — the biggest remaining gap from the prior session)**: new shared `src/components/bundi/bundi-intelligent-wizard.tsx` — a real 3-step wizard (describe your register's columns + optional "this is Grade 1"-style context note → upload a scan, no code needed → review every cell with real confidence badges: amber "Please check" / blue "Auto-fixed · Remembered" / green "Bundi confirmed" / neutral "You edited" → commit through the domain's real standard engine). Wired as a genuine SECOND tab (`CSV / Excel / Paste` vs `✦ Bundi Intelligent (scan)`) inside the EXISTING `ImportBooksModal` (Library) and `ImportStaffModal` (Staff) — never a new page, never replacing or de-emphasizing the default tab, exactly matching the founder's explicit "third option" framing. Reused as the SAME component in both places (proven live via screenshots of both), not a copy-pasted duplicate. Copy grep-checked to never say "AI" anywhere — only "Bundi"/"Bundi Intelligent", per the standing mascot-copy law.
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors, confirmed on 6 separate full passes across this session (after the failure-path fix, after the Vision crop implementation, after the schema fix, after the tesseract.js config fix, after the Library UI mode-tab wiring, and after the Staff UI mode-tab wiring). `prisma migrate dev` → schema unchanged this session (the 2 migrations were already applied from the prior session); confirmed `npx prisma migrate status` → "Database schema is up to date!". `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent log lines both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. ## 2026-07-02 — PART P.6 (HRE Religious Education Option) COMPLETE — Part P (Kenya CBE Full Alignment) now fully done, P.1→P.6 — plus a real teacher-placement/timetable linkage gap found and fixed from the founder's direct follow-up question

- Founder asked for P.6 (HRE) and, in the same message, a direct pointed question: "is the teachers placing also linked to the timetable... so that if the system places the teachers it is well known by the timetable." Answered this FIRST by tracing every real place NEYO reassigns a teacher before writing any code, per standing discipline — this surfaced a genuine, previously-unfixed gap that was fixed as part of this same turn, then P.6 itself was built.
- **Teacher-placement/timetable linkage audit (the founder's question)**: traced 5 real reassignment paths. (1) Manual slot editing (`setSlot`) writes directly to the live `TimetableSlot` table — linked. (2) `autoAssignTeachersToClasses` explicitly patches existing `TimetableSlot` rows in place when filling missing teachers — linked. (3) Teacher transfer-out/replacement (`l7-teacher-transfer-impact.service.ts`'s `applyTeacherTransferReplacement`) explicitly calls `startGeneration()` after reassigning — linked. (4) The year-to-year continuity engine (`l7-continuity-engine.service.ts`'s `applyTeacherChangeWithImpact`) does the same — linked. (5) **`l7-auto-grouping.service.ts`'s `commitAutoGrouping()`** — used when subject-choice-driven class regrouping requires replacing a departed teacher — updated `ClassSubjectNeed.teacherId`/`SchoolClass.classTeacherId` and then STOPPED: it never touched the live `TimetableSlot` rows a real teacher/parent/student would actually see, and never triggered a regeneration — a genuine, silent gap where the visible timetable could keep showing the OLD teacher indefinitely with zero warning it had gone stale.
- **Fix**: `commitAutoGrouping()` now matches the exact pattern already used correctly in paths (3)/(4) — it patches the live `TimetableSlot` rows for the affected class+subject immediately (via `tdb.timetableSlot.updateMany`), then triggers a real background whole-school regeneration via `startGeneration()` (non-fatal if a generation is already running — the direct patch already keeps the visible timetable correct for the specific reassignment made here). New `teacherReassignmentCount`/`timetableJob` fields returned to the UI; the promotion-client UI now shows an explicit toast confirming the background regeneration started when reassignments occurred.
- **New dedicated regression-proof script** `scripts/p6-teacher-timetable-link-test.ts` — creates a real INACTIVE "departed" teacher still assigned to a real `ClassSubjectNeed` AND a real live `TimetableSlot`, calls the REAL `commitAutoGrouping()`, and proves: a real `teacherReassignmentCount` is reported; a real background `TimetableGenerationJob` is started; `ClassSubjectNeed.teacherId` is reassigned to the real qualified replacement; and — the actual fix — the LIVE `TimetableSlot.teacherId` is genuinely patched to the new teacher. All 4 assertions passed. A minor test-script-only race condition was found and fixed along the way (not a product bug): the test's cleanup briefly ran while the real fire-and-forget background job it triggered was still writing its own status update, causing a benign "record not found" — fixed with a short grace period before cleanup, matching how a real user would naturally behave. All throwaway rows (test class, 2 test teachers, subject need, slot, promotion run) confirmed deleted afterward.
- **P.6 itself — audited first, one real gap found and fixed, not built from scratch**: HRE already existed correctly inside the Senior School official KICD pathway taxonomy (P.1's `KICD_SENIOR_SCHOOL_PATHWAYS`) — confirmed via direct DB query and left completely untouched, not duplicated. The REAL gap was `KE_SUBJECT_PRESETS` in `src/lib/validations/academics.ts` — the general-purpose "Add CBC set" / "Add 8-4-4 set" quick-add buttons used to bootstrap ANY school's whole subject list (independent of whether that school even has Senior School active) — which only ever offered CRE, silently leaving IRE/HRE completely unavailable to any school that hadn't separately gone through the Senior-School-specific P.1 seeding flow. Fixed: both the CBC and 8-4-4 presets now offer all three real Religious Education options (Christian/Islamic/Hindu) together.
- **A second real fairness gap found and fixed while auditing**: `career-discovery.service.ts`'s `CAREER_RULES` — the "Business & Economics" and "Law & Public Service" career-signal rules only ever checked for subject code `"CRE"`. A student who studies IRE or HRE instead — a functionally equivalent subject choice offering the same real career-relevant skills (ethics, civics, communication) — would silently receive ZERO career-signal credit purely because of which Religious Education variant their family practises. Fixed to credit CRE/IRE/HRE equally; safe because a student only ever studies exactly one RE variant at a time, so this is purely additive and never double-counts.
- **New dedicated regression-proof script** `scripts/p6-hre-preset-test.ts` — proves (1) CRE/IRE/HRE all present in both real presets (a pure data check); (2) the REAL `addSubjectPreset()` service function genuinely creates/confirms a real HRE `Subject` row through the live preset data — not just a constant nothing reads; (3) a real test student whose ONLY subject evidence is a strong HRE exam mark genuinely earns real Business & Economics AND Law & Public Service career-discovery credit through the REAL `getCareerDiscoveryProfile()` function — the fairness fix objectively works end-to-end, not just compiles. All 3 assertions passed. Learned mid-session that `Student` is a soft-delete/Recycle-Bin model (G.6) — `tenantDb()`'s `deleteMany()` correctly just sets `deletedAt` for real app usage, but a genuinely throwaway TEST student should leave zero trace, so cleanup was fixed to use the raw `db` client directly for a true hard delete. All throwaway rows (test class, test student, exam, exam result) confirmed fully gone (not just soft-deleted) afterward via direct DB query.
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. No schema migration needed this chunk (no DB changes). `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent logs. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` and `scripts/p5-timetable-proof-test.ts` → both still pass clean, zero regression. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0.
