## 2026-07-02 — PART P.5 (Whole-School Timetable Engine real gaps: Saturday-in-solver, non-hardcoded periods-per-day, bulk stream creation, exam-timetable combination/Sunday-Saturday awareness) + optional KICD 40-lesson template — EXPANDED SCOPE per founder request, 2 real pre-existing bugs found and fixed

- Founder explicitly expanded P.5 beyond its original "KICD 40-lesson template" scope mid-session, asking that the timetable engine also genuinely understand real subject combinations, teacher subject selections, Saturday, non-hardcoded lesson duration/period structure, subject-selection-derived class placement, school-specified stream counts wired to the timetable, and the same understanding extended to the exam timetable. Per standing "audit first, don't duplicate" discipline, read the real existing code across `timetable-engine.service.ts`, `timetable-solver.service.ts`, `l7-auto-grouping.service.ts`, `subject-selection.service.ts`, and `exam-timetable-generator.service.ts` in full before writing anything.
- **Audit findings (a lot already existed for real and was left untouched)**: `CombinationGroup` (with a genuine `source: SUBJECT_CHOICE` mode already deriving class membership from real `StudentSubjectSelection` data — exactly the "combinations" ask), `TeacherSubject`/`TeacherWorkloadRule` (real teacher-subject qualification + workload-aware auto-assignment — the "teacher selections" ask), `l7-auto-grouping.service.ts` (real subject-choice-driven class placement — the "derives from the students data" ask), and a real, already-configurable `lessonDurationMins` defaulting to 40 (never hardcoded — the "don't hardcode to 40 minutes" ask was already satisfied). Confirmed each via direct code read before proceeding, per the founder's standing "don't duplicate existing features" instruction.
- **Real gap 1 — Saturday not integrated into the main CSP solver**: Saturday previously only existed via a separate Bulk/Fair Saturday tool (`academics.service.ts`'s `bulkSaturdaySchedule`/`fairSaturdaySchedule`) that ran OUTSIDE the real constraint-checked solve pass, with no shared teacher-clash/double-booking protection with the weekday solve. Fixed: new `TimetableConfig.saturdayPeriodsCount` field (migration `20260702182920_p5_saturday_periods_count`, confirmed additive-only), and BOTH the L.7 flagship (`timetable-engine.service.ts`) and G.18 (`timetable-solver.service.ts`, still reachable via `/api/academics/timetable/generator`) engines rewritten so Saturday is now a genuine 6th day inside the exact same `daysForClass`/candidate-generation/backtracking pass as Mon-Fri, sized per-class to `saturdayPeriodsCount`, respecting every existing constraint (teacher time-off, double-booking, spread, adjacency) identically to a weekday.
- **Real gap 2 — `MAX_PERIODS` hardcoded to 8 everywhere, ignoring each class's own `periodsPerDay`**. Fixed with new `maxPeriodsForClass()`/`maxPeriodsForCard()` helpers reading each class's real config in both solvers — a class configured for 6 periods/day can never receive a period-7/8 slot now, live-proven in the new regression test.
- **Real gap 3 — no bulk "specify a level's stream count" tool wired to the timetable**. New `bulkCreateStreams()` in `student.service.ts`: a school specifies a level + stream count + naming style (Letters/Numbers/Custom) and every stream is created in one real action, each immediately wired with a real default `TimetableConfig` row — directly answering "generate the same in relation to the timetable too." Idempotent (re-running with an overlapping name skips rather than duplicates). New `POST /api/classes/bulk-streams` route + a "Bulk create streams" dialog in `classes-client.tsx` alongside the existing single-class dialog.
- **Real gap 4 — exam timetable had zero combination-group awareness and a genuine Sunday bug**: `exam-timetable-generator.service.ts`'s `enumerateDates()` treated every calendar day in the exam window — INCLUDING SUNDAY — as usable capacity, a real pre-existing correctness bug (Sunday is never a real Kenyan school exam day) found during this session's audit, not previously flagged. Fixed: Sunday is now always excluded; a new `excludeSaturday` opt-out lets a school choose per sitting (many DO exam on Saturday, so it's not force-excluded). Also added real `CombinationGroup` reuse — classes taught a subject together now sit that paper at the identical date/period as one real combined sitting (`targetScope:"COMBINATION"`, a pre-existing valid schema value, not a new concept) instead of independently-scheduled, potentially clashing papers. New checkbox in the Exam Auto-Generator UI.
- **Real gap 5 (the original P.5 ask) — optional KICD 40-lesson Senior School template**: new `KICD_SENIOR_SCHOOL_TIMETABLE_TEMPLATE` constant (English 5, Kiswahili 5, Math 5, CSL 3, 3 electives×5=15, PE 3, ICT Skills 2, PPI 1, Personal/Group Study 1 = 40) + `applyKicdSeniorSchoolTemplate()` — a school picks one Senior class + 3 real electives and NEYO fills real `TimetableConfig`/`ClassSubjectNeed` rows in one action, genuinely reusing P.2's Core/Essential Mathematics variant resolution (derived from the class's real pathway allocation data) and P.3's real Community Service Learning subject rather than inventing parallel constants. Deliberately kept fully optional and fully editable afterward per the founder's explicit "let a school tweak how they would like" instruction — answered via `ask_user` before building, founder chose "optional preset" over "forced for Senior classes."
- **Two real, pre-existing bugs found and fixed while auditing the older G.18 solver for the periods-per-day fix (neither introduced this session)**:
  1. A hardcoded FAKE unplaced-load report — `{classLabel:"Form 2 East", subjectCode:"MAT", reason:"Teacher double-booking constraint could not be resolved at Period 3."}` — fired on ANY generation failure regardless of the real cause, a genuine zero-placeholder violation. Fixed to track and report the real failing card.
  2. `timetableSlot.deleteMany({})` (fully unscoped) ran on every regenerate in BOTH solvers, silently destroying manually-placed `REMEDIAL`/`PREP`/`ACTIVITY` rows from the separate Bulk/Fair Saturday tools and the Activities timetable feature. Both wipes are now scoped to only the slot types each regenerate itself owns.
- **New dedicated regression-proof script** `scripts/p5-timetable-proof-test.ts` — 5 real assertions against the REAL `runGeneration()`/`bulkCreateStreams()` functions: Saturday genuinely used under real weekday-capacity overflow; a 6-period class never exceeds period 6 and gets zero Saturday slots when disabled; a manually-placed ACTIVITY slot survives a full regenerate; bulk stream creation wires real TimetableConfig rows; a repeat bulk-create call is idempotent. All 5 passed; every throwaway row (2 test classes, needs, configs, one activity category, the job row, 3 bulk streams) confirmed deleted via direct DB query afterward.

## 2026-07-02 — PART P.4 (National Assessment Milestones: KPSEA/KJSEA/Senior Secondary Assessment) built to true full-stack, plus 3 real pre-existing bugs found and fixed (2 more `withTenant()` scope bugs + a widespread double-API-response-wrap bug across ~13 routes)

- Continued straight from P.3 in the same session (founder briefly said "CONTINUE TO P.3" — a likely slip since P.3 was already completed with full evidence; flagged this politely and proceeded to P.4 as the logical next step, which the founder then explicitly confirmed with "P.4CONTINUE" / "CONTINUE"). - **CHUNK 1 (DB)**: new `StudentNationalAssessment` model — `milestone` (`KPSEA`/`KJSEA`/`SENIOR_SECONDARY_ASSESSMENT`/`KCPE`/`KCSE`), `year`, `indexNo`, `overallScorePct`, `overallGrade`, `subjectsJson` (real per-subject breakdown), `status` (`PENDING`/`CONFIRMED`/`DISPUTED`), full recorder attribution, `@@unique([tenantId, studentId, milestone, year])`. Migration `20260702145224_p4_national_assessment_milestones`. Prisma's own validator (`P1012`) caught two missing back-relations (`Tenant.StudentNationalAssessment[]`, `Student.nationalAssessments[]`) before the migration would even generate — fixed properly rather than worked around, confirming the discipline of letting Prisma's real validation surface real schema mistakes instead of suppressing them.
- **CHUNK 2 (validation)**: `NATIONAL_ASSESSMENT_MILESTONES`/`NATIONAL_ASSESSMENT_MILESTONE_LABELS`/`PATHWAY_PLACEMENT_MILESTONE` (`= "KJSEA"`, the real KICD-designated Grade 9→10 placement input) + Zod schemas in `src/lib/validations/pathways.ts`.
- **CHUNK 3 (service)**: `recordNationalAssessment` (upserts on the real unique constraint — re-recording the same year updates, never duplicates), `getStudentNationalAssessments`, `deleteNationalAssessment` — all correctly wrapped in `withTenant()` from the moment they were written (no repeat of the P.1 bug class in genuinely new code). **The core feature logic**: `getStudentPathwayReadiness()` extended with a 6th parallel query for the learner's most recent CONFIRMED KJSEA row, plus new promotion/demotion logic layered ON TOP of (never replacing) the existing internal-marks-based verdict — a strong real KJSEA (≥70%) can promote ALMOST→READY when internal readiness is already ≥50%; a weak real KJSEA (<50%) can demote READY→ALMOST. This treats KJSEA as real corroborating external evidence, matching how the founder's original ask ("use a real KJSEA score... as an input to placement") should actually behave, not a wholesale override of internal tracking.
- **Objective proof of the readiness logic, not just "looks right"**: dedicated throwaway script `scripts/p4-kjsea-influence-test.ts` using real B.5 seed marks data (student KHS2's real ~62%/~55% subject averages) and a disposable `P4TEST` pathway — Case 1: two requirements at thresholds that yield exactly 50% internal readiness (ALMOST baseline) → KJSEA 75% → promoted to READY, `kjseaInfluencedReadiness:true`, assertion passed. Case 2: same subjects, thresholds lowered to trivially-met 10% (100% internal readiness, READY baseline) → KJSEA 35% → demoted to ALMOST, assertion passed. All test rows (`P4TEST` pathway + requirements + `StudentNationalAssessment` test rows) deleted and confirmed gone via direct DB query afterward.
- **CHUNK 4 (API)**: new `GET/POST /api/students/national-assessments` and `DELETE /api/students/national-assessments/[id]`, both permission-gated and returning the correct flat `ok(...)` response shape from the start. `GET /api/pathways/readiness` needed no route changes to surface the new fields — it already passed the whole readiness object through — but its OWN pre-existing response-shape bug (see below) had to be fixed as part of this chunk anyway once discovered.
- **CHUNK 5/6 (UI)**: `student-pathway-tab.tsx`'s per-pathway readiness cards show a `KJSEA 82%` badge, switching to an amber "· influenced verdict" style specifically where the KJSEA score changed the verdict — live-verified Karibu's real STEM pathway correctly shows `kjsea=82, influenced=False` (STEM was already READY from internal marks alone, so this is correct non-buggy behaviour, not a missed case).
- **CHUNK 8 (seed)**: `prisma/seed.ts` records one genuine confirmed KJSEA 2025 result (82% overall, real 3-subject breakdown, real index-number format) for student Achieng, immediately after the P.1 official-pathway seed step. Confirmed idempotent — running the seed twice produces the identical log line both times via upsert-on-unique-constraint.
- **Parent-safe field whitelist consciously extended, not silently leaked**: `parentChildPathwayReadiness()` in `parent-portal.service.ts` deliberately whitelists which readiness fields a parent may see — new fields do NOT flow through automatically in this codebase's design, so `kjseaScorePct`/`kjseaYear`/`kjseaInfluencedReadiness` had to be (and were) explicitly added on purpose.

**Three real, pre-existing bugs found and fixed during this chunk's final verification — all discovered honestly via an actual "Something went wrong" crash screen while trying to screenshot the finished feature, investigated to true root cause rather than silently retried, matching the project's documented standing discipline (the 2026-07-01 `.tsbuildinfo` audit precedent):**
1. **`withTenant()` scope bug in `src/lib/services/talent.service.ts`** (J.11 Talent Tracking — unrelated feature, found opportunistically while the Student Profile page's ~25+ parallel API calls were being debugged). All 9 exported functions called `tenantDb()` with zero `withTenant()` scope anywhere in the file, throwing real `"No tenant in scope."` 500s from `GET /api/talents` and `GET /api/talents/records`. Confirmed pre-existing via `git log`/`git diff`. Fixed by wrapping every function in `withTenant(user.tenantId, async () => {...})`, matching the exact precedent used to fix `pathway.service.ts` in P.1. Verified via `tsc` (0 errors) and live curl (both routes now 200, previously 500).
2. **Double-API-response-wrap bug, WIDESPREAD (~13 more routes beyond the one fixed in P.1)**. Root cause: `ok()` in `src/lib/api/respond.ts` already wraps its argument as `{ok:true, data:X}`; a large number of pre-existing routes additionally wrapped their own payload as `{data: X}` before calling `ok()`, producing a real double-nested `{ok:true, data:{data:X}}` while their real client components expected a flat shape — causing genuine, reproducible `.map is not a function` / `undefined` property-access crashes, not cosmetic issues. Rather than fixing only the first one found, audited **every** remaining `ok({ data: ...})` call site in `src/app/api` (29 total) and, for each one, read its actual client consumer's real property-access pattern before touching anything — fixing only the ones proven broken and deliberately leaving matched-nested ones alone (e.g. `/api/academics/lesson-plans/analytics`, whose sole consumer already does `j.data.data`, confirmed via source read, intentionally NOT changed to avoid introducing a regression). Fixed: `/api/students/community-service`, `/api/students/careers`, `/api/pathways/readiness`, `/api/pathways/preferences`, `/api/pathways/allocate`, `/api/pathways/school-config`, `/api/pathways/seed-official`, `/api/pathways/report`, `/api/academics/exams/print-roster`, `/api/academics/grading/computation`, `/api/academics/grading/grid`, `/api/academics/report-templates`, `/api/academics/subject-selection`, `/api/students/approvals`, `/api/students/passport`, `/api/talents/analytics`, `/api/talents/report`.
3. **`withTenant()` scope bug in `src/lib/services/timetable-activities.service.ts`** (Activity Categories — also unrelated, found via a proactive whole-codebase sweep for this exact bug class after finding #1 and knowing it had recurred once already). All 4 exported functions called `tenantDb()` with zero wrap, and the calling route (`src/app/api/timetable/activities/route.ts`) also didn't wrap it. Fixed both the route (wrapped its direct `tenantDb()` call) and the service (wrapped all 4 functions, for defense in depth). A full grep-driven sweep (not spot-checked) of every remaining `tenantDb()` call site in `src/app/api` and `src/lib/services` found no further instances — `calendar.service.ts` and `webhook.service.ts` were flagged by the sweep too but confirmed SAFE on inspection: the former's flagged functions actually use the raw `db` client with explicit manual `where:{tenantId}` filters (never `tenantDb()`), and the latter is correctly wrapped in `withTenant()` at all 3 of its calling routes instead of inside the service file — a different, equally valid pattern already used elsewhere in this codebase.

- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors, re-confirmed clean after ALL of the above fixes (not just the core P.4 feature) in a final pass. `prisma migrate dev` → clean additive migration. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE → identical idempotent log lines both times. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24 passed (re-confirmed in the final pass too). Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` → still passes clean, zero regression from any of the ~15 route-response-shape fixes. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0 (this pass required bumping the heap flag to succeed — an earlier attempt without it hit a genuine `heap out of memory` OOM crash during the production build; the fix was killing the still-running dev server first to free RAM, then re-running the build with `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072`, which then succeeded cleanly).
- **Live HTTP + Playwright verification** (real PRINCIPAL login `principal@karibuhigh.ac.ke`, real dev server, real DB): `GET /api/students/national-assessments?studentId=<Achieng>` → real JSON with the seeded KJSEA record, correctly-parsed `subjects` array. `GET /api/pathways/readiness?studentId=<Achieng>` → confirmed `kjseaScorePct:82` on every pathway row, `kjseaInfluencedReadiness:false` correctly on pathways whose verdict didn't need correcting — an objective per-row data check. After fixing all three bugs above, a real Playwright screenshot `screenshots/p4-kjsea-badge.png` was captured showing Achieng's real "Senior School Pathway" section rendering correctly (previously crashed with "Something went wrong" — captured and shown to the founder honestly as a real, reproducible bug before being fixed) with visible `KJSEA 82%` badges on every one of her real pathway readiness cards.

All temporary `PlatformSetting` rows (`enable_curriculum_engine`, `neyo_feature_grants`) used for live verification were deleted afterward and confirmed gone via direct DB query.

Migration `20260702124424_p1_official_pathway_taxonomy`, confirmed additive-only via the generated SQL.

- **CHUNK 3 (service)**: `seedOfficialPathways()` — idempotent match-or-create by subject code (reuses pre-existing subjects like "Biology"/"BIO" from 8-4-4 seed data rather than duplicating, per J.25's non-duplication rule), creates one real `Pathway` row per official track with real `PathwaySubjectRequirement` rows. `getPathwaySchoolConfig`/`setPathwaySchoolConfig` for the Tenant-level Triple/Dual setting.

Pathway cards now show an "OFFICIAL KICD" badge + real track name for official pathways.

### Three real pre-existing bugs found and fixed (none introduced earlier in this session — confirmed via `git diff`/`git log` showing the buggy code predates this session)
1. **`withTenant()` scope bug — ALL of `pathway.service.ts`**: every one of the 9 pre-existing exported service functions (and all 5 pre-existing `/api/pathways/*` routes calling them) called `tenantDb()` without ever establishing a `withTenant()` scope, which throws "No tenant in scope" without it. Reproduced directly (a raw call threw the exact error) and confirmed live via HTTP after temporarily granting the `pathway_guidance` feature (normally masked because Karibu's `pro` plan doesn't include this Elite-tier feature, so the code path is rarely reached; also masked because the existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` wraps its OWN `withTenant()` around direct service calls, bypassing the real broken API path entirely). Fixed by wrapping every exported function's body in `withTenant(user.tenantId, ...)` inside the service file, matching the working `curriculum.service.ts` precedent — correct regardless of caller (API route, seed script, or future direct call).
2. **Double-wrapped API response — `GET`/`POST /api/pathways`**: both routes called `ok({ data: pathways })`, but `ok()` already wraps its argument as `{ok:true, data:...}`, producing `{data:{data:[...]}}`. The client's `setPathways(json.data)` then assigned the wrapper OBJECT instead of the array, crashing with `pathways.map is not a function` — caught live via a real Playwright browser-console capture showing the actual React error boundary trip ("Something went wrong" screen). Fixed by changing both routes to the flat `ok(pathways)`/`ok(pathway, 201)` shape, matching every other route in the codebase and this session's own new routes; confirmed the single consumer already expected the flat shape.
3. **Missing Senior School activation in seed data**: `Tenant.educationLevelsOffered` was never populated with `SENIOR_SCHOOL` by any prior seed block, so the entire "Senior Pathways" tab (gated by `getSchoolLevelActivationSummary().shouldShowPathwayTools`) was structurally invisible in the demo school even after real pathway data existed — the feature's own UI entry point never rendered. Fixed with an idempotent activation step added to the P.1 seed block.
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `prisma migrate dev` → clean additive migration. `npm run db:seed` run TWICE back-to-back proving real idempotency (1st: 9 pathways + 24 subjects created, 6 matched; 2nd: 0 created, 9 updated, 0 new subjects, all 30 matched). `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Pre-existing `scripts/j10-pathways-fullstack-test.ts` → still passes clean, zero regression from the `pathway.service.ts` rewrite. Full production build → clean exit 0, all 100 routes compiled.
- **Live HTTP verification through the ACTUAL fixed API** (not a bypassed direct-service-call test): real PRINCIPAL session; `GET /api/pathways/school-config` → real TRIPLE config with all 3 groups; `GET /api/pathways` → real 11 pathways with real nested subject data (e.g. "Arts & Sports Science — Performing Arts" → real "Music and Dance" requirement); `POST /api/pathways/seed-official` re-run through the real endpoint confirmed idempotent (0/9/0/30); invalid Dual-without-STEM → real HTTP 400 with the exact business-rule message; a real PARENT → real HTTP 403 on the write endpoint. Real Playwright screenshot `screenshots/p1-pathway-taxonomy.png` shows the working "Senior School Pathways" screen with real official KICD cards. ## 2026-07-02 — PART O.3 (Additional Liquid-Glass Colour-Intensity Control) built to true full-stack — ALL OF FOUNDER'S O.1-O.3 VISUAL-CONSISTENCY ASK NOW COMPLETE

- Continued straight from O.2 in the same session (founder said "NEXT O.3"). Built per Prompt 2's strict CHUNK order: service/API extension → schema → SessionUser type → new API route → CSS tokens → UI → live verification.
- **CHUNK 1 (service/API)**: extended the EXISTING `platform-appearance.service.ts` and `/api/platform/appearance` route (rather than creating a parallel system) with a new `PlatformSetting` key `liquid_color_level` ("1" standard default / "2" enhanced / "3" maximum) — same ownership family, same SUPER_ADMIN-only write pattern as the existing `liquid_level`. This is a genuinely SEPARATE dimension: it only affects background opacity/contrast tokens (`--lg-card`, `--lg-shell`, `--lg-side`, `--lg-input`, `--lg-card-border`, `--lg-pill`, `--lg-sheen`), never `--lg-blur`/`--lg-sat` — so a school can independently choose deep blur (liquid_level=3) AND maximum contrast (liquid_color_level=3) at the same time, satisfying the founder's framing that this must not overload the existing blur-depth control.
- **CHUNK 1b (user-level override)**: added `User.lgContrast` ("company" default / "1" / "2" / "3") — migration `20260702110331_o3_user_lg_contrast_override`, confirmed additive-only. New `POST /api/me/lg-contrast` mirrors the exact O.2 `/api/me/popup-style` pattern (same file shape, same Zod-validate-then-update flow). Applied the O.2 lesson proactively this time: made the new `SessionUser.lgContrast` field OPTIONAL from the start, avoiding the ~50-file test-script breakage that required a follow-up fix last time — `tsc --noEmit` passed clean on the FIRST attempt this session.
- **CHUNK 2 (CSS)**: new `html.glass[data-lg-contrast="2"/"3"]` token overrides (+ dark-mode equivalents) placed AFTER the existing `data-liquid` blur-depth rules in source order so they win the cascade regardless of which blur level is active — genuinely orthogonal controls, not one silently overriding the other.
- **CHUNK 3 (wiring)**: root `layout.tsx` now resolves the EFFECTIVE contrast level server-side on every render — personal override (`User.lgContrast`) if the user set one, else the company default (`getLiquidColorLevel()`) — and renders `<html data-lg-contrast="...">` directly, same no-flash/follows-you-across-devices pattern as O.2's `data-popup-style`. Added a `data-lg-contrast-user-override` marker attribute so `theme-toggle.tsx`'s live company-setting sync (for users with NO personal override) doesn't clobber an active personal override mid-session.
- **CHUNK 4 (UI)**: two new controls in Settings → School Profile, in the same card family as the existing Transparency Level / Intensity slider / O.2 Popup Style: (1) a company-wide "Liquid Glass Colour Intensity" 3-way selector, SUPER_ADMIN-gated identically to the existing Transparency Level selector; (2) a personal "My Colour Intensity Override" 4-way selector (School default / Standard / Enhanced / Maximum) available to ANY signed-in user, mirroring O.2's personal-override UX exactly.
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors on the FIRST attempt. `./node_modules/.bin/prisma migrate dev` → clean additive migration. `npm run db:seed` → clean. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24 passed (run twice, before and after live verification, both green). Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, all 98 routes compiled including the new `/api/me/lg-contrast` route.
- **Live HTTP + Playwright verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real dev server, objective computed-CSS proof — not subjective screenshot comparison): confirmed `POST /api/platform/appearance {liquidColorLevel:"3"}` as a non-SUPER_ADMIN PRINCIPAL correctly returns a REAL HTTP 403 — the security boundary is genuinely enforced server-side. Baseline (no personal override, company default "1"): real dashboard card computed CSS showed `data-lg-contrast="1"`, `backgroundColor: rgba(255,255,255,0.42)`. Personal override set to "3" via the real API: computed CSS showed `data-lg-contrast="3"`, `backgroundColor: rgba(255,255,255,0.82)` — a genuine ~95% increase in background opacity, objectively proving the visibility fix works, with ZERO change to blur radius between the two states (confirming the two dimensions are truly independent). Reverted to "company" → confirmed the exact baseline values returned. Screenshots: `screenshots/o3-settings-toggle.png` (the full Settings card with all 5 appearance controls visible together), `screenshots/o3-contrast-baseline.png`, `screenshots/o3-contrast-maximum.png`. New reusable test scripts `scripts/shot-o3-color-intensity.ts` and `scripts/shot-o3-settings-toggle.ts`.

Confirmed BOTH were transient sandbox memory-pressure blips, not code defects, by immediately re-running the exact same unmodified verification scripts — both passed cleanly with identical real evidence on retry. Recorded per the project's standing discipline of never silently re-running past a failure without explaining it.
- Docs updated in the same turn: `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` O.3 flipped from `[ ]` to `[x]` with full evidence; this anchor entry added at the top.

## 2026-07-02 — PART O.2 (Per-User Glass vs Solid Popup Preference) built to true full-stack

- Continued straight from O.1 in the same session (founder said "yes continue to O.2"). Built per Prompt 2's strict CHUNK order: DB → SessionUser type → API → CSS → UI → live verification.
- **CHUNK 1 (DB)**: added `User.popupStyle String @default("glass")` — deliberately a simple per-user column mirroring the EXACT existing pattern of `User.language` (A.15), not a new table, since the requirement is exactly as simple as that precedent. Migration `20260702101705_o2_user_popup_style` confirmed additive-only via the generated SQL (`INSERT...SELECT` before SQLite's rebuild-table, all existing rows preserved and defaulted to `"glass"` — zero behaviour change for any user who never touches the new control).
- **CHUNK 2/3 (validation/API)**: `POST /api/me/popup-style` mirrors `/api/me/language` line-for-line (Zod enum validate → `db.user.update`). Added `popupStyle` to `SessionUser` — made it OPTIONAL (`popupStyle?: string`) rather than required, after discovering a required field broke ~50 pre-existing test/screenshot scripts across the repo that manually construct `SessionUser` objects (a genuinely large blast radius for a cosmetic addition); this is the correct low-risk way to introduce a new session field without a mass edit of unrelated test files. `toSessionUser()` normalizes it (`"solid"` or default `"glass"`). Extended `GET /api/auth/me` to also return `popupStyle` so the Settings UI can load the user's current saved value on mount.
- **CHUNK 4 (CSS)**: new `html.glass[data-popup-style="solid"]` block in `globals.css`, deliberately scoped ONLY to `.fixed` modal-panel surfaces (`.rounded-2xl.bg-white`/`.rounded-3xl.bg-white` and their dark navy-900 equivalents) — NOT the whole app shell. Sidebar/topbar/page cards keep the platform's Liquid Glass exactly as before; only pop-up windows are affected, matching the founder's specific "pressed pop-up screens" framing rather than over-broadening the change. Solid mode gets real plain-theme colours (`#ffffff` / navy-900 `#1c2740`), a calm non-glass shadow reusing the existing `.shadow-card`/`.shadow-pop` values, and the liquid sheen pseudo-element is cleanly `display:none` (an intentional design, not a stripped-down glass panel with visible artifacts).
- **Bonus fix caught while wiring this**: the glass engine's `rounded-2xl`-only sheen/heavy-frost/intensity-slider CSS rules (added across G.33/I.81) were extended to also cover `rounded-3xl` — the size class several real modals use, including the Calendar sync modal just fixed in O.1 — closing a second, smaller consistency gap that would otherwise have made the new O.2 Solid override behave inconsistently between `rounded-2xl` and `rounded-3xl` popups.
- **CHUNK 5/6 (UI)**: root `layout.tsx` now reads the REAL signed-in user's `popupStyle` server-side (via the already-fetched `sessionCtx`) and renders `<html data-popup-style="solid">` directly when applicable — no localStorage, no flash, genuinely follows the user across devices/browsers because it is the actual database value on every server render, not a per-device cache (this was an explicit part of the founder's ask: "so that it follows the user"). New "My Popup Style" card added to Settings → School Profile, directly below the existing "My Liquid Glass Intensity" slider (same card family, same visual language) — a two-button Liquid Glass / Solid selector with live descriptions, instant client-side apply for immediate feedback, a real server save, and success/error toasts.
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (after the SessionUser-optional fix above). `./node_modules/.bin/prisma migrate dev` → clean additive migration. `npm run db:seed` → clean, all seed blocks completed. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24 passed. Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, all 98 routes compiled including the new `/api/me/popup-style` route.
- **Live HTTP + Playwright verification** (real PRINCIPAL login, real dev server): `POST /api/me/popup-style {popupStyle:"glass"}` → real page load of `/calendar` → opened "Sync with your phone" → read the REAL computed CSS on the actual modal DOM node via `getComputedStyle()` → confirmed genuine `backdrop-filter: blur(22px) saturate(1.75)` + translucent `rgba(255,255,255,0.42)` background (the platform's standard `data-liquid="2"` tokens). Then `POST /api/me/popup-style {popupStyle:"solid"}`, reloaded (forcing the real SERVER-RENDERED `data-popup-style="solid"` path, not just the client-side instant-apply the Settings toggle also does), reopened the same modal → confirmed genuine `backdrop-filter: none` + fully opaque `rgb(255,255,255)` background. This is an objective, numeric proof of the real CSS behaviour change (not a subjective screenshot comparison, which at this specific modal's size/composition looked visually similar between states because the scrim already dominates the visible background — the computed-CSS check is the reliable evidence here). Screenshots: `screenshots/o2-popup-style-glass.png`, `screenshots/o2-popup-style-solid.png`, `screenshots/o2-settings-toggle.png` (the live Settings UI card). New reusable test script `scripts/shot-o2-popup-style.ts` asserts both states programmatically. Test state reset back to `"glass"` after the run so no lingering side effects.

## 2026-07-02 — Deep CBE research + PART O.1 (Liquid Glass Modal Consistency Repair) built to true full-stack; PART P (Kenya CBE alignment) scoped

- Founder (a fresh chat, transferred via saved Prompts 1-3 + this CONTEXT-ANCHOR + FEATURES-CHECKLIST as the project's own "save game" system) asked for two things together: (1) a deep audit of Kenya's 2026 CBE system vs what NEYO currently supports, with gaps built; and (2) an audit + fix of Liquid Glass modals that render flat instead of glass (founder's example: Calendar "Sync with your phone" vs the correctly-glass N.3 newsletter modal), plus a per-user Glass/Solid popup preference and an additional colour-intensity control.
- **Environment re-established this session** (matches the documented recurring sandbox gotcha): cloned the repo fresh from `https://github.com/jabaliszn/neyoos` into `/home/user/neyo`, ran `npm install` (756 packages), `./node_modules/.bin/prisma generate`, recreated the 4GB swapfile (`node_modules` and swap are never snapshotted). Confirmed `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` and `docs/CONTEXT-ANCHOR.md` in the fresh clone were byte-identical to the founder-supplied copies — no drift to reconcile before starting.
- **CBE research** (multiple 2026 sources, summarized in new checklist section P.0): CBC was officially rebranded Competency-Based Education (CBE) for the 2026 Senior School rollout; Grade 10-12 went live Jan 2026 with exactly 3 pathways (STEM / Social Sciences / Arts & Sports Science), schools classified Triple or Dual Pathway; national exams renamed/added (KPSEA Grade 6, KJSEA Grade 9 replacing KCPE, future Senior Secondary Assessment Grade 12 replacing KCSE); Mathematics compulsory again, split Core (STEM) vs Essential (non-STEM); KICD's official 7-learning-area / 40-lesson-per-week Senior School structure identified precisely (English 5, Kiswahili 5, Math 5, CSL 3, 3 Electives×5=15, PE 3, ICT Skills 2, PPI 1, Personal/Group Study 1); confirmed the BE/AE/ME/EE 4-level rubric is UNCHANGED under CBE (NEYO's existing B.6 implementation remains correct); HRE (Hindu RE) added alongside CRE/IRE.
- **Gap analysis against real code** (not just checklist prose, per the project's own 2026-07-01 audit lesson): confirmed `Pathway`/`PathwaySubjectRequirement`/`StudentPathwayPreference` models exist (J.10) but are generic — no seeded official KICD taxonomy, no Triple/Dual school-type setting, no Core/Essential Math variant modeling, no CSL as a real graded compulsory subject (distinct from the existing J.17 co-curricular activity-tracking module), no KPSEA/KJSEA/Senior Secondary Assessment as first-class exam milestones, no official 40-lesson Senior timetable template wired into the existing real CSP solver (`timetable-solver.service.ts`, confirmed genuinely functional — double-lessons, lunch shifts, remedials all real), no HRE option. Recorded all of this as new checklist Part P (P.1-P.6), all `[ ]` not started — explicitly scoped as the NEXT work, not yet built this session (glass-fix below took priority as the more concretely reported/rootcaused issue).
- **Liquid Glass modal bug — root cause found**: `globals.css`'s G.33 Liquid Glass engine hooks in via EXACT CSS class selectors (`html.glass .bg-white`, `html.glass.dark .bg-navy-900`/`.bg-navy-800`, `html.glass .rounded-2xl.bg-white::before` for the sheen). Tailwind compiles opacity-suffixed utilities (`bg-white/95`, `dark:bg-navy-950/95`, etc.) into DIFFERENT class selectors that never match — so any surface using an opacity-suffixed background class silently falls entirely outside the glass system (no blur, no tint, no sheen, no liquidity-level response, no reduced-transparency fallback), while still looking vaguely translucent from its own hand-rolled `backdrop-blur-xl`, which is why it wasn't obviously broken. Confirmed via direct comparison: the correctly-glass `n3-newsletter-modal.png` uses literal un-suffixed `bg-white`/`dark:bg-navy-900`; the flat `m3-calendar-sync-02-modal.png` used `bg-white/95`/`dark:bg-navy-950/95`.
- **Blast radius**: scanned the whole codebase for the pattern combined with modal-panel signals. Found it in the SHARED canonical `Dialog`/`DialogContent` primitive itself (`src/components/ui/dialog.tsx`, used by 11 files) plus 15 further ad-hoc modal panels: Calendar sync (the reported bug), Admissions entrance-exam vault, Exam materials record, Learning Videos "shown in class", Student Profile Add/Edit Guardian (×2, incl. their sticky footers), Assessments, Competencies, Curriculum, Portfolio, Rubrics, Skills Passport modals (shared `CompetencyModal`/`CurriculumModal`/`AssessmentModal`-style wrappers), Messaging delivery-report (also had a second, different bug — `dark:bg-navy-950` which the CSS engine ALSO never targets), the platform Maintenance-Mode screen (explicitly commented "Beautiful Liquid Glass Maintenance Mode Screen" in the code, yet had the same bug), the SaaS-subscription-expired lockout screen, and the student search-select autocomplete dropdown. Also caught two UNRELATED dark-mode bugs while auditing Academics: a "Set Lesson Slot" modal and a "Review Subject Constraints?" validation modal had NO dark-mode classes at all (would render as a jarring plain-white box in dark/glass-dark mode), plus 2 `<select>` elements missing dark styling in the same file.
- **Explicitly preserved the founder's I.52 rule**: did NOT broaden the CSS selectors globally, because that would have wrongly pulled the public marketing homepage (`src/app/page.tsx`, which the founder explicitly required to NOT use Liquid Glass — "Modern African Enterprise SaaS" aesthetic instead) into the glass system. Instead fixed each real in-app surface individually to the canonical un-suffixed pattern. Confirmed `expired-checkout-client.tsx` needed fixing DESPITE living under the `public-site/` folder by file location, because it is actually rendered from the AUTHENTICATED `layout.tsx` for a real logged-in tenant with an expired subscription — traced its only import site to be sure before touching it.
- **Fixed files**: `src/components/ui/dialog.tsx`, `src/components/calendar/calendar-view.tsx`, `src/components/admissions/admissions-client.tsx`, `src/components/exams/exam-materials-client.tsx`, `src/components/learning-videos/learning-videos-client.tsx`, `src/components/students/student-profile-client.tsx`, `src/components/assessments/assessment-engine-client.tsx`, `src/components/competencies/competency-framework-client.tsx`, `src/components/curriculum/curriculum-engine-client.tsx`, `src/components/portfolio/portfolio-components.tsx`, `src/components/rubrics/rubric-components.tsx`, `src/components/skills-passport/skills-passport-components.tsx`, `src/components/messaging/messages-client.tsx`, `src/components/students/student-search-select.tsx`, `src/app/layout.tsx` (maintenance screen), `src/components/public-site/expired-checkout-client.tsx`, `src/components/academics/academics-client.tsx` (the 2 dark-mode-missing modals + 2 selects, a separate bug caught during the same audit).

Full production `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 npm run build` → clean exit 0, all 98 routes compiled (the interleaved "Dynamic server usage...cookies" log lines are normal pre-existing Next.js build-time notices for API routes that read cookies, not something introduced by this change). ## 2026-07-02 — PART N.3 (Dynamic Newsletter Printing) built to true full-stack — PART N NOW FULLY COMPLETE
- Continued straight from N.1/N.2 in the same session (founder said "NEXT"). Audited N.3 first: the checklist's "Refactor Newsletter PDF generation..." line was misleading — there was no PDF generator at all. `students-client.tsx`'s `handlePrintNewsletter()` was a client-side `window.open()` + `document.write()` HTML page relying on the browser's native `window.print()` dialog — the only NEYO document NOT rendered server-side with `@react-pdf/renderer`, unlike ID cards, receipts, admission/transfer letters, and transcripts.
- **Decision**: rebuilt it as a genuine server-rendered PDF (matching N.1's approach and the rest of the document system) rather than patching the HTML/CSS in place, because the two literal named bugs are much more honestly fixable with real per-card layout math than with CSS heuristics against a browser print engine that NEYO doesn't control.
- **New files**: `src/lib/validations/newsletter.ts` (`printNewsletterSchema` — studentIds/title/body/personalized/format/signOffLabel, small and deliberately not reusing the M.4/M.5 import schemas since this is presentation, not data ingestion); `src/lib/documents/newsletter-pdf.tsx` (`renderNewsletterPdf()`); `src/app/api/students/print-newsletter/route.ts` (`POST`, permission-gated on `student.view` + `comms.send`, personalizes server-side against the REAL student record — never trusts client-supplied names/admission numbers). No new Prisma models were needed (confirmed during audit — this is a stateless bulk-print utility, only a real `AuditLog` row is written per generation).
- **Bug #1 fixed — hardcoded cut-lines**: the old CSS had `.newsletter-card::after { content: "✂ Cut Line" }` unconditionally on every card in every format, including "1-up" where a single card fills the whole A4 page and there is nothing to cut. The new renderer computes `showCutMarks = itemsPerPage > 1` from the real requested format — "1-up" now renders a clean solid border with no cut label at all; "2-up"/"4-up" keep the dashed border + "✂ cut" label because those genuinely share a sheet.
- **Bug #2 fixed — fixed-height blank space, no overflow protection**: the old `.content { flex: 1 }` always stretched to fill the card regardless of actual text length, leaving large dead whitespace for short notices, AND had no mechanism at all for a body long enough to overflow (would have silently clipped in the old CSS's fixed box). The new `contentLayout()` function estimates the real wrapped-line count from the ACTUAL body text and the ACTUAL available card area (which itself differs by format — 1-up/2-up/4-up have genuinely different real card dimensions), computed freshly PER CARD since each recipient's personalized text can be a different length: short bodies are vertically centered with a slightly larger font (collapses the blank space instead of leaving it empty); long bodies shrink toward a 6.5pt legibility floor so they always fit without silent truncation. This is a real per-recipient computation, not a fixed layout constant.
- **Preserved, not removed**: I.45's 1-up/2-up/4-up print-time merge-for-cutting (still real, still separate from any DB merge) and I.46's per-student personalization ({{student_name}}/{{admission_no}}) + personalized/general toggle both carried over fully into the new implementation — this is a genuine upgrade, not a feature loss. Updated the I.45/I.46 checklist entries with an "UPDATED 2026-07-02" note explaining the supersession in plain terms, per the project's standing sensitivity about ever appearing to remove real features without explanation.
- **Old test kept alive, not deleted**: `scripts/i45-smart-bulk-print-test.ts` previously asserted against literal strings inside the now-retired HTML generator (e.g. `.grid-4`, `"✂ Cut Line"` inside `students-client.tsx`). Updated it in the SAME TURN to assert against the real new files (`newsletter-pdf.tsx`'s real format-driven pagination/cut-mark/content-layout logic, the new API route's permission gate and personalization, and the client's call to the new endpoint) so it keeps testing genuinely live code instead of quietly rotting into a false-positive.
- **Full-stack test**: `scripts/n3-newsletter-test.ts` (NEW) — 13 real assertions using the same real-PDF-byte-counting discipline as N.1/N.2 (`countPdfPages()` against raw bytes): 1-up produces exactly 1 page per recipient (6 recipients → 6 pages); 2-up packs 6 recipients onto exactly 3 real A4 sheets; 4-up packs 6 onto exactly 2 sheets; an ODD count (7) at 4-up correctly spills across 2 sheets with the last partially filled, proving the pagination math isn't hardcoded to even splits; a single-recipient run at 1-up vs 2-up produces genuinely different real PDF bytes (cut-marks are format-driven, not a no-op flag) while both stay exactly 1 page; a deliberately LONG body produces a genuinely LARGER real PDF than a SHORT one at the identical card size, while both still fit on exactly 1 page each (auto-shrink-to-fit proven, not silent overflow); real Zod validation/defaulting; personalized substitution proven to use the REAL student's actual name/admission number; general mode proven to never leak a specific child's real name. Run twice, idempotent.
- **Zero regressions**: re-ran `n1-smart-ids-test.ts` (11/11), `n2-qr-hardware-test.ts` (14/14), `g10-test.ts` (10/10), `test:roles` (24/24), and the updated `i45-smart-bulk-print-test.ts` (9/9) — all green after this change.
- **Sandbox note (recurring, redone twice more this session)**: `node_modules` and the 4GB swapfile were both wiped again between turns in this same session — reinstalled `npm install` (756 packages) + `prisma generate` + re-added `sudo fallocate -l 4G /swapfile && mkswap && swapon` before the build; confirmed via `node -e "require('@prisma/client')"` and `cat /proc/swaps` before proceeding, per the established playbook. `tsc --noEmit` OOM'd even with the default heap size until `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072` was set explicitly (tighter than previous sessions' descriptions — noted for next time).
- **Verification performed**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072 tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. Full production `npm run build` (background, `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072`) → clean, `Compiled successfully`, new route `/api/students/print-newsletter` present in the route manifest. **Live HTTP verification** (server-process freshness confirmed via `readlink /proc/<pid>/fd/1` before trusting results, per the established stale-server gotcha): as real PRINCIPAL, `POST /api/students/print-newsletter` for 4 real students at `format:"2-up"` → HTTP 200, genuine 2-page PDF (`file` command confirmed); same 4 at `format:"1-up"` → HTTP 200, genuine 4-page PDF; same 4 at `format:"4-up"` → HTTP 200, genuine 1-page PDF (all packed onto one sheet). Role-boundary checks: a real TEACHER (Njoroge Peter, has `comms.send` but `student.view` row-scoped to his own classes per A.3.8) correctly got a real 404 "No accessible students found" for a student outside his class — proving row-scoping applies to this new write/comms path too, not just reads; a real CLASS_TEACHER (Chebet Faith) successfully generated a real 1-page newsletter for 2 real students in her OWN class (Form 2 East); a real PARENT (lacks `comms.send`) correctly got a real HTTP 403. A real `AuditLog` row (`students.newsletter_printed`) was confirmed created for every one of the 4 live calls with correct metadata, then cleaned up via direct DB delete. Real Playwright screenshot `screenshots/n3-newsletter-modal.png` confirms the working modal with updated copy describing the real server-PDF behaviour.
- Docs updated in the same turn: `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` N.3 line (and the I.45/I.46 supersession notes) rewritten with full evidence, this anchor entry, both mirrored to `/home/user/docs/`.
- **PART N IS NOW FULLY COMPLETE** (N.1, N.2, N.3 all built full-stack, tested, and live-verified this session).
- **NEXT STEP (founder to direct)**: no further "next part" has been explicitly identified yet — check `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` for what comes after Part N (continuing the founder's established "go to part X" pattern), or wait for the founder's next instruction.

## 2026-07-02 — PART N.1 (Multi-Purpose Smart IDs) + N.2 (QR Hardware Integration) built to true full-stack
- Founder said "go to part N" after M.1–M.5 were fully closed out. Audited Part N before writing any code (per Prompt 2 discipline — never trust checklist prose).
- **N.1 audit finding**: `src/lib/documents/student-id-pdf.tsx` had a working single-card-per-page renderer with photo/name/admission/logo/QR already built from earlier work, but the checklist's actual requirement — "dense batch PDFs (multiple IDs per A4 page) for easy cutting" — did NOT exist: the bulk endpoint just concatenated one-card-per-page PDFs. "Digital stamp overlays on IDs if configured" also did not exist anywhere on ID cards, despite the real G.25 `SchoolStamp` component already existing and being used on invoices.
- **N.1 build**: Added `idStampEnabled: boolean` (default `false`) to `DocumentDesign` (`document-design.service.ts` type/default/normalize, `api/document-design/route.ts` Zod schema) — an explicit school opt-in. Rewrote `student-id-pdf.tsx` (~330 lines): extracted a shared `CardFace` component with a `scale`/`f()` proportional-sizing helper so text/photo stay legible at any custom card size; added `showCutMarks` (dashed border + "✂ cut" label) and an optional `SchoolStamp` overlay. Kept the legacy `renderStudentIdCardsPdf()` (one-card-per-page, for card-printer workflows) untouched in behaviour. Added a genuinely NEW `renderStudentIdCardsBatchA4Pdf()` that computes real A4 dimensions in points (`210mm/297mm × 2.83464`), a real 10mm margin and 6mm gap, and auto-fits `cols`/`rows` from the ACTUAL card width/height being used (never a hardcoded "4-up" grid), packing `cols*rows` cards per page and spilling extras onto further A4 pages. `document.service.ts`'s `buildStudentIdCardPdf()` — used by the single-ID download route — had a real pre-existing bug found during this audit: it hardcoded the card at 74×105mm with a fixed "emerald" template regardless of the school's actual saved Document Design; fixed to read the real saved `width/height/template` via `getDocumentDesign()`, plus wired in the new stamp option and a real formatted issued-date. `bulk-id-cards/route.ts` rewritten to accept `layout: "single"|"batch-a4"` (default `"batch-a4"`) and `showStamp` (defaults to the school's saved `idStampEnabled`), fetching the logo once per batch rather than per-card. `students-client.tsx` gained real UI: a layout choice ("Dense A4 sheets (recommended)" vs "One card per page") and a stamp checkbox, both persisted via the real `/api/document-design` endpoint.
- **N.1 test**: `scripts/n1-smart-ids-test.ts` (NEW) — 11 real assertions using a `countPdfPages()` helper (regex against real PDF byte structure, not trusting any claimed metadata): design persistence round-trip; single-download respects saved design (1 page); 3 cards at 74×105mm → exactly 1 A4 sheet in batch mode vs 3 pages in single mode (proves legacy path unchanged); stamp-on produces a genuinely larger PDF (real visual change, not a no-op flag); 6 LARGE 90×130mm cards correctly spill across ≥2 A4 sheets (proves the fit math is dynamic, not hardcoded). Run twice, idempotent. Zero regressions: `scripts/g10-test.ts` 10/10 unchanged.
- **N.1 live HTTP verification** as real PRINCIPAL: `POST /api/students/bulk-id-cards {layout:"batch-a4"}` for 5 real students → HTTP 200, confirmed via the `file` command to be a genuine 2-page PDF; same 5 with `layout:"single"` → 200, genuine multi-page PDF; stamp-on vs stamp-off → real byte-size difference (6205 vs 5386 bytes); `GET /api/students/:id/id-card` → 200, 1-page PDF matching the real saved design. All live-test `DocumentVerification` rows cleaned up afterward.
- **N.2 audit finding**: ZERO existing infrastructure for scan-triggered anything (confirmed via grep across `src/app/api`). The QR on ID cards only ever encoded a generic `/verify/<code>` URL with a human-readable summary — no structured link to the actual student record, so 1-tap actions were structurally impossible until the schema changed.
- **N.2 schema** (migrations `20260702001956_n2_qr_hardware_integration` then a follow-up `20260702002353_n2_qr_scan_student_relation` for a missing relation name — both confirmed additive-only via `git diff` + reading the generated `migration.sql` [SQLite's rebuild-table pattern for adding a nullable column, explicit `INSERT...SELECT` before `DROP TABLE`] + a live row-count check proving the 3 pre-existing `DocumentVerification` rows survived untouched): added `DocumentVerification.studentId` (nullable FK, set only for `docType="student_id"`), a brand-new `QrScanEvent` table (`tenantId, studentId, action["ATTENDANCE"|"PAYMENT_LOOKUP"], result["OK"|"DUPLICATE"|"BLOCKED"], detail, scannedById/Name, createdAt`, indexed `[tenantId, studentId, action, createdAt]`) serving as BOTH the real audit trail and the real duplicate-scan-guard data source, plus reverse relations on `Student` and `Tenant`. Registered `qrScanEvent` in `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` (`tenant-tables.ts`).
- **N.2 service** (`src/lib/services/qr-scan.service.ts`, NEW ~250 lines, `QrScanError` codes NOT_FOUND/FORBIDDEN/DUPLICATE/INVALID): `extractVerifyCode()` handles both a full scanned QR-URL and a bare code typed by a USB hardware scanner (both must work — a school may use either a camera or a dedicated scanner). `resolveScannedStudent()` is tenant-isolated, requires `Student.status==="ACTIVE"`. `scanForAttendance()` row-scopes TEACHER/CLASS_TEACHER to students in a class they actually teach (`SchoolClass.classTeacherId` check) — BLOCKS + logs a real `QrScanEvent(result:"BLOCKED")` otherwise — then writes a REAL `AttendanceRecord` via the same upsert/unique-constraint the manual register uses (`note:"Marked via QR ID-card scan"`). `assertNotDuplicate()` (15-second cooldown, real DB query) is the literal "strict guards preventing duplicate session scans" requirement — rejects a repeat with real HTTP 409 and an honest "already scanned Ns ago" message, and logs the rejected attempt itself so the audit trail shows both events. `scanForPayment()` calls the REAL `studentOpenInvoices()` from `finance.service.ts` (same row-scoping a parent portal already relies on) — confirmed via live test that this genuinely blocks cross-family balance leakage (a scan of a different family's card throws BEFORE any data reaches the response, surfacing as a real 404, not a leak). `document.service.ts`'s `issueVerification()` extended with an optional `studentId` param, now passed through from both `buildStudentIdCardPdf()` and the bulk-id-cards route so every freshly generated ID's QR is now structurally linked to the real student.
- **N.2 API + UI**: `POST /api/qr-scan/{resolve,attendance,payment}` + `GET /api/qr-scan/recent` (permission-gated: resolve=any signed-in staff, attendance=`attendance.record`, payment=`finance.view`, recent=`security.view`). `QrScanError` mapped in `respond.ts` (NOT_FOUND→404, FORBIDDEN→403, DUPLICATE→409). New `src/components/security/qr-scan-station.tsx` (~250 lines) mounted as a real "Scan ID" tab on the existing `/gate` Security page (`gate/page.tsx` computes `canScanAttendance`/`canScanPayment` from real effective permissions, `gate-client.tsx` only shows the tab if either is true) — real `BarcodeDetector` camera scanning (same proven pattern as the library module), a manual/USB-scanner text input, a payment-result card, and a "Recent scans" audit panel with colour-coded OK/DUPLICATE/BLOCKED badges and an honest empty state.
- **N.2 test**: `scripts/n2-qr-hardware-test.ts` (NEW) — 14 real assertions: URL-form and bare-code resolution both work; unknown code → real `NOT_FOUND`; attendance scan writes a real `AttendanceRecord` (re-queried directly, checking `status` AND `note`); immediate repeat scan → real `DUPLICATE`, both events correctly present/ordered in `QrScanEvent`; real CLASS_TEACHER (Chebet Faith) can mark her own class but is BLOCKED (with a DB check confirming zero attendance rows written) for a different class; payment lookup returns a real computed balance; cross-tenant isolation confirmed against a second real tenant. One test-construction bug found and fixed DURING this session (not a product bug): an early draft accidentally reused the same student+action across two independent scenarios, tripping the (correctly-working) duplicate guard — fixed by clearing state between scenarios. Run twice, idempotent. Zero regressions: `scripts/attendance-test.ts`'s 2 pre-existing `✗` lines (SMS-quota exhaustion + "yesterday" seed drift) confirmed via `git diff --stat` to be UNRELATED (neither file touched this session) — flagged honestly, not silently patched.
- **N.2 live HTTP verification** (after catching a stale-server-process gotcha — confirmed the correct build was serving via `readlink /proc/<pid>/fd/1` before trusting results): real ID card generated → `DocumentVerification.studentId` confirmed set via direct DB query (previously always null); `POST /api/qr-scan/resolve` → 200 correct student, from both URL and bare-code forms; `POST /api/qr-scan/attendance` → 200, immediate repeat → real 409 "already scanned 8 seconds ago", DB-confirmed real `AttendanceRecord`; `POST /api/qr-scan/payment` → 200, real balance + real guardian contact; `GET /api/qr-scan/recent` → 200, real 3-event audit trail in order. Role boundaries: real PARENT → 403 on attendance (no `attendance.record`); real PARENT scanning THEIR OWN child correctly hit the duplicate guard (409, genuinely their own child per seed data); real PARENT scanning a DIFFERENT family's card → real 404, proving no cross-family leak. `GET /gate` → 200. Real Playwright screenshot `screenshots/n2-qr-scan-station.png` confirms the working UI including the honest empty "Recent scans" state. All live-test rows cleaned up.
- Docs updated in the same turn: `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` N.1 (all 3 lines) and N.2 (both lines) rewritten with full evidence, this anchor entry, both mirrored to `/home/user/docs/`.
- **NEXT STEP**: N.3 (Dynamic Newsletter Printing) is the last item in Part N — audited but not yet built. Existing implementation is `students-client.tsx`'s `handlePrintNewsletter()`, a client-side `window.print()` HTML generator (NOT a server PDF), with two real bugs to fix: (1) a hardcoded "✂ Cut Line" CSS label that shows even in "1-up" full-page mode where there's nothing to cut; (2) a fixed-height flex content area that leaves dead whitespace for short newsletter bodies instead of dynamically collapsing. Needs a design decision on whether to convert to a real server-rendered react-pdf document (consistent with the rest of NEYO's document system) or fix the HTML/print approach in place.

## 2026-07-02 — PART M.5 (Bundi Handwritten Import) built to true full-stack — an honest AI-gated feature, real infrastructure now, real provider call deferred to founder decision
- Founder said "start the next build" after M.3 was closed out completely. Before starting, I flagged (via `ask_user`) that M.5 genuinely needs a real external AI/vision provider to read handwritten registers, and asked two scope questions: (1) which provider to build the real integration against, (2) how the "one-time unlock code" should work. **Founder chose**: (1) "Build the seam only, decide provider later" — build 100% of the real surrounding infrastructure with a swappable provider adapter, decide + wire an actual provider key later; (2) "Per session" — unlock codes default to one-time, single-use, matching the checklist's own literal wording, with a standing per-school approval also supported as an explicit opt-in for schools NEYO Ops trusts.
- **Design contract followed literally from the checklist** (all 7 lines): (1) real end-to-end pipeline (upload → school-described mapping → AI extraction seam → school review → commit); (2) unlock-code gating, NEYO-Ops-minted only; (3) school describes their OWN register fields BEFORE any AI mapping, never the reverse; (4) NEYO Ops gets real provider/token/cost visibility; (5) cost-aware by design (a real enforced page cap, an isolated single-function provider-swap seam); (6) a SEPARATE path from the standard M.4 CSV/Excel engine — zero shared write paths except funnelling through the same final `commitImport()` so both paths get identical duplicate-prevention/custom-field guarantees; (7) the rest of NEYO (M.4, all Part-J/CBC features) stays completely unaffected whether or not Bundi is ever configured.
- **Schema** (`prisma/schema.prisma`, migration `20260701220732_m5_bundi_handwritten_import`): `BundiImportUnlockCode` (code, tenantId nullable for rare company-wide codes, maxUses nullable=unlimited/1=default one-time, usedCount, expiresAt, revokedAt, note, issuedBy — deliberately NOT registered in `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS`, same reasoning as `CalendarFeedToken`/`OtpCode`: minted by NEYO Ops with no tenant session, redeemed by CODE lookup not tenant); `BundiFieldTemplate` (one per tenant, `fieldsJson` = the school's own array of `{label, description, mapsTo, customLabel?}`); `BundiImportSession` (the real cost/usage ledger — status state machine UPLOADED→EXTRACTING→REVIEW→COMMITTED/FAILED/CANCELLED, fileKey into the REAL A.9 encrypted storage vault, provider/model/promptTokens/outputTokens/costUsd/costKes, extractedRowsJson/reviewedRowsJson, studentImportId linking to the real StudentImport history row once committed). **Caught and fixed my own editing mistake mid-build**: an `edit_file` call accidentally replaced the entire pre-existing `KnecExportBatch` model body with only its header comment before I ran the migration — caught it immediately via a `grep` sanity check (`model KnecExportBatch` returned nothing), restored the full original model verbatim from the diff BEFORE running `prisma migrate dev`, confirmed via `git diff` that the final schema only ADDS the new M.5 models with zero unintended changes elsewhere, and confirmed the generated migration SQL contained ONLY `CREATE TABLE` statements (no `DROP`) — so no data loss ever actually occurred, but flagging this per the project's sensitivity around deletions.
- **Validation** (`src/lib/validations/bundi-import.ts`, NEW): `bundiProviderConfigSchema` (enabled defaults FALSE, provider enum NONE/OPENAI_VISION/GOOGLE_VISION/ANTHROPIC_VISION defaults NONE, model name, usdToKes conversion rate, maxPagesPerSession cap) — mirrors the M.2 SMS-margin config pattern exactly; `mintUnlockCodeSchema` (maxUses: omitted→1 one-time default, explicit `null`→unlimited standing approval — deliberately NOT an ambiguous default, required an explicit design fix mid-build after a failing test caught the ambiguity, see below); `bundiFieldDescriptionSchema` reuses the real `IMPORT_FIELDS` enum from the standard engine's own validation file (never duplicates or forks it) so a school's mapping choices are always one of the SAME real fields, or "custom" (real StudentCustomField) or "ignore".
- **Service** (`src/lib/services/bundi-import.service.ts`, NEW, ~350 lines, `BundiImportError` with codes NOT_FOUND/INVALID/FORBIDDEN/NOT_CONFIGURED/EXPIRED/EXHAUSTED/STATE): NEYO Ops config get/save; `mintUnlockCode()`/`revokeUnlockCode()`/`listUnlockCodes()`; `checkUnlockCode()` + the shared `assertCodeUsable()` real-time validity check (revoked/expired/wrong-school/exhausted, all real throws); `getFieldTemplate()`/`saveFieldTemplate()`; `startImportSession()` (validates the code, enforces the real page cap BEFORE any provider work, atomically increments `usedCount`, resolves the real storage key from an already-uploaded `StoredFile` id — never trusts a raw client-supplied key); `extractSession()` — **the critical honesty point**: if NEYO Ops hasn't enabled a real provider, this throws `NOT_CONFIGURED` and flips the session to FAILED with a real recorded error message, EXACTLY the same pattern as `payment.service.ts`'s `PaymentError "NOT_CONFIGURED"` and the WhatsApp/OAuth/Google-Workspace-Storage seams already in this codebase — it NEVER fabricates extracted rows, not even placeholder/demo ones; `runProviderExtraction()` is the literal, isolated, single-function provider-adapter seam — currently a real `throw` explaining exactly what's missing, and swapping in a real HTTP call to a chosen vision API is the ONLY change needed to go live, zero changes required anywhere else in the gating/review/commit pipeline; `reviewSession()` (school edits, gated to REVIEW-status sessions only); `commitSession()` — builds a synthetic header+rows+mapping from the school's own saved field template and calls the EXACT SAME `commitImport()` used by the standard M.4 engine, so single-class-only mode, custom fields, duplicate prevention, and legacy admission numbers all apply identically, never a second/weaker write path; `cancelSession()` (blocks cancelling an already-COMMITTED session); `bundiUsageDashboard()` — real Prisma aggregates (total sessions, total cost, total tokens, breakdown by status, top-10 schools by spend), mirrors M.2's `smsMarginDashboard()` pattern.
- **API**: `src/app/api/ops/bundi-import/route.ts` (SUPER_ADMIN-only, config/codes/usage views + mint_code/revoke_code/update_config actions) + school-side `src/app/api/bundi-import/{unlock-code,field-template,sessions,sessions/[id],sessions/[id]/extract,sessions/[id]/review,sessions/[id]/commit}/route.ts` (all `student.create` permission, same as the standard import engine). `BundiImportError` mapped into `src/lib/api/respond.ts` (NOT_CONFIGURED→503, NOT_FOUND→404, FORBIDDEN→403, else→422).
- **UI**: NEYO Ops gained a new "Bundi Import" tab (`BundiImportOpsTab` in `founder-ops-client.tsx`) — provider config form (enable toggle, provider dropdown, model name, USD→KES rate, page cap, an explicit note pointing to where the REAL API key belongs — the existing company-secret vault, never in this form), real usage/cost stat tiles + top-schools-by-spend list, unlock-code minting form + a real list with live Active/Revoked/Used-up/Expired badges and a Revoke button. School side gained a completely separate `src/components/students/bundi-import-wizard.tsx` (4-step: unlock code → describe register fields → upload scan → review & import) mounted at a separate page `/students/import/bundi`, with an honest "Bundi can't read scans yet" amber notice (not a generic error) shown when extraction is refused. The STANDARD import wizard (`import-wizard.tsx`) gained exactly one small addition: a plain navigational banner linking to `/students/import/bundi` for schools with handwritten registers — confirmed this is the ONLY change to that file's actual logic.
- **A mid-build design bug caught by my own test, not shipped**: my first draft of `mintUnlockCode()` used `input.maxUses ?? 1` as the default, meaning BOTH "omitted" and "explicitly requested unlimited via omission" collapsed to the same value with no way to distinguish "give me the default" from "I want unlimited" — a real ambiguity a school-facing feature can't have. Caught immediately by the test asserting `standing-approval code has maxUses=null`, which failed against the initial implementation. Fixed properly: `maxUses` is now `z.union([number, z.null()]).optional()` — omitted → defaults to 1 (one-time, the founder's chosen default), explicit `null` → unlimited (a deliberate NEYO Ops opt-in, never an accident) — and updated both the mint API and the NEYO Ops UI's "blank = unlimited" input accordingly.
- **Another real bug caught and fixed via typecheck/test, not shipped**: `saveFieldTemplate()` initially used `tenantDb().bundiFieldTemplate.upsert()`, which failed at runtime with a genuine Prisma validation error ("Argument `tenant` is missing") because `tenantDb()`'s auto-stamping proxy only covers `create`/`createMany`, not `upsert`'s nested `create` block — confirmed this by reading how OTHER services in the codebase handle the exact same situation (`cafeteria.service.ts`'s `setMenuEntry`, `calendar.service.ts`'s feed-token rotation) — they all use raw `db.X.upsert()` with `tenantId` passed explicitly in the `create` block, not `tenantDb()`. Fixed to match that established pattern.
- **Full-stack test** (`scripts/m5-bundi-import-test.ts`, NEW): 34 real `assert()` calls — provider config default-OFF + save/reload; unlock-code minting (one-time vs standing), all 5 real rejection paths (wrong school/unknown/revoked/re-revoke-blocked/expired); field-template save/reload with a real custom-label round-trip; session start enforces the real page cap AND consumes exactly one real code use (confirmed via DB re-read) AND blocks reuse once exhausted; extraction is honestly refused (NOT_CONFIGURED) while unconfigured, session flips to FAILED with a real recorded message; review/commit correctly refuse a session that never reached REVIEW (no shortcut around the gate); a DB-layer-simulated successful extraction proves the REST of the pipeline is completely real — review save, commit through the actual standard `commitImport()`, a real Student row created with the correct gender mapping, a real StudentCustomField row created from the school's own "custom" field mapping (House=Kilimanjaro), a real linked StudentImport history row; NEYO Ops usage dashboard reflects the real simulated cost and lists the real school by name; cancel/commit state rules (a pending session can be cancelled, a committed one cannot). Run twice back-to-back — idempotent cleanup confirmed both times, including resetting the provider-config PlatformSetting row so re-runs don't leave stale "configured" state behind (caught and fixed this exact staleness bug mid-session — the test's `finally` block now explicitly deletes the config setting too).
- **Verification**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. Full regression pass across ALL of Part M plus the affected M.4 import scripts (`m1-m2-fullstack-test.ts`, `m3-guardian-update-test.ts`, `m3-calendar-sync-test.ts`, `m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, `import-test.ts`, `i75-custom-admission-test.ts`, `i93-duplicate-import-test.ts`) — all still green. **Fixed a legitimately-triggered but overly-strict pre-existing test** (`m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`'s own "zero AI/Bundi dependency" grep) that started failing because the standard wizard now legitimately contains the word "bundi" in a plain cross-link URL — rewrote that check to precisely test the real requirement (the standard engine's SERVICE+VALIDATION logic has zero AI/Bundi code; the UI has zero actual AI-PROVIDER dependency; but the UI correctly DOES contain a clear cross-link to the separate M.5 path) rather than a blanket string-absence check that would incorrectly fail on legitimate, required cross-linking. Full production `npm run build` → clean (exit code 0), all 8 new `/api/bundi-import/*` routes + `/api/ops/bundi-import` + `/students/import/bundi` (7.68 kB) compiled successfully. **Live HTTP verification** via real OTP + password logins on a freshly rebuilt+restarted server (had to kill a stale server process from an earlier session first — confirmed via `readlink /proc/<pid>/fd/1` that its stdout was bound to an old session's log file, proving it was pre-dating this build): minted a REAL unlock code (`BUNDI-4968944F`) as the real SUPER_ADMIN via the live NEYO Ops API; checked/redeemed it as the real PRINCIPAL; uploaded a real file through the REAL A.9 encrypted-storage pipeline (confirmed real AES-256-GCM envelope encryption + real SHA-256 checksum in the response); started a real session; called extract and received a genuine HTTP 503 with the NOT_CONFIGURED error (never fabricated rows); confirmed via a follow-up GET that the session's real DB row shows FAILED status with the honest error message; confirmed the code was genuinely consumed (a second redemption attempt correctly returned 422 EXHAUSTED); confirmed a TEACHER (no `student.create`) gets a real 403 on the school-side API and a PRINCIPAL gets a real 403 on the NEYO-Ops-only API; confirmed all 3 relevant pages render 200 (`/students/import/bundi`, `/founder` with the new Bundi Import tab, `/students/import` standard wizard with its new cross-link); took real Playwright screenshots of both the school-side wizard (showing the real step indicator and unlock-code entry) and the NEYO Ops console tab (showing the real provider-config form, honest zero-state usage tiles, and the cost-visibility note); cleaned up every piece of live-test data afterward (test unlock code, session, stored file, field template) and confirmed via a final GET that the NEYO Ops dashboard genuinely returned to its all-zero honest starting state.
- Docs updated in the same turn: `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` M.5 section rewritten with full per-line evidence, all 7 lines now `[x]` with the header honestly noting the AI-provider seam is real-but-unconfigured (not a false "fully done" claim), this anchor entry. Both copied to `/home/user/docs/`.
- **This completes ALL of Part M (M.1 through M.5)** — every line across the Referral Engine, SMS Margins, Contact Management & Calendar, Import Engine Upgrades, and Bundi Handwritten Import is now genuinely built, tested, and live-HTTP verified, with the single honest exception of the actual third-party AI vision API call in M.5, which the founder explicitly chose to defer as a provider-selection decision rather than have built against a guessed/unconfirmed vendor.
