## 2026-07-02 — PART M.3 continued: native-mobile calendar sync built for real (closes out M.3 completely, all 3 lines now genuine full-stack)
- Continued directly from the earlier M.3 session (guardian-update fix + chat-UI fix) in the same day. Founder said "next m3" to keep going on the remaining open line. Environment was already warm from the earlier session (node_modules, swapfile, Playwright/Chromium all still present — no re-setup needed this time).
- **The gap, precisely**: audience targeting for calendar event invites was already real (built under A.17 — `createEventSchema.audience`, `inviteAudience()` sends real in-app+SMS invites). But "sync with native mobile calendars" was NOT real: `/api/calendar/ics` (read via the route file directly) only ever produced a one-shot authenticated download — open it once in a phone's Calendar app and it becomes a dead, stale copy forever. A genuine sync needs a STANDING SUBSCRIPTION: a stable URL a phone's Calendar app polls automatically on its own schedule (this is literally how `webcal://` links work on iOS/Android/Outlook — a widely-supported open standard, not a NEYO invention).
- **Built for real, DB → service → API → UI → test → live HTTP, no shortcuts**:
  - **DB**: new `CalendarFeedToken` model (migration `20260701213657_m3_calendar_feed_token`) — `id, tenantId, userId (unique), token (unique), createdAt, rotatedAt, lastPolledAt`. Deliberately documented as NOT registered in `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` (added an explicit comment to `tenant-tables.ts` explaining why) — the public feed route resolves a raw token with ZERO session/cookie, exactly like the pre-existing `OtpCode`/`MagicLink` pattern, so it must be queried via plain `db`, never `tenantDb()` (which requires an active tenant context that doesn't exist pre-auth).
  - **Service** (`calendar.service.ts`, extended): `newFeedToken()` (crypto.randomBytes(24) base64url, following the same pattern as `webhook.service.ts`'s signing secrets and `api-key.service.ts`'s tokens); `feedUrlForToken()` returns both a plain `https://.../api/calendar/feed/<token>.ics` URL and a `webcal://` variant (just a protocol swap — that's literally the spec, `webcal://` tells the OS "this is a subscribe link, poll it automatically" instead of "download this file once"); `getOrCreateCalendarFeedToken()` (idempotent — same token on repeat calls until explicitly rotated); `rotateCalendarFeedToken()` (upsert with a new token — the OLD token immediately stops resolving, so a leaked/lost link on an old phone can be killed without affecting other devices... well, ALL devices, since it's one token per user — documented tradeoff, acceptable for a school context); `revokeCalendarFeedToken()` (hard delete); `resolveCalendarFeedToken()` — the PUBLIC lookup used by the feed route itself, joins to the User to get `tenantId`/`role`, and fails closed (`return null`) if the user has been deactivated (`isActive: false`) — proven live in the test by actually deactivating a real user mid-test and confirming their token stopped resolving, then reactivating them.
  - **API**: new `GET/POST /api/calendar/feed` (authenticated, `calendar.view` permission — every signed-in role has this) for a user to fetch their own link / rotate it / revoke it. New PUBLIC `GET /api/calendar/feed/[token]/route.ts` (genuinely no `requirePermission()` call at all — this is the actual sync endpoint a Calendar app hits) that strips the `.ics` suffix from the URL param, resolves the token, and if valid streams REAL live `.ics` content built via the EXISTING `getOccurrences()` + `buildIcs()` functions (same code path as the old authenticated download, just re-scoped to the resolved user's own role instead of the logged-in session) with `Cache-Control: no-store` so it's never served stale from any intermediate cache — always the live calendar at fetch time.
  - **UI** (`calendar-view.tsx`): a new "Sync to phone" button next to the pre-existing "iCal" button, opening a modal (`SyncToPhoneButton` component) with: the real copyable `https://` link, an "Open in Calendar app" button using the real `webcal://` link, plain non-technical setup instructions for both iPhone (Settings → Calendar → Accounts → Add Subscribed Calendar) and Android/Google Calendar (Settings → Add calendar → From URL), a "New link" rotate button, and an honest live status line ("Not synced by a device yet." / "Last synced {real timestamp}") driven by the genuine `lastPolledAt` field — never a fake placeholder.
  - **Full-stack test** (`scripts/m3-calendar-sync-test.ts`, NEW): 16 real `assert()` calls — idempotent token creation; correct `https`/`webcal` URL shapes; the resolver returns the right tenant/user/role; rotation genuinely invalidates the old token (re-resolves to null) while the new one works; a garbage/unknown token resolves to null without crashing; a REAL deactivated user's token fails closed (actually flipped `isActive: false` on a real DB row mid-test, confirmed the block, then restored it); the important PRIVACY check — created a real TEACHER-audience-targeted event and confirmed it appears in that teacher's OWN live feed and the PRINCIPAL's feed (leadership sees everything) but is genuinely ABSENT from a PARENT-role feed, proving cross-role event leakage can't happen just because someone knows a URL pattern; confirmed the feed produces genuine RFC-5545 content (`BEGIN:VCALENDAR`/`BEGIN:VEVENT`/the real event's `SUMMARY`), not a stub string; revocation genuinely deletes the DB row and the token stops resolving. Ran twice back-to-back — idempotent cleanup confirmed both times. Re-ran the pre-existing `scripts/calendar-recurrence-test.ts` (14/14) to confirm zero regression to the existing recurring-events engine that the feed's occurrence-fetching shares code with.
  - **Live HTTP verification** (real OTP login, freshly rebuilt server): logged in as PRINCIPAL (Wanjiru Kamau) → `GET /api/calendar/feed` → 200, real freshly-generated `https://localhost:3000/api/calendar/feed/<token>.ics` + matching `webcal://` link; fetched that EXACT URL with a plain `curl` and ZERO cookies (deliberately simulating what a real Calendar app does — it never sends a NEYO session cookie) → 200, `Content-Type: text/calendar`, `Cache-Control: no-store`, and genuine iCalendar content containing real seeded data (Madaraka Day, Eid al-Adha, a real "Fees due reminder" event) — not a fixture or stub; confirmed `lastPolledAt` updated in the DB to the real timestamp of that unauthenticated curl request; called the rotate action for real → got a genuinely different token, and the OLD URL now returned a real HTTP 404; called revoke for real → the newest URL also then returned 404. Took real Playwright screenshots of the actual rendered UI (`screenshots/m3-calendar-sync-01-page.png` showing the new "Sync to phone" button on the live `/calendar` page, `m3-calendar-sync-02-modal.png` showing the real modal with a live-generated link, copy button, and "Not synced by a device yet" honest status).
- **Verification for the whole calendar-sync chunk**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors. `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/m3-calendar-sync-test.ts` → 16/16, run twice (idempotent). `scripts/calendar-recurrence-test.ts`, `scripts/guardians-test.ts`, `scripts/m3-guardian-update-test.ts` re-run as no-regression checks on the earlier M.3 work from the same day — all still green. This half of the checklist line was a genuine gap.

But genuine native-mobile CALENDAR SYNC is a real gap: `/api/calendar/ics` (confirmed by reading the route) only serves a one-shot downloadable `.ics` file behind a manual "Add to calendar" button in `calendar-view.tsx` — there is no subscribable `webcal://` feed URL that a phone's Calendar app would poll automatically to stay live-updated. Left this sub-line honestly unticked; not started this session (see Next Steps).
  - Line 3 ("chat UI message input hides behind cards while scrolling"): confirmed as a REAL bug via direct root-cause investigation (see below), not previously understood or fixed.
- **Line 1 built for real**: added `updateGuardianSchema` to `src/lib/validations/student.ts` (all fields optional — a partial edit, no `isPrimary`/`createLogin` toggle since those stay on the dedicated `set_primary` action). Added `updateGuardian(user, studentId, guardianId, input)` to `src/lib/services/student.service.ts`: row-scoped via the EXISTING `scopeWhere()` helper (the same fail-closed A.3.8 rule that already restricts TEACHER/CLASS_TEACHER to their own classes elsewhere in B.1) — confirms the target student is visible to the caller AND the target guardian is actually linked to that student before allowing any write; if the guardian has a linked PARENT portal login (`Guardian.userId`), that `User`'s phone/email/fullName are updated too in the SAME call so the login doesn't silently go stale/unreachable; writes a real `AuditLog` row with before/after snapshot; handles the empty-patch case as a safe no-op instead of throwing. Wired into `POST /api/students/:id/guardians` as a new `action: "update_guardian"` branch (alongside the existing default-add and `set_primary` branches) — `StudentError` was already mapped in `respond.ts` so no new error-mapping work was needed. UI: added an `EditGuardian` modal component to `student-profile-client.tsx` (mirrors the existing `AddGuardian` modal's visual style), with a small blue notice when the guardian has a linked portal login explaining the login will update too; mounted next to the existing "Set as Primary" button on every guardian card, gated by the same `canEdit` prop (`student.edit` permission — CLASS_TEACHER already has this).
- **Full-stack test**: `scripts/m3-guardian-update-test.ts` (NEW) — 12 real `assert()` calls: a real CLASS_TEACHER (Chebet Faith) editing a guardian on HER OWN class's student succeeds and the phone lands correctly normalized (+254...); the SAME class teacher is BLOCKED (fail-closed) editing a guardian on a DIFFERENT class's student, confirmed the blocked write did NOT change the DB; editing a guardian WITH a linked PARENT login also updates that `User`'s phone/email/name so they keep receiving OTP; an empty-patch no-op returns cleanly; editing a guardian not actually linked to the given student is rejected. Then confirmed the fail-closed rule live: same class teacher targeting a guardian on a DIFFERENT class's student (Wanjiru Njoroge, not in Chebet's class) → real HTTP 404 `{"code":"NOT_FOUND","message":"Student not found."}` — the row-scoping genuinely blocks it, not just in the unit test.
- **Line 3 (chat UI bug) — root-caused and fixed for real, this was the most involved piece**:
  - Reproduced with a NEW Playwright diagnostic script `scripts/shot-m3-chat-bug-diagnosis.ts` (full-page desktop 1920×1080 shots matching the project's existing `shot-j*` screenshot convention, PLUS a real mobile 390×844 viewport since that's almost certainly where the founder actually saw it — narrow screens have much less vertical headroom). First had to learn the real seeded conversations are ANNOUNCEMENT ("Closing Day", composer correctly hidden by design) and GROUP ("Form 2 Teachers", composer SHOULD show) — initially mis-tested against the ANNOUNCEMENT thread and wrongly concluded "no bug", caught the mistake and re-tested against the GROUP thread.
  - Root cause found via a deep DOM-geometry dump (walked every ancestor of the `<textarea>` composer, logging `getBoundingClientRect()` + `overflowY` + `position` for each): the whole message panel's height was a HARDCODED `className="grid h-[calc(100vh-12rem)] ..."` in `src/components/messaging/messages-client.tsx` — a guess that "12rem (192px) of stuff sits above this panel". That guess only roughly held on desktop. On a real mobile viewport with the topbar + breadcrumb bar + a dismissible "Coming soon: fees due reminder" banner + the "Messages" page heading/subtitle all stacked above it, the REAL space consumed was well over 192px, so the panel ended up taller than the space actually left below it. That forced the WHOLE PAGE (not just the internal message-list div) to become scrollable — confirmed via `document.documentElement.scrollHeight` (970px) exceeding `window.innerHeight` (844px) by 126px. Since the composer lives at the very bottom of that oversized panel, scrolling the page dragged the composer down with it, and it could end up rendering underneath the sticky topbar / floating "Install NEYO" card and other overlays — exactly matching "message input box hiding behind cards while scrolling".
  - Fixed properly (not a hack): the panel no longer guesses its height. It now measures its OWN real position on screen via `getBoundingClientRect().top` in a `useEffect`, and sizes itself with inline `style={{height}}` to exactly fill the remaining viewport (`window.innerHeight - top - bottomGutter`), so it self-adjusts correctly regardless of what banners/notices happen to be showing above it that day. Re-measures on `resize`, `orientationchange`, and once more ~300ms after mount (dismissible banners and webfonts can still shift layout slightly after first paint). Verified the fix numerically: the same mobile-viewport overflow measurement dropped from 126px (970 vs 844) to just 7px (851 vs 844) — the page is effectively no longer scrollable at all, so the composer never needs to move relative to the sticky chrome above it. Confirmed with before/after screenshots (`screenshots/m3-chat-bug-01` through `-06`) and confirmed AGAIN after a full fresh `npm install` + rebuild (in case the first measurement was a fluke of stale build artifacts) — same ~7px result both times.
  - Desktop appearance confirmed unchanged (screenshot `m3-chat-bug-02-thread-open.png`, 1920×1080): composer still renders fully visible inside the panel exactly as before, no visual regression.
- **Verification performed for the whole M.3 session**: `rm -f tsconfig.tsbuildinfo && tsc --noEmit` → 0 errors (run after both the guardian-update work and the chat-UI fix). `npm run test:roles` → 24/24. `scripts/guardians-test.ts` → 7/7 (no regression). `scripts/m3-guardian-update-test.ts` → 12/12, run twice (idempotent). `scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts` and `scripts/m1-m2-fullstack-test.ts` re-run as no-regression checks on unrelated M.4/M.1/M.2 work from earlier in the week — still green. Full production `npm run build` → clean (0 compile/type errors), `/students/[id]` route grew from 16.6 kB to 17.1 kB (the new EditGuardian modal), `/messages` unchanged at 12.2 kB. Live HTTP verification as documented above (real class-teacher login, real guardian edit, real fail-closed 404 block).

  - **DB**: `StudentCustomField` model (`id, tenantId, tenant, studentId, student, label, value, createdAt, updatedAt`, unique `[studentId, label]`, indexed `[tenantId, studentId]`, cascade-deletes with the student) + `StudentImport.targetClassId` (nullable String, stamped onto the import history row so admins can see later which imports were single-class-scoped). Both registered in `Tenant` relations AND `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` in `src/lib/core/tenant-tables.ts` — a real tenant-isolation requirement, not optional. Migration `20260701193356_m4_import_engine_upgrades` applied cleanly.
  - **Validation** (`src/lib/validations/student-import.ts`): added `"custom"` to the `IMPORT_FIELDS` union with an empty synonym list in `HEADER_SYNONYMS` (a school must always explicitly choose "custom" and type its own label — it is NEVER auto-guessed from header text, keeping the importer fully deterministic/non-AI). `columnMappingSchema` changed from a bare field-per-column list to `{column, field, customLabel?}` objects with a `.refine()` that requires `customLabel` whenever `field === "custom"`. `targetClassId` (optional string) added to both `importPreviewSchema` and `importCommitSchema`.
  - **Service** (`src/lib/services/student-import.service.ts`): `buildCandidates()` now splits mapped columns into normal single-value fields vs `customColumns` (any `field:"custom"` mapping with a label), collecting a `_customFields: {label,value}[]` array per row (added to the `PreviewRow` type) — kept completely separate from the free-text `notes` field so custom data is never silently dumped/merged. `previewImport()` gained an optional 5th param `targetClassId`: when set, it validates the class exists, SKIPS class resolution/auto-creation entirely (no `unknownClasses` scan), and returns `targetClass:{id,label}` in the response so the UI can show it. `commitImport()` gained `input.targetClassId`: when set, validates the class as `forcedClassId`, skips the entire class-auto-creation loop, and every student's `classId` is set to `forcedClassId` regardless of any className column value; also writes real `StudentCustomField` rows via `createMany()` per student after creation, and stamps `targetClassId` onto the `StudentImport` history row for audit visibility.
  - **API**: `src/app/api/students/import/preview/route.ts` — multipart branch reads `form.get("targetClassId")`, JSON branch already flows it through via the updated `importPreviewSchema`; both pass it as the 5th arg to `previewImport()`. The commit route (`src/app/api/students/import/route.ts`) needed ZERO changes — it already forwards the whole validated body (which now includes `targetClassId` via the updated `importCommitSchema`) straight to `commitImport()`.
  - **UI** (`src/components/students/import-wizard.tsx`, the real `/students/import` wizard used by registrars/bursars): Step 1 now opens with a real mode picker — "Use the Class column in my file" (default, unchanged behavior) vs "Put everyone in one class" (fetches real classes from `/api/classes`, shows a dropdown, disables the upload button and the paste button until a class is actually chosen). Step 2's column-mapping grid gained a "Custom field (school-defined)…" option per column; picking it reveals an inline text input for the label (onBlur re-previews with the label attached). The summary strip shows "All students → {class label}" instead of "N new classes will be created" when in single-class mode. The sample-rows table gains a real "Custom fields" column (only rendered when at least one mapping uses `custom`) showing `label: value` pairs per row; the Class column in the sample table shows the forced target class label when applicable instead of the (ignored) file value.
  - **Full-stack test** (`scripts/m4-import-upgrades-test.ts`, NEW): 14 real `assert()` calls, not prints — creates a real throwaway class; previews+commits a 2-row import with `targetClassId` set and a deliberately bogus/nonexistent Class column value ("Grade 9 Rainbow" / "Nonexistent Stream Z") to prove it's ignored; confirms both students land in the forced class in the real DB; confirms class count did NOT increase (no auto-creation); previews+commits a row with 2 `field:"custom"` mapped columns (House, Sponsor) and confirms exactly 2 real `StudentCustomField` DB rows exist with correct label/value, and that `notes` stayed `null` (no accidental merge); confirms the `StudentImport` history row is stamped with the real `targetClassId`; re-runs `i75-custom-admission-test.ts` and `i93-duplicate-import-test.ts` as sub-processes to prove zero regression; greps the 3 relevant source files for `openai|anthropic|gemini|gpt-|ai.service|bundi` and asserts zero matches (proves the importer stays fully rule-based/non-AI as the checklist itself requires). ## 2026-07-01 — PART M (M.1 Referral Engine + M.2 SMS Margins) rebuilt to true full-stack (same audit session, continued)
- Continued the same live-audit discipline from the earlier 2026-07-01 entry into Part K/L/M as the founder directed. Part K: ran all 6 regression scripts (k1-k2, k3-k5, k5-master-report, k6-k8, k10, k16) — genuinely solid, all pass. Part L: 10/11 scripts pass; found `l3-matcher-test.ts` asserted NOTHING (just printed "Assignments made: 0" and called it done) — tested the real `autoAssignTeachersToClasses()` service directly with a clean scenario and confirmed the FEATURE itself works correctly (assigns the right teacher, blocks when nobody teaches the subject, doesn't double-assign); the bug was in the test, not the feature. Rewrote `scripts/l3-matcher-test.ts` with real `assert()` calls proving all three behaviors.
- **Part M audit confirmed the checklist's own honesty note was accurate — M.1 and M.2 were NOT full-stack.** Verified directly: `referral.service.ts` only wrote an `AuditLog` row claiming a discount *should* apply (`applyDiscountToNextInvoice` never touched any real invoice/payment); ZERO API routes and ZERO UI existed anywhere for referrals (`grep` confirmed no `src/app/api` or `src/components/founder` references); and worse, the ONE place it was wired in (`patch_referral_hook.js` → `finance.service.ts applyPaymentToInvoice`) fired on a PARENT paying SCHOOL FEES (B.7), not on a SCHOOL paying its own NEYO subscription — completely the wrong trigger, matching neither the checklist's own M.1 spec nor common sense. M.2: `costPerSms`/`pricePerSms` were hardcoded literals in `src/lib/notifications/sms.ts`, only logged on the dev-console fallback (never the real Africa's Talking send path), with zero NEYO Ops configuration UI or dashboard.
- **Founder chose: build Part M fully now**, per Prompt 2 zero-shortcut full-stack rules. Built in full chunks:
  - **DB**: new `ReferralCredit` model (real ledger: role REFERRER/REFERRED, counterpart tenant+name, discountPct, `triggerPaymentId` unique idempotency key, status PENDING/APPLIED/EXPIRED, appliedToPaymentId/appliedAmountKes/appliedAt) + `SubscriptionPayment.referralDiscountKes` (the REAL KES amount deducted off a REAL NEYO subscription charge, not a school-fee invoice). Both `smsMarginLedger` and the new `referralCredit` added to `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` (neither was registered before — a real tenant-isolation gap). Migrations `20260701145642_m1_m2_full_stack` + `20260701150153_m1_subscription_payment_referral_discount`.
  - **Validation**: `src/lib/validations/revenue-ops.ts` — `referralRulesSchema` (enabled/discountPct capped 50%/rewardBothSides/minimumPaidTermsBeforeReward), `smsMarginConfigSchema` (cost/price/billingWindow MONTHLY|TERMLY|YEARLY, with a `superRefine` that BLOCKS NEYO Ops from ever configuring a sell price below cost — can't accidentally sell SMS at a loss), `referralActionSchema` discriminated union for the API.
  - **Service** (`src/lib/services/revenue-ops.service.ts`, ~400 lines): NEYO Ops config get/save for both rules (same `PlatformSetting` pattern as `pricing-catalog.service.ts`, keys `neyo_referral_rules` / `neyo_sms_margin_config`); `ensureReferralCode()` (idempotent, collision-retried); `applyReferralCode()` (self-refer blocked, double-apply blocked); `processReferralRewardsForPayment(paymentId)` — the real trigger, keyed to a `SubscriptionPayment.status === "PAID"` row, idempotent via the `triggerPaymentId` unique constraint, credits BOTH schools when `rewardBothSides` is on, marks `hasClaimedReferral` FIRST to prevent any double-credit race; `pendingReferralDiscountKes()` computes the real KES discount to shave off the NEXT subscription charge; `markReferralCreditsApplied()` confirms it once that discounted payment itself clears; `expireReferralCredit()` for NEYO Ops manual override (audited); `referralDashboard()` + `schoolReferralStatus()` real Prisma-aggregated views; `smsMarginDashboard()` + `markSmsLedgerInvoiced()` for M.2.
  - **Wired into the REAL billing flow** (`src/lib/services/central-billing.service.ts`, the live Daraja/M-Pesa STK path for NEYO's own subscription revenue — NOT the simpler seam in `billing.service.ts`): `initiateCentralSubscriptionStk()` now computes `pendingReferralDiscountKes()` before charging and sends the DISCOUNTED amount to the real M-Pesa STK push (not a cosmetic number); `activateSubscriptionFromPayment()` (fires from the real Daraja callback) now marks used credits APPLIED and calls `processReferralRewardsForPayment()` in a best-effort try/catch that can never block a real payment activation.
  - **Removed the wrongly-wired old hook**: deleted the `M.1 Trigger Referral Rewards on payment` block from `finance.service.ts applyPaymentToInvoice` (school-fee payment, wrong business entirely) — confirmed via `git diff` this was the ONLY change to that file this session, isolated cleanly from the fee/invoice logic.
  - **`sms.ts` rewritten**: `sendSms()` now reads `getSmsMarginConfig()` live instead of hardcoded 0.8/1.2, and records a real `SmsMarginLedger` row on BOTH the dev-console fallback path AND (newly) the real Africa's Talking send path — previously ONLY the dev fallback ever recorded margin, meaning production SMS sends were tracking ZERO revenue.
  - **API**: `src/app/api/ops/revenue/route.ts` (SUPER_ADMIN-only, GET dashboard/rules/config, POST update_referral_rules/update_sms_margin_config/expire_credit/mark_sms_ledger_invoiced) + `src/app/api/billing/referral/route.ts` (school-side, `owner.dashboard` permission, GET own referral status, POST apply a code) + `src/app/api/billing/public-stk/route.ts` extended to surface `fullAmount`/`referralDiscountKes` alongside the discounted `amount`. `RevenueOpsError` mapped into `src/lib/api/respond.ts`.
  - **UI**: NEYO Ops gained a new "Revenue Ops" tab (`RevenueOpsTab` in `founder-ops-client.tsx`) — referral master ON/OFF, reward-both-sides toggle, discount % + minimum-terms editor, live stat tiles (referred schools/pending/applied/expired), recent-credits list with manual Expire button; SMS cost/price/billing-window editor + live total-messages/total-margin tiles + top-schools-by-margin list. School side gained `src/components/settings/referral-card.tsx` mounted on `/settings/billing` — shows the school's own referral code with one-tap copy, an apply-a-code form (hidden once already referred), schools-referred count, and a real credits history list; the whole card hides itself if NEYO Ops has referrals turned off platform-wide.
  - **Full-stack proof**: new `scripts/m1-m2-fullstack-test.ts` (real `assert()` calls, not prints) — referral rules save/reload; code generation is idempotent; self-referral blocked; double-apply blocked; a PENDING subscription payment triggers NOTHING; a PAID one credits BOTH schools exactly once with the CENTRALLY-CONFIGURED discount %, never a hardcoded number; re-processing the same payment is a true no-op (checked via `triggerPaymentId` uniqueness AND a total-credit-count assertion); the pending credit correctly computes a real KES discount off a real charge amount; marking applied/expired really flips status; both dashboards show real aggregated data; SMS config rejects a loss-making price; a real `sendSms()` call creates exactly one real ledger row using the LIVE configured prices. Old dishonest `scripts/m1-m2-test.ts` (asserted nothing, only exercised M.2) replaced with a note + a delegate-through to the real test so nothing 404s.
  - **Verification**: fresh `npm install` needed (node_modules had been wiped by a sandbox reset mid-session — also had to redo `rm -rf node_modules/@prisma node_modules/.prisma && npm install && prisma generate` to fix a broken `PrismaClient` export, the exact documented gotcha from earlier sessions); `npx tsc --noEmit` with zero `.tsbuildinfo` cache → 0 errors; `npm run test:roles` → 24/24; `scripts/m1-m2-fullstack-test.ts` → all real assertions pass (run twice back-to-back to confirm idempotent cleanup); full production `npm run build` → clean, 0 compile/type errors (needed the same 4GB swapfile trick as the earlier audit — sandbox RAM resets are not persistent, redo `sudo fallocate -l 4G /swapfile && mkswap && swapon` each fresh session if a build OOMs); **live server test**: logged in for real via OTP as SUPER_ADMIN → `GET /api/ops/revenue` 200 with real config + real SMS margin totals from actual sends made during today's testing (8 messages, KES 3.20 margin); logged in for real as PRINCIPAL → `GET /api/billing/referral` 200 with a genuinely freshly-generated code `NEYO-ADDC08`; confirmed a TEACHER gets 403 on the school referral endpoint and the PRINCIPAL gets 403 on the NEYO Ops endpoint (role boundaries correctly enforced).

## 2026-07-01 — REPO-WIDE AUDIT: found + fixed a build-cache bug that was hiding 224 real TypeScript errors (new chat, fresh GitHub clone)
- Founder cloned the repo into a NEW CHAT (transferred via GitHub: `https://github.com/jabaliszn/neyoos`) and asked for a full audit because he doubted recent work (Part J onward) was truly full-stack. Per Prompt 2, this meant actually running the project end-to-end, not trusting the checklist's prose.
- **ROOT CAUSE FOUND**: the repo had `.tsbuildinfo` files (TypeScript's incremental compile cache) COMMITTED TO GIT (`tsconfig.tsbuildinfo` + 5 `tsconfig.*check*.tsbuildinfo` variants). Because `tsconfig.json` has `"incremental": true`, every `npm run typecheck` run against a fresh clone was SILENTLY SKIPPING re-checks of most files and reporting 0 errors even when hundreds existed. **This means every prior "typecheck clean ✅" claim in this file for weeks of work was not trustworthy.**
- Deleted all 6 `.tsbuildinfo` files, added `*.tsbuildinfo` to `.gitignore` so this can never happen again.
- Re-ran a genuinely clean `tsc --noEmit`: **224 real errors surfaced across 33 files.** Fixed every one, verified down to a clean 0 after each batch. Full forensic writeup: `docs/I60B-TYPECHECK-CACHE-AUDIT-2026-07-01.md`.
- **Also found (only by actually running the project, not by typecheck):**
  1. A byte-identical DUPLICATE Prisma migration (`20260630164219` and `20260630164229_exam_timetable_invigilators`, 10 seconds apart) — broke `prisma migrate deploy` outright on a fresh clone. Removed the duplicate.
  2. SCHEMA/MIGRATION DRIFT: `Curriculum.adoptedTemplateId/Version`, `AssessmentType.effectiveFrom/effectiveTo`, `GlobalCurriculumTemplate.publishedAt/changeNote/announcedAt` existed in `schema.prisma` with NO migration ever written for them (likely applied via `prisma db push` directly to the old session's dev DB during J.20/J.21 and never captured) — broke seeding (`P2022`) on fresh clone. Fixed with new migration `20260701125337_j20_j21_schema_drift_fix`.
  3. `src/app/api/academics/exams/print-roster/route.ts` called `tenantDb()` WITHOUT wrapping in `withTenant()` — threw "No tenant in scope" on every real request. Not caught by typecheck OR build — only found by curling the route as a logged-in principal. Fixed + re-verified live (200, real computed averages: Achieng 85%, Kamau 59%, Atieno 47%). Same route also had a real Prisma relation bug (`ExamResult` has no `student` relation, only `studentId`) — fixed with a proper separate join.
- **Biggest single bug**: `src/components/academics/academics-client.tsx` had 143 of the 224 errors. Root cause: a bad automated patch had copy-pasted the "Draft resume protection" UI card + its localStorage draft-save effects (which legitimately belong ONLY to the Smart Timetable / `TimetableEngineTab` screen) into 6 unrelated functions (`SubjectsTab`, `TermsTab`, `TimetableTab`, `ObservationDialog`, `DutyRosterTab`, `TimetableGeneratorTab`) that had none of the required state — broke the production build. FIXED BY: removing the 5 broken stray copies, restoring the ONE real copy to `TimetableEngineTab` (verified nothing real was lost — screenshotted/explained to founder mid-session since he asked directly "are you deleting files?"). ALSO deleted a 450-line DEAD/unused `OldCoCurricularTab` function (confirmed via grep that nothing calls it; the real active `CoCurricularTab` is a 3-line wrapper around `TalentManagerClient` right above it).
- Remaining 81 errors were genuine smaller bugs across ~30 files: `<Badge variant=.../>` and `<Button variant="default"|size="icon">` misuse (component APIs only support `tone` on Badge and `primary|secondary|ghost|danger` / `sm|md|lg` on Button) in pathway-manager/student-pathway-tab/subject-selection-manager/talent-manager/promotion-client/students-client/student-service-tab/parent-pathway-card/learner-journey-components; `EmptyState action={{label,onClick}}` misuse (needs `primaryAction`) in 3 files; null-unsafe `s.subject.name` on the genuinely-optional `TimetableSlot.subject` relation across 5 service/route files (activity/PE slots have no subject); missing `tenantId`/`actorName` on 6 raw `AuditLog.create`/`ActivityCategory.create` calls (tenantDb() stamps tenantId at runtime but TS still needs it in the literal for these two models); `fail()` called without required `status` arg; a wrong-field-path bug (`pack.export.generatedAt` should be `pack.manifest.generatedAt` — would have produced `undefined` dates in real PDFs); a genuinely UNIMPLEMENTED `exportJourney` button handler in `learner-journey-card.tsx` that was wired to a function that didn't exist anywhere (built the real implementation — calls `/api/learner-journey/export`, downloads the file); a `useIdea(...)` helper function name that tripped React's hooks-lint rule and broke the build (renamed to `applyIdea`); a `Set<string>` type-inference gap; missing `pinned/pinVisibility/pinNote` fields in the `learnerJourneyEntrySchema` Zod type (service was legitimately returning them at runtime, type just hadn't caught up); and several test/seed scripts with real bugs (`User.name` should be `User.fullName`, incomplete `SessionUser` mocks, wrong argument shapes).
- **Full verification performed (not just "it compiles")**: fresh `npm install` + `prisma migrate deploy` (171→172 migrations, all clean) + `npm run db:seed` (idempotent, re-run confirmed) + `npx tsc --noEmit` with zero cache → **0 errors** (was 224) + `npm run test:roles` → 24/24 (unchanged) + re-ran `j15-report-builder-fullstack-test`, `j8-chunk8-seed`, `j8-learning-journey-export-test`, `j8-learning-journey-pins-service-test`, `j8-learning-journey-service-test`, `timetable-solver-test`, `l7-timetable-engine-test` (15/15), `l7-auto-grouping-test` (8/8), `j10-pathways-fullstack-test`, `j11-talent-fullstack-test`, `l4-subject-selection-test` — ALL GREEN + full production `npm run build` clean (0 compile/type errors; only expected informational "Dynamic server usage: used cookies" log lines for auth'd API routes, not errors) + **live server test**: built app started with `npm start`, logged in for REAL via OTP as principal@karibuhigh.ac.ke, hit real HTTP 200s on `/students/promotion`, `/settings/rubrics`, `/academics`, `/dashboard`, and confirmed the print-roster fix live (500→200 with real data).
- Sandbox note: this environment only has 1.9GB RAM (tighter than earlier sessions) — added a 4GB swapfile (`sudo fallocate -l 4G /swapfile && mkswap && swapon`) and used `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=3072` for `npm run build` to avoid OOM-kills during Next's internal lint+typecheck pass. This is sandbox-only; not a code change.
- **Answer to founder's original question**: yes, real gaps existed between "checklist says done" and "truly full-stack and working" — not deliberate faking, but (a) a tooling footgun (committed build cache hid real errors for weeks), (b) one bad automated patch that corrupted a large file with copy-paste errors, (c) ordinary integration bugs (missing `withTenant`, wrong field paths, UI prop mismatches, one genuinely-unimplemented button) that only surface when the app is actually run and clicked through, not just typechecked from a checklist description. ALL of the above are now fixed and verified LIVE, not just typechecked. `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` updated in the same turn (see Foundation Setup section note).
- **NEXT STEP (founder to direct)**: continue the same live-audit discipline into Part K/L/M and manually exercise more authenticated screens per role (teacher/parent/bursar) to build the same confidence there. Do not assume any remaining checklist `[x]` is proven until it has been run, not just read.

## 🔁 PART J BATCH 48 — J.8 LEARNING JOURNEY TIMELINE CHUNK 3 BACKEND AGGREGATION SERVICE COMPLETED (2026-06-28)
- Completed J.8 Chunk 3 — Backend Aggregation Service. Added `src/lib/services/learner-journey.service.ts`.
- The new service builds a unified learner journey **without** creating a duplicate timeline table. It reads and normalizes existing source modules into one ordered entry shape already defined by J.8 validation:
  - B.5 Exams (`ExamResult`) → grouped exam-result milestones
  - J.3 Flexible Assessments (`AssessmentRecord`) → released/internal assessment milestones
  - B.3 Attendance (`AttendanceRecord`) → important attendance events (absent / late / excused)
  - B.20 Discipline (`DisciplineIncident`, `Suspension`) → behavior/suspension milestones
  - J.4 Competency Evidence (`CompetencyEvidence`) → competency growth milestones
  - J.6 Skills Passport (`SkillsPassportEntry`) → talent/leadership growth milestones
  - J.7 Portfolio (`PortfolioItem`) → portfolio milestones
  - J.7 portfolio certificates (`PortfolioItem.category = CERTIFICATE`) → certificate milestones
  - B.1 transfer history (`StudentTransfer`) → system milestones
- Added `LearnerJourneyError` and `getLearnerJourneyTimeline(user, query)`.
- Service behavior:
  - verifies row-scoped learner access using existing `scopeWhere()`
  - enforces J.8 access mode rules (`staff` vs `parent`)
  - supports `from`, `to`, `source`, and `limit`
  - returns normalized entries sorted newest-first plus source counts/summary
  - keeps parent mode strictly `PARENT_SAFE`
  - intentionally excludes confidential `CounselingNote` content from the timeline
  - separates `PORTFOLIO` and `CERTIFICATE` source filtering while still reusing the same underlying portfolio table
- Added `scripts/j8-learning-journey-service-test.ts`, verifying:
  - accountant forbidden access
  - parent blocked from `staff` mode
  - real aggregation across EXAM / ASSESSMENT / ATTENDANCE / DISCIPLINE / COMPETENCY / SKILLS / PORTFOLIO / CERTIFICATE
  - parent-safe filtering of unpublished exams, internal assessments, internal competencies, hidden portfolio items, and counseling content
  - certificate-only source filter
  - date filtering and limit behavior
- Verification: `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=1536 npm run typecheck` ✓, `scripts/j8-learning-journey-service-test.ts` ✓, `scripts/j8-learning-journey-validation-test.ts` ✓, `npm run test:roles` 24/24 ✓.
- No screenshot because this was a backend service chunk only.
- NEXT = J.8 Chunk 4 — API route for learner journey timeline, then J.8 Chunk 5 reusable UI timeline components.

## 🔁 PART J BATCH 47 — J.8 LEARNING JOURNEY TIMELINE CHUNK 2 VALIDATION & SECURITY COMPLETED (2026-06-28)
- Completed J.8 Chunk 2 — Security & Validation. Added `src/lib/validations/learner-journey.ts`.
- The new validation layer defines strict schemas for the future timeline query and normalized timeline-entry shape:
  - `learnerJourneyQuerySchema` with `studentId`, `mode` (`staff` | `parent`), optional `from`/`to`, optional `source`, and bounded `limit`.
  - `learnerJourneyEntrySchema` with normalized fields such as `date`, `sourceModule`, `eventType`, `title`, `summary`, `visibility`, and `verificationStatus`.
- Added source/mode registries for the aggregation layer: timeline sources include `EXAM`, `ASSESSMENT`, `ATTENDANCE`, `DISCIPLINE`, `COMPETENCY`, `SKILLS`, `PORTFOLIO`, `CERTIFICATE`, and `SYSTEM`.
- Added 16-role access helpers:
  - `userCanReadLearnerJourney()`
  - `userCanReadStaffLearnerJourney()`
  - `userCanReadParentSafeLearnerJourney()`
  - `userCanAccessLearnerJourneyMode()`
  - `learnerJourneyAccessMatrix()`
- Important J.8 privacy rule is now encoded in access semantics: `PARENT` and `STUDENT` may access only `parent` mode, while staff-like roles with learner visibility may access `staff` mode. This sets up later filtering so confidential records (especially counseling notes) never leak into family timelines.
- Added `scripts/j8-learning-journey-validation-test.ts`, verifying valid query parsing/defaults, invalid date-window rejection, invalid source rejection, normalized entry parsing, 16-role access spot checks, secondary-role inheritance, mode guard behavior, and source-registry coverage.
- Verification: `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=1536 npm run typecheck` ✓, `scripts/j8-learning-journey-validation-test.ts` ✓, `npm run test:roles` 24/24 ✓.
- No screenshot because this was validation/security only.
- NEXT = J.8 Chunk 3 — Backend aggregation service (`learner-journey.service.ts`) that reuses Exams, Flexible Assessments, Attendance, Discipline, Competency Evidence, Skills Passport and Portfolio without creating a duplicate DB table.

## 🔁 PART J BATCH 46 — J.8 LEARNING JOURNEY TIMELINE AUDIT COMPLETED (2026-06-28)
- Started J.8 with the required non-duplication audit before building. Added `docs/J8-LEARNING-JOURNEY-TIMELINE-AUDIT.md`.
- Audited existing source modules that can already feed a learner timeline: `ExamResult` / `exam.service.ts` (B.5), `AssessmentRecord` / `assessment.service.ts` (J.3), `AttendanceRecord` / `attendance.service.ts` (B.3), `DisciplineIncident` + `Suspension` + confidential `CounselingNote` / `discipline.service.ts` (B.20), `CompetencyEvidence` (J.4), `SkillsPassportEntry` (J.6), and `PortfolioItem` / `portfolio.service.ts` (J.7).
- Audited learner-facing surfaces: `src/components/students/student-profile-client.tsx` and `src/components/portal/parent-portal-client.tsx` already carry many learner-growth sections (results, attendance, competencies, skills passport, portfolio links, etc.), so J.8 should extend these instead of creating a disconnected duplicate learner detail module.
- Key finding: J.8 should begin as a **read-only aggregation layer**, not a new database subsystem. There is currently no unified learner-timeline service, but the source records already exist. The safest next implementation is a service such as `learner-journey.service.ts` that normalizes events from the mature modules.
- Privacy finding: `CounselingNote` must NOT be exposed directly in a parent-safe timeline. J.8 needs audience-aware filtering (`staff` vs `parent`) when it aggregates discipline / wellbeing records.
- Gap finding: awards/clubs/community-service are only partially represented today. `PortfolioItem` and `SkillsPassportEntry` can provide early signals, but deeper club/award/community-service history should later connect with J.11 Talent Tracking and J.17 Community Service instead of being duplicated now.
- Updated `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` with a J.8 audit note and refreshed J.25 audit discipline note.
- No screenshot because this was an audit-only chunk.
- NEXT = J.8 Chunk 2/3: start the actual read-only learner journey aggregation layer (validation + service) over existing sources, still without introducing a duplicate timeline database table.

## 🔁 PART J BATCH 39 — J.7 STUDENT PORTFOLIO SYSTEM CHUNK 3 BACKEND SERVICE COMPLETED (2026-06-27)
- Completed J.7 Chunk 3 — Backend Logic / Service. Added `src/lib/services/portfolio.service.ts` with real Prisma-backed functions: `getPortfolioTimeline()`, `submitPortfolioItem()`, `updatePortfolioItem()`, `approvePortfolioItem()`, `rejectPortfolioItem()`, `deletePortfolioItem()`, and `exportPortfolioPack()`.
- Enforced encrypted Storage Vault path: `submitPortfolioItem()` verifies that `storedFileId` corresponds to a real `StoredFile` row with `encrypted = true`, throwing `PortfolioError` if unencrypted or missing.
- Media size controls and storage warnings: `getPortfolioTimeline()` calculates total portfolio storage usage, checks `MAX_PORTFOLIO_FILE_SIZE_BYTES` (50 MB cap), and sets `storageWarningExceeded` if usage exceeds `STORAGE_WARNING_THRESHOLD_BYTES` (10 MB).
- Student self-submission and teacher approval workflow: `STUDENT` submissions are forced to `SUBMITTED` status and hidden from parents until an authorized teacher or leader (`exam.publish` / `academics.manage`) approves them.
- Audit logs added for real changes: `portfolio.item_submitted`, `portfolio.item_updated`, `portfolio.item_approved`, `portfolio.item_rejected`, `portfolio.item_deleted`, and `portfolio.pack_exported`.
- Added `scripts/j7-student-portfolio-service-test.ts`, verifying student self-submission, unapproved item parent hiding, principal approval, parent visibility, encrypted Storage Vault check, 12 MB storage warning flag, rejection, export pack generation, accountant forbidden access, parent row-scoping block, and audit log creation.

## 🔁 PART J BATCH 19 — J.4 COMPETENCY FRAMEWORK CHUNK 2 SECURITY & VALIDATION COMPLETED (2026-06-26)
- Completed J.4 Chunk 2 — Security & Validation. Added `src/lib/validations/competency.ts` with strict Zod schemas and TS types for `CompetencyGroup`, `Competency`, `CompetencyEvidence`, evidence approval, and discriminated `competencyActionSchema`.
- Validation rules include safe names, uppercase code normalization, optional Curriculum/LearningArea linkage, source modules (`CBC`, `ASSESSMENT`, `LMS`, `MANUAL`, `CLUB`, `PORTFOLIO`), evidence requiring level/score/narrative, YYYY-MM-DD evidence dates, source consistency checks (`assessmentRecordId` requires source `ASSESSMENT`; `cbcAssessmentId` requires source `CBC`), and strict unknown-field rejection.
- Security helpers cover all 16 roles: read = `academics.view`, `exam.view` or `student.view`; manage = `academics.manage` or `tenant.manage_settings`; record evidence = `exam.enter_marks`, `homework.assign` or `academics.manage`; approve parent-visible evidence = `exam.publish` only. Secondary roles are honored. HOD can manage/record but cannot approve evidence for parent visibility unless they have a secondary release role.
- Added `scripts/j4-competency-validation-test.ts`, verifying schema success/failure cases, action validation, source consistency, approval visibility, all-role access matrix, and secondary-role access.
- Verification: `./node_modules/.bin/tsx scripts/j4-competency-validation-test.ts` ✓, `./node_modules/.bin/tsx scripts/j4-competency-schema-test.ts` ✓, `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=1536 npm run typecheck` ✓, `npm run test:roles` 24/24 ✓. ## 🔁 PART J BATCH 18 — J.4 COMPETENCY FRAMEWORK CHUNK 1 DATABASE FOUNDATION STARTED (2026-06-26)
- Completed J.4 Chunk 1 — Database Foundation. Added tenant-owned competency framework models in `prisma/schema.prisma`: `CompetencyGroup`, `Competency`, and `CompetencyEvidence`. These create a configurable competency layer without forcing everything into B.6 CBC-only tables.
- `CompetencyGroup` stores curriculum-linked groups such as “Core Competencies” with code, description, sequence and active status. `Competency` stores individual competencies such as Communication or Critical Thinking, with optional groupId, curriculumId and learningAreaId scalar links.
- `CompetencyEvidence` stores learner evidence over time, with competencyId, studentId, sourceModule/sourceId, optional `assessmentRecordId` for J.3 flexible assessments, optional `cbcAssessmentId` for B.6 CBC observations, level, scorePct, narrative, evidenceDate, recordedBy, approved and visibleToParents fields.
- Added `competencyGroup`, `competency`, and `competencyEvidence` to `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` so tenant isolation applies. Migration created/applied non-interactively at `prisma/migrations/20260626173000_j4_competency_framework_foundation/migration.sql`, then marked applied; `prisma migrate status` reports DB up to date.
- Added `scripts/j4-competency-schema-test.ts`, verifying real DB creation of competency group/competency/evidence, links to Curriculum/LearningArea, optional links to J.3 AssessmentRecord and B.6 CbcAssessment, tenantDb scoping and relations, then cleanup.
- Verification: `./node_modules/.bin/tsx scripts/j4-competency-schema-test.ts` ✓, `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=1536 npm run typecheck` ✓, `npm run test:roles` 24/24 ✓. No screenshot because this chunk is database-only. NEXT = J.4 Chunk 2 Security & Validation.

## 🔁 PART J BATCH 17 — J.4 COMPETENCY FRAMEWORK AUDIT COMPLETED; READY FOR CHUNK 1 (2026-06-26)
- Started J.4 with the required non-duplication audit. Added `docs/J4-COMPETENCY-FRAMEWORK-AUDIT.md`.
- Audited J.2 Curriculum Engine: `Curriculum`, `EducationLevel`, `GradeBand`, and `LearningArea` already exist and should be the configurable foundation for competencies. J.4 competencies should link to `Curriculum` and optionally `LearningArea`, not hardcode CBC only.
- Audited B.6 CBC: `CbcStrand`, `CbcAssessment`, and `studentCompetencies()` already provide CBC-style strand observations. J.4 should reuse CBC observations as evidence sources but create a general configurable competency framework.
- Audited J.3 Flexible Assessment Engine: `AssessmentRecord` can become a source of competency evidence later; J.4 should not wait for J.3 final seed completion.
- Audited Student Profile and Parent Portal: no general competency summary/heatmap exists yet. J.4 should start with database foundation, then service/API, then student/parent UI later.
- Proposed J.4 foundation models: `CompetencyGroup`, `Competency`, and `CompetencyEvidence`, all tenant-owned and connected to Curriculum/LearningArea/Student plus source modules (CBC, ASSESSMENT, LMS, MANUAL, CLUB, PORTFOLIO).
- Checklist updated with J.4 audit note. NEXT = **J.4 Chunk 1 — Database foundation**.

## 🔁 PART J BATCH 10 — J.3 FLEXIBLE ASSESSMENT ENGINE CHUNK 1 DATABASE FOUNDATION STARTED (2026-06-26)
- Completed J.3 Chunk 1 — Database Foundation. Added tenant-owned flexible assessment models in `prisma/schema.prisma`: `AssessmentType`, `AssessmentPlan`, `AssessmentRecord`, and `AssessmentEvidence`. These sit beside existing B.5 Exams, B.6 CBC and B.13 LMS instead of replacing them.
- `AssessmentType` stores configurable assessment categories and scoring modes for exam, CAT, project, practical, oral, observation, portfolio, peer/self and continuous assessment use cases (`key`, `name`, `category`, `scoreMode`, default marks/weight, evidence/moderation flags).
- `AssessmentPlan` links to `AssessmentType` and stores optional compatibility IDs for J.2 Curriculum/EducationLevel/GradeBand/LearningArea plus existing Subject/Class/AcademicTerm and future bridges to Exam/Homework/Quiz/CBC strand. It stores title, instructions, year/term, weight, maxMarks, dueDate, rubricJson, status and parent visibility.
- `AssessmentRecord` stores one learner's result/observation for a plan with marks, percentage, rubric level/code, narrative, sourceModule/sourceId, status, assessor, moderation and release timestamps. `AssessmentEvidence` stores evidence file references (`storedFileId`, fileUrl/fileName/contentType/evidenceType/note) and is ready for later encrypted Storage Vault upload wiring.
- Added all four new models to `TENANT_OWNED_MODELS` so tenant isolation applies. Migration created non-interactively via Prisma diff and stored at `prisma/migrations/20260626162000_j3_flexible_assessment_foundation/migration.sql`; applied with `prisma db execute`; then marked applied with `prisma migrate resolve --applied ...`. `prisma migrate status` reports database schema is up to date.
- Added `scripts/j3-assessment-schema-test.ts`, which creates real AssessmentType/Plan/Record/Evidence rows, verifies plan/type/record/evidence relationships, confirms optional Curriculum/LearningArea/Subject/Class/Term links work, verifies tenantDb scoping, and cleans up.
- Verification: `./node_modules/.bin/tsx scripts/j3-assessment-schema-test.ts` ✓, `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=1536 npm run typecheck` ✓, `npm run test:roles` 24/24 ✓, `./node_modules/.bin/prisma migrate status` ✓. - Audited B.5 Exams: `Exam`, `ExamSubject`, `ExamResult`, release approvals, marks entry, report cards and I.60 analytics. Existing exams/CATs are full-stack and should remain the formal-exam path; J.3 must not replace them.
- Audited B.6 CBC: `CbcStrand` and append-only `CbcAssessment` already handle 4-level formative observations and parent-friendly CBC reports. J.3 should reuse the append-only evidence philosophy but not force projects/practicals/portfolio assessments into CBC-only tables.
- Audited B.13 LMS: homework submissions and quiz attempts already support graded work and file uploads, but they are not a unified assessment ledger. J.3 should later reference LMS outcomes/evidence rather than duplicate homework/quiz systems.
- Audited Storage Vault: evidence files for J.3 must use existing encrypted upload path (`FileUpload` → `/api/files/encrypted`) and `StoredFile` encrypted metadata.
- J.3 implementation decision recorded: add a compatible flexible assessment layer (AssessmentType, AssessmentPlan, AssessmentRecord, AssessmentEvidence and release/moderation workflow) linked to J.2 Curriculum/LearningArea/GradeBand plus existing Subject/Class/Term/Student, while keeping Exams/CBC/LMS intact.
- Checklist updated: J.3 now has the audit note and “Extend existing Exam / ExamResult...” is `[~]` with audit evidence. NEXT = J.3 Chunk 1 — Database foundation for the flexible assessment layer.

- Migration assistant behavior: creates or matches `CBC Kenya` and `8-4-4 Legacy` curricula for the active seed year; creates education levels from class levels (e.g. Forms, Junior School), grade bands from existing class levels (e.g. Form 1/Form 2), and learning areas from existing subjects; maps existing Subjects → Curriculum/LearningArea, Classes → Curriculum/GradeBand, Terms → main Curriculum, CBC strands → LearningArea.
- Assistant is idempotent and audit-logged (`curriculum.migration_assistant_run`). It is exposed through `/api/curriculum` action `run_migration_assistant` and surfaced on `/settings/curriculum` in the mapping modal as “Run migration assistant.”
- Updated `prisma/seed.ts` so a fresh `npm run db:seed` automatically runs the J.2 assistant after B.4/B.6 seed data exists. Verified seed output: `✓ Seeded J.2: Curriculum Engine migration assistant mapped 11 subjects, 2 classes, 3 terms and 3 strands.`

- Added tenant-aware school-name prefixing for WhatsApp: callers can pass `{ tenantId }`; the transport prefixes the correct school name unless already prefixed or disabled with `{ prefix:false }`. Notification cascade now passes `tenantId` into WhatsApp transport.
- Added `whatsapp_phone_number_id` and `whatsapp_api_version` to the Integration Credential Vault.

## 🔁 PART I BATCH 113 — I.56 STORAGE VAULT ENCRYPTED UPLOAD ADAPTER COMPLETED (2026-06-25)
- Built Storage Vault Batch 2: encrypted upload adapter.

Processed image uploads now go through encrypted upload.
- API: added `/api/files/encrypted` for multipart server-side encrypted uploads. Direct presigned browser uploads remain legacy/non-encrypted until a future migration to server-side encrypted upload or client-side encryption.

## 🔁 PART I BATCH 111 — STORAGE STRATEGY FOUNDER CORRECTION RECORDED (2026-06-24)
- Founder clarified the desired storage model: NEYO should provision a fresh Google storage account per school, start with the included storage where available, then upgrade/pay when full from inside NEYO.
- Updated `docs/NEYO-STORAGE-STRATEGY.md` with a safer compliant version: use managed Google Workspace accounts or school-owned Workspace BYOS, not mass-created consumer Gmail accounts. Example: `karibu-high.storage@storage.neyo.co.ke`.
- Added password/security rule: NEYO should not store plaintext Google passwords in normal app storage. Prefer service-account/domain-wide delegation or encrypted OAuth/service credentials in a vault; any break-glass credential must be sealed, encrypted, rotated and SUPER_ADMIN-only.

## 🔁 PART I BATCH 110 — I.56 STORAGE STRATEGY / GOOGLE BYOS DESIGN ANSWER COMPLETED (2026-06-24)
- Founder proposed using Google BYOS/free Drive storage per school plus WhatsApp-style device storage to reduce NEYO storage costs.
- Researched the idea and documented the safe design in `docs/NEYO-STORAGE-STRATEGY.md`. Key conclusion: the concept is useful, but NEYO should not rely on mass-created free consumer Gmail accounts as the primary backend. Safer design is a storage abstraction with NEYO-managed encrypted object storage as default, optional Google Workspace/BYOS connector, usage bars, quota checks, paid storage add-ons and legal consent.
- Strategy covers: Google BYOS reality check, `StorageProvider` abstraction, AES-256-GCM envelope encryption, encrypted blobs in provider storage, metadata/key wrapping in NEYO, deletion/corruption protection, quota thresholds, upgrade flows, WhatsApp-style local/device media retention, live class no-recording default, Google account disabled/deleted handling, and Kenya Data Protection Act considerations.
- Updated `docs/FEATURES-CHECKLIST.md` and ticked the I.56 storage strategy/answer line. NEXT = either build the Storage Settings MVP later, or continue with I.56 scale architecture hardening line.

Grace ending within 3 days sends a one-time warning `billing.grace_warning_sent`. - Customer communication: grace notices create in-app notices for active School Owner/Principal users and SMS the tenant phone where available. Data is never deleted; suspended schools remain locked by the existing root-layout subscription gate and reconnect after payment.

- Validation/security: `pricingCatalogSchema` validates package keys, prices, student/staff limits, included modules, add-ons and duplicate keys. It enforces the founder rule that SMS is NOT included in packages (`limits.smsPerTerm` must stay 0 and package highlights cannot include SMS). Saving is SUPER_ADMIN-only through Founder Ops and audit-logs `platform.pricing_catalog_updated`.
- Billing integration: `ensureSubscription()` and `subscribeToPlan()` now read prices through `getPlanFromCatalog()`. New/changed subscriptions lock the current dynamic price into `Subscription.grandfatheredPrice`; saving global pricing does NOT rewrite existing locked prices.
- Usage integration: `limits.service.ts` now treats SMS quota as out-of-package: base packages give 0 SMS, while active SMS add-ons in `Subscription.addOns` grant quota (e.g. `sms_topup_1000` gives 1,000).
- UI: Founder Ops → Business Operations now has “Pricing & Package Editor — no code touch” for plan price, student/staff limits, per-student price, max add-ons, support promise, included modules, package inclusions/highlights, and out-of-package add-on prices. SMS bundles are shown separately and package SMS is locked to 0.
- Billing pages/API: `/api/billing`, `/api/billing/subscribe`, and Settings → Billing now read dynamic plans; Settings copy clarifies that SMS is bought as a separate top-up outside packages.
- Test added: `scripts/i48-pricing-catalog-test.ts` verifies Founder Ops API/UI source, dynamic catalog persistence, grandfathering, new subscription price locking, SMS top-up quota, and validation rejecting SMS inside packages.

Important honesty note: YouTube can still enforce its own adverts inside an embed; true zero-ad classroom playback requires school-owned uploaded video storage or YouTube-side ad-free/education entitlement when available.

## 🔁 PART I BATCH 65D — I.9 CLASS-GROUP DISAPPEARING VOICE CHUNK 3 COMPLETED (2026-06-22)
- Continued I.9 class-group disappearing voice. Completed Chunk 3 — Backend Logic / Service.
- Added `src/lib/services/class-voice.service.ts` with real Prisma-backed functions: `startClassVoiceRoom`, `joinClassVoiceRoom`, `postClassVoiceSignal`, `pollClassVoiceSignals`, `endClassVoiceRoom`, and `cleanupExpiredClassVoiceRooms`.
- Access/security: service requires the target conversation to be a real class-group conversation (`Conversation.classId`, type GROUP) and requires the user to be an existing conversation participant. A teacher outside the class group cannot join. A parent/student can join only through their existing class-chat membership.
- Storage discipline: service creates only `ClassVoiceRoom`, `ClassVoiceParticipant`, and `ClassVoiceSignal` rows; it never creates audio file/message attachments. Rooms/signals are short-lived and cleanup marks old rooms EXPIRED and deletes expired signals.
- Room controls: starting a room creates a 15-minute DISAPPEARING room, notifies other class-chat participants in-app, and audit-logs `class_voice.started`. Only the creator or leadership can end the room for everyone, audit-logging `class_voice.ended`.
- Added `scripts/i9-class-voice-service-test.ts` verifying: class chat sync, teacher starts room, parent joins, outside teacher blocked, signal post/poll works, non-creator end blocked, creator end works, cleanup expires old room, no stored voice-note attachment is created by the service, and audit logs exist.
- Verification: `./node_modules/.bin/tsx scripts/i9-class-voice-service-test.ts` ✓, `NODE_OPTIONS=--max-old-space-size=1536 npm run typecheck` ✓, `npm run test:roles` 24/24 ✓.

It validates safe peer IDs, `cvr_...` room keys, allowed signal types (`join`, `leave`, `offer`, `answer`, `ice`, `control`), short TTL constants (15-minute room, 20-minute signals), and payload size.

## 🔁 PART I BATCH 63 — I.7 GATE PASS & DISCIPLINE AUTHORITY COMPLETED (2026-06-22)
- Continued Part I in order and completed I.7 Gate Pass & Discipline Authority.
- Gate pass approvals: added approval metadata to `GatePass` (`approvedById`, `approvedByName`, `approvedAt`, `decisionNote`) through migration `20260622020000_i7_gate_discipline_approvals`. `issueGatePass()` now enforces: Principal/Deputy/Owner/SUPER_ADMIN issue ACTIVE passes directly; HOD/Dean can only propose PENDING passes; receptionist/security cannot issue passes. `decideGatePass()` lets Principal/Deputy/Owner approve/reject pending passes; pending passes cannot be used at the gate. HOD/Dean suspension requests stay PENDING; Principal/Deputy/Owner can approve through existing `approveSuspension()`; ordinary teachers cannot propose suspensions. Behavior board now counts APPROVED incidents only.

- **NEW — Recurring events (RRULE subset):**
  - DB (migration `b25_calendar_recurrence`): CalendarEvent += recurrence (null|WEEKLY|MONTHLY) + recurUntil (YYYY-MM-DD). Nullable → existing events unaffected.
  - Validation: eventFields += recurrence (enum) + recurUntil (isoDate) + refinements (until ≥ date; recurUntil requires a recurrence).
  - Service (calendar.service.ts): **pure expandRecurrence(firstDate, recurrence, recurUntil, from, to)** — WEEKLY = same weekday every 7d; MONTHLY = same day-of-month, months WITHOUT that day are SKIPPED not shifted (31st skips Feb/Apr/Jun/Sep/Nov — verified); bounded by recurUntil + the view range + HARD_CAP=400 safety. getOccurrences now pulls non-recurring overlapping rows AND recurring rows whose window reaches the range, then expands each series into per-date occurrences (id "<seriesId>:<date>" when >1, recurring flag set, shared seriesId; multi-day span preserved via daysBetween). createEvent/updateEvent persist the two fields. buildIcs naturally exports one VEVENT per expanded occurrence.
  - API: existing /api/calendar/events POST already passes the full validated input through — recurrence flows automatically (no route change).
  - UI (calendar-view.tsx): event dialog "Repeats" select (does-not-repeat / every week / every month) + conditional "Repeat until" date; green "🔁 weekly/monthly" badge on agenda occurrences; **delete is series-aware** — remove() strips the ":date" suffix so deleting any occurrence removes the whole stored series.
  - Seed: weekly Monday "Staff Briefing" 07:30 (TEACHER audience, until Dec 15) via nextMondayIso() helper + monthly 5th "Fees due reminder" (PARENT, until Dec 5). Idempotent (calendar block deleteMany+recreate each seed, as A.17 already did).
  - calendar-recurrence-test.ts **14/14 ✓** (SELF-HEALS): WEEKLY/MONTHLY expansion, August 5-Mondays bounding, 31st-skips-short-months, recurUntil cap, seed briefing expands 4× in July w/ shared seriesId, monthly fees once/month, new event round-trips + expands, iCal 4 VEVENTs, series-delete removes all.

## ✅ CARD BALANCE FIX (founder 2026-06-13: "text not well balanced in the cards")
- ROOT CAUSE: shared CardContent had static `p-5 pt-0 sm:p-6 sm:pt-0` — standalone CardContent (no CardHeader) rendered with ZERO top padding on desktop (twMerge keeps sm:pt-0), so text hugged the card top while bottom/sides had full padding.
- FIX in ONE place (`src/components/ui/card.tsx`): CardContent now `p-5 sm:p-6 [&:not(:first-child)]:pt-0` — standalone = full equal padding all sides; after a CardHeader = top padding stripped (header already supplies it). Fixes ALL ~51 card usages at once; no per-page edits.
- BALANCE RULE recorded: start-of-card → text === text → edges/dividers, always. Screenshots 104 + 113 retaken + QA'd (owner tiles + dashboard cards now even).

## ✅ G.31 AUTO-PRINT QUEUE (founder: "INVOICES PRINT THEMSELVES"; built + live-tested, screenshots 99-100 at 1920×1080)
- DB (migration `20260612180000_g31_print_queue`): **PrintJob** (kind INVOICE|RECEIPT|CLASS_BATCH, refId, classId/classLabel frozen, url = PDF endpoint, QUEUED|PRINTED|FAILED, queuedBy). In TENANT_OWNED_MODELS.
- Service `print-queue.service.ts`: queuePrint (DEDUPES identical un-printed jobs), queueInvoiceAfterPayment (balance auto-computed into the title), queueReceiptForPayment, queueClassBatch (all invoices of a structure's class, grouped for distribution), queuedJobs (grouped by classLabel + printedToday), markPrinted (double-print 409).
- **AUTO-QUEUE HOOKS (no tap, founder rule)**: ① reception recordWalkInPayment (CASH + manual M-Pesa) → receipt; ② finance applyPaymentToInvoice → updated invoice; ③ M-Pesa onPaymentPaid → receipt + invoice. All best-effort try/catch — printing must never break the ledger. Bank slips wire into the same hooks when bank integration lands (B.7 deferred line).
- **HOW PRINTING WORKS (no special hardware)**: /print-station page stays open at reception → polls /api/print-queue every 10s → each job's PDF loads in a hidden iframe → contentWindow.print() to the default printer → marks PRINTED. Pause/resume button. PRINTER/PC OFF = jobs simply stay QUEUED (persistence verified: 4 jobs) and flush on reopen — this IS the founder's "if the printer is off it is queued" requirement, no driver/daemon needed. Access: reception.operate OR finance.view.
- print-queue-test.ts (12 ✓): cash auto-queue, payment auto-queue w/ balance in title, dedupe, M-Pesa double-queue, class batch 3×F2E grouped, double-print 409, offline persistence, teacher 403.
- NOTE: full silent printing without ANY dialog needs kiosk mode (chrome --kiosk-printing) on the reception PC — one-line setup note for founder deployments; the queue+iframe flow works regardless.

## ✅ B.12 TEACHER PORTAL: COMPLETE (built + live-tested 2026-06-12, screenshots 65-68)
- DB (migration `b12_teacher_portal`): **Homework** (classId, subjectId, teacherId+teacherName denorm, title, instructions, dueDate YYYY-MM-DD, optional fileUrl/fileName via A.9) + **ClassNote** (same shape, fileUrl REQUIRED). - **Teacher scoping rule (teacher-portal.service `teacherClassIds()`)**: a teacher "owns" a class when classTeacherId=them OR they appear on its timetable (teacherId on TimetableSlot). Fail-closed `["__none__"]` when neither (njoroge verified). Returns `null` for leadership = unrestricted oversight. THIS IS WIDER than B.1 scopeWhere (classTeacher only) — by design: subject teachers must assign homework to classes they teach but don't own.
- Service `src/lib/services/teacher-portal.service.ts`: teacherHome (class cards w/ student counts + subjects-I-teach from timetable + open-homework count + today's lessons Nairobi-day-aware), listHomework/createHomework (due-date-in-past 422)/deleteHomework (ONLY assigning teacher or leadership), listNotes/createNote/deleteNote, classReport (summary tiles + per-student 30d attendance % / absence count / latest-exam avg). ## A.1 line 7 "WebAuthn / passkey": COMPLETE & VERIFIED (server side; ceremony is browser-only)
- Libs: @simplewebauthn/server@10 + /browser@10. RP config in src/lib/core/webauthn.ts (env WEBAUTHN_RP_ID / WEBAUTHN_ORIGIN; dev=localhost).
- NOTE on v10 API: registrationInfo uses credentialID/credentialPublicKey/counter; verifyAuthenticationResponse takes `authenticator:{credentialID,credentialPublicKey,counter,transports}`.
- DB: Credential (publicKey b64url, counter, transports, deviceLabel), WebAuthnChallenge (purpose REGISTER/LOGIN). Migration a1_webauthn_passkeys.
- Service src/lib/services/passkey.service.ts: getRegistrationOptions/verifyRegistration/getLoginOptions/verifyLogin(+2FA via maybeConvertToTotpChallenge)/listPasskeys/deletePasskey.
- API: /api/auth/passkey/{register/options,register/verify,login/options,login/verify,[id] DELETE}.
- UI: login "passkey" step (startAuthentication), settings PasskeysCard (startRegistration).
- TESTABLE ONLY in real browser at localhost (WebAuthn needs secure context + authenticator; NOT in Arena preview iframe).

## A.1 line 8 "2FA via TOTP": COMPLETE & VERIFIED
- Libs: otplib (RFC 6238) + qrcode (inline data-URI). No external account.
- DB: User.totpSecret/totpEnabled/totpVerifiedAt; models RecoveryCode (hashed, single-use), TotpChallenge (short-lived). Migrations a1_totp_2fa, a1_totp_challenge.
- Service `src/lib/services/totp.service.ts`: startTotpSetup/enableTotp(+recovery codes)/disableTotp/checkSecondFactor(TOTP or recovery)/createTotpChallenge/solveTotpChallenge/maybeConvertToTotpChallenge.
- ENFORCEMENT: all 3 login routes (otp/verify, password/login, magic/callback) call maybeConvertToTotpChallenge -> if 2FA on, NO session; returns {twoFactorRequired, challengeToken} (magic redirects /login?challenge=).
- API: /api/auth/2fa/{setup,enable,disable,verify}. Login page has a "twofactor" step (OtpInput). Settings: /settings/security + components/settings/two-factor-card.tsx. Sidebar has "Security".

## A.1 line 12 "Logout everywhere": COMPLETE & VERIFIED
- Service `destroyAllSessionsForUser(userId)` deletes all Session rows for a user, audit-logs `auth.logout_everywhere`.
- API `POST /api/auth/logout-everywhere` (requires session, clears current cookie).
- UI: "Sign out all devices" in `components/shell/user-menu.tsx` (confirm step).
- Verified cross-session: device1 logout-everywhere invalidates device2.

## 0) SANDBOX TIP — running the dev server
The sandbox kills a plain `... &` background job. Use this exact pattern:
```bash
cd /home/user/neyo
(setsid npm run dev </dev/null >/tmp/dev.log 2>&1 &) ; sleep 12
# ...run curl tests...
pkill -9 -f next-server   # to stop
```

## 1) What we have successfully built
- **A.1 line 1 "Phone + OTP login (KE-first)": COMPLETE & VERIFIED (all 8 chunks).**

  - `auth.service.ts`: crypto OTP gen, SHA-256 hash, constant-time compare, rate limit (3/15min), attempt limit (5), session create, AuditLog on login/logout. SMS seam in `notifications/sms.ts` (dev console; swap for Africa's Talking in A.7).
  - API: `POST /api/auth/otp/request`, `POST /api/auth/otp/verify` (sets cookie), `POST /api/auth/logout`, `GET /api/auth/me`.
  - UI: `Input`, `Label`, `OtpInput` (auto-advance/paste/backspace) added to library.
  - Pages: `(auth)/login` (phone→code→success), `(auth)/layout`. `(app)/layout` is now SESSION-GUARDED (redirects to /login) and passes the REAL user to the shell. Logout via `UserMenu`.
  - 4 UX states: `login/loading.tsx`, `(app)/loading.tsx`, global `error.tsx`, success card + toasts.
  - Seed: 8 Kenyan staff across roles (Principal/Bursar/Deputy/Teacher/ClassTeacher/Receptionist/Accountant/Librarian), normalized phones, idempotent.

```bash
npm run dev            # http://localhost:3000
```
